
DECKBLATT_DYNAMIC.gs

/**
 * Dynamically replicates the functionality of the "Werte verschieben" button
 * from multiple VBA macros (Modul 47, 48, 49, 50).
 *
 * This function detects the active "Deckblatt..." sheet, copies a specific range,
 * pastes it as values only, and navigates the user to the next sheet in a
 * predefined workflow.
 *
 * The workflow is:
 * Deckblatt Gesamt -> Deckblatt Food -> Deckblatt Nonfood -> Deckblatt O+G -> Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche
 *
 * This function can be run directly from the Apps Script editor, a custom menu,
 * or a button assigned to it.
 */
function moveWerteAndNavigate() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const activeSheet = ss.getActiveSheet();
  const activeSheetName = activeSheet.getName();

  let sourceRangeA1, destCellA1, nextSheetName, successMessage, nextCellToActivate;

  // Use a switch statement to determine the correct actions based on the active sheet.
  switch (activeSheetName) {
    case "Deckblatt Gesamt":
      sourceRangeA1 = "B5:N57";
      destCellA1 = "Y5";
      nextSheetName = "Deckblatt Food";
      nextCellToActivate = "R1";
      successMessage = "The current Salesforce numbers have been inserted as values into columns Y-AK!\n\nYou will now be forwarded to 'Deckblatt Food'.";
      break;

    case "Deckblatt Food":
      sourceRangeA1 = "M4:O57";
      destCellA1 = "R4";
      nextSheetName = "Deckblatt Nonfood";
      nextCellToActivate = "R1";
      successMessage = "The current Salesforce numbers have been inserted as values into columns R-T!\n\nYou will now be forwarded to 'Deckblatt Nonfood'.";
      break;

    case "Deckblatt Nonfood":
      sourceRangeA1 = "M4:O57";
      destCellA1 = "R4";
      nextSheetName = "Deckblatt O+G";
      nextCellToActivate = "R1";
      successMessage = "The current Salesforce numbers have been inserted as values into columns R-T!\n\nYou will now be forwarded to 'Deckblatt O+G'.";
      break;

    case "Deckblatt O+G":
      sourceRangeA1 = "M4:O57";
      destCellA1 = "R4";
      nextSheetName = "Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche";
      nextCellToActivate = "E1";
      successMessage = "The current Salesforce numbers have been inserted as values into columns R-T!\n\nYou will now be forwarded to 'Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche'.";
      break;

    default:
      // If the script is run on any other sheet, inform the user and stop.
      ui.alert('Action Not Applicable', 'This script can only be run on one of the "Deckblatt..." sheets.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
  }

  // --- 1. Perform the copy/paste operation ---
  const sourceRange = activeSheet.getRange(sourceRangeA1);
  const destinationRange = activeSheet.getRange(destCellA1);

  // Copy the data, pasting only the values (contents).
  sourceRange.copyTo(destinationRange, {
    contentsOnly: true
  });

  // --- 2. Notify the user ---
  ui.alert('Success!', successMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);

  // --- 3. Switch to the next sheet in the workflow ---
  const nextSheet = ss.getSheetByName(nextSheetName);

  if (!nextSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', `The next sheet "${nextSheetName}" could not be found. The process is partially complete.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return; // Stop the script if the next sheet doesn't exist.
  }

  // Activate the next sheet and select the designated cell.
  nextSheet.activate();
  if (nextCellToActivate) {
    nextSheet.getRange(nextCellToActivate).activate();
  }
}

/**
 * 🖨️ EXPORT DECKBLATT (Backend)
 * Fetches data, prepares the base PDFs via Google's native engine, 
 * and sends them to the HTML frontend for pdf-lib processing.
 */

function export_deckblatt_new() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");

  if (!sheetExport) {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. RESOLVE FOLDER ---
  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
    DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId); 
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert("Ordner Fehler", "Der Zielordner konnte nicht gefunden werden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const response = ui.alert("Achtung!", "Hat das betrachtete Jahr 53 Kalenderwochen?", ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO);
  if (response === ui.Button.CLOSED) return; 
  const is53Weeks = (response === ui.Button.YES);

  ss.toast("Bereite Tabellen vor... Bitte warten.", "Schritt 1/3", 10);

  // --- 2. FETCH DASHBOARD DATA (B31:D144) ---
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  // --- 3. CONFIGURATIONS ---
  const configs = [
    {
      liveName: "Deckblatt Gesamt",
      filePrefixes: ["8-Wochen-Statistik_Deckblatt Gesamt_KW", "01_Statistik_ASM_Deckblatt_Gesamt_KW"],
      week53Row: 57, kwCell: "T1", trimLeft: 0, keepCols: 14,
      keys: {
        htl: "Deckblatt Gesamt header left", htc: "Deckblatt Gesamt header center", htr: "Deckblatt Gesamt header right",
        fbl: "Deckblatt Gesamt footer left", fbc: "Deckblatt Gesamt footer center", fbr: "Deckblatt Gesamt footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      liveName: "Deckblatt Food",
      filePrefixes: ["01_Statistik_ASM_Deckblatt_Food_KW"],
      week53Row: 56, kwCell: "L1", trimLeft: 17, keepCols: 4,
      keys: {
        htl: "Deckblatt Food header left", htc: "Deckblatt Food header center", htr: "Deckblatt Food header right",
        fbl: "Deckblatt Food footer left", fbc: "Deckblatt Food footer center", fbr: "Deckblatt Food footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      liveName: "Deckblatt O+G",
      filePrefixes: ["01_Statistik_ASM_Deckblatt_O+G_KW"],
      week53Row: 56, kwCell: "L1", trimLeft: 17, keepCols: 4,
      keys: {
        htl: "Deckblatt O+G header left", htc: "Deckblatt O+G header center", htr: "Deckblatt O+G header right",
        fbl: "Deckblatt O+G footer left", fbc: "Deckblatt O+G footer center", fbr: "Deckblatt O+G footer right"
      }
    }
  ];

  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const payloadJobs = [];
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  // --- 4. PREPARE BASE PDFs ---
  for (const config of configs) {
    const liveSheet = ss.getSheetByName(config.liveName);
    if (!liveSheet) continue;

    const kwValue = liveSheet.getRange(config.kwCell).getValue();

    // Clone & Trim
    const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
    const tempSheet = liveSheet.copyTo(ss);
    tempSheet.setName("Temp_Deckblatt_" + uniqueSuffix);
    const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
    tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

    try {
      const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
      if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

      if (!is53Weeks) tempSheet.hideRows(config.week53Row);
      // --- NEU: Formeln in feste Werte umwandeln ---
      const dataRange = tempSheet.getDataRange();
      dataRange.setValues(dataRange.getValues());
      // --------------------------------------------
      if (config.trimLeft > 0) tempSheet.deleteColumns(1, config.trimLeft);
      const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
      if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

      SpreadsheetApp.flush(); 
      Utilities.sleep(1500); 

      // // Fetch Base PDF (Perfect Scaffold, Centered Grid)
      // const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
      //   `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}` +
      //   `&size=A4&portrait=true&fitw=true&gridlines=false` +
      //   `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED` +
      //   `&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + // <--- THIS CENTERS THE TABLE
      //   `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.709&right_margin=0.709`;

      // Fetch Base PDF (Perfect Scaffold, Centered Grid)
      const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
        `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}` +
        `&size=A4&portrait=true&scale=4&gridlines=false` +
        `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED` +
        `&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + // <--- THIS CENTERS THE TABLE
        `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.709&right_margin=0.709`;

      const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
        headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      });

      if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        const base64Pdf = Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes());
        
        // Create job items for each prefix
        for (const prefix of config.filePrefixes) {
          payloadJobs.push({
            filename: `${prefix}${kwValue}.pdf`,
            base64: base64Pdf,
            layout: {
              htl: getDashboardText(config.keys.htl),
              htc: getDashboardText(config.keys.htc),
              htr: getDashboardText(config.keys.htr),
              fbl: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbl),
              fbc: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbc),
              fbr: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbr)
            }
          });
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    }
  }

  // --- 5. OPEN HTML FRONTEND ---
  if (payloadJobs.length > 0) {
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('pdf-lib');
    htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ jobs: payloadJobs, folderId: folderId, tempSheets: tempSheetIds });
    
    const htmlOutput = htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setWidth(500)
      .setHeight(300)
      .setTitle('PDF Renderer');
      
    ui.showModalDialog(htmlOutput, 'Generiere PDFs...');
  } else {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Keine PDFs konnten vorbereitet werden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  }
}

/**
 * BACKEND CALLBACK: Called by the HTML frontend when rendering is complete.
 * Saves the final Base64 strings to Drive as PDF files and cleans up temp sheets.
 */
function saveFinalPdfsToDrive(finalJobs, folderId, tempSheets) {
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId);
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let savedCount = 0;
  
  try {
    // Save PDFs
    for (const job of finalJobs) {
      const decodedBytes = Utilities.base64Decode(job.finalBase64);
      const blob = Utilities.newBlob(decodedBytes, 'application/pdf', job.filename);
      folder.createFile(blob);
      savedCount++;
    }

    return savedCount; // Returns count to frontend
  } finally {
    // Clean up Temp Sheets even if saving one PDF fails.
    for (const ts of tempSheets || []) {
      const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
      if (sheet && ss.getSheets().length > 1) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
    }

    cleanUpOrphanedTempSheets();
  }
}

Dialog.html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <base target="_top">
  <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/html2pdf.js/0.10.1/html2pdf.bundle.min.js"></script>
  <style>
    body { font-family: Arial, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; background-color: #f4f4f4; }
    .status { margin-bottom: 20px; font-weight: bold; color: #555; }
    .pdf-page { padding: 0.4in; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 8px; text-align: left; page-break-after: always; position: relative; box-sizing: border-box; background: white; overflow: hidden; }
    .pdf-page:last-child { page-break-after: auto; }
    .pdf-header { text-align: center; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 15px; font-size: 11px; }
    .pdf-footer { position: absolute; bottom: 0.3in; left: 0; width: 100%; text-align: center; font-size: 8px; }
    .pdf-signature { position: absolute; bottom: 0.3in; left: 0.4in; font-size: 8px; font-style: italic; }
    table { width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; font-size: 7px; margin-bottom: 20px; table-layout: fixed; }
    th, td { border: 0.5px solid #000; padding: 2px; vertical-align: middle; word-wrap: break-word; overflow-wrap: break-word; }
    th { text-align: center; font-weight: bold; }
    #render-stage { position: absolute; left: -9999px; top: 0; }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <h3>PDF Generator</h3>
  <div id="status" class="status">Initializing...</div>
  <div id="render-stage"></div>

  <script id="data-packet" type="application/json">
    <?!= jsonPayload ?>
  </script>

  <script>
    const statusEl = document.getElementById('status');
    let CONFIG_DATA;

    try {
        CONFIG_DATA = JSON.parse(document.getElementById('data-packet').textContent);
    } catch(e) {
        statusEl.innerText = "Error parsing data packet.";
        console.error(e);
    }

    window.onload = function() {
        if(CONFIG_DATA) renderPdf(CONFIG_DATA);
    };

    function renderPdf(config) {
      statusEl.innerText = "Rendering PDF...";
      
      const container = document.createElement('div');
      const orientation = config.orientation || 'landscape';
      const width = orientation === 'landscape' ? '11.69in' : '8.27in';
      const height = orientation === 'landscape' ? '8.27in' : '11.69in';

      const headerText = config.centerHeader || config.header || "";
      const footerText = config.centerFooter || config.footer || "";
      const headerHTML = `<div class="pdf-header">${parseVba(headerText)}</div>`;
      const footerHTML = `<div class="pdf-footer">${parseVba(footerText)}</div>`;
      const sigHTML = config.signature ? `<div class="pdf-signature">${config.signature}</div>` : '';

      config.sheets.forEach(sheetDef => {
          const rawTable = config.rawTables.find(t => t.sheetName === sheetDef.name);
          if (!rawTable) return;

          const rows = processSheetRows(rawTable, sheetDef);
          
          if (rows.body.length > 0) {
              const page = document.createElement('div');
              page.className = 'pdf-page';
              page.style.width = width;
              page.style.height = height;

              let content = headerHTML;
              content += buildTableHTML(rows.headers, rows.body, rows.colWidths);
              content += footerHTML + sigHTML;
              page.innerHTML = content;
              container.appendChild(page);
          }
      });

      if (container.children.length === 0) {
          statusEl.innerText = "No data to print.";
          setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 2000);
          return;
      }

      document.getElementById('render-stage').appendChild(container);
      
      const opt = {
        margin: 0,
        filename: config.pdfName,
        image: { type: 'jpeg', quality: 0.98 },
        html2canvas: { scale: 2, logging: false, useCORS: true },
        jsPDF: { unit: 'in', format: 'a4', orientation: orientation },
        pagebreak: { mode: ['avoid-all', 'css'] }
      };

      html2pdf().from(container).set(opt).output('datauristring').then(function(pdfBase64) {
          statusEl.innerText = "Uploading...";
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(() => { 
                statusEl.innerText = "Success!"; 
                setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 1500); 
            })
            .withFailureHandler(showError)
            .uploadPDFBlobToDrive(pdfBase64, config.pdfName, config.targetFolderId);
      });
    }

    function processSheetRows(rawTable, sheetDef) {
        const headers = [];
        const body = [];
        const hiddenRows = sheetDef.hideRows || [];
        const area = parsePrintArea(sheetDef.printArea);
        
        const headerRowCount = sheetDef.headerRows || 0;
        let localHeaderCount = 0;

        rawTable.values.forEach((row, index) => {
            const excelRowNum = index + 1; 
            if (excelRowNum < area.startRow || excelRowNum > area.endRow) return; 
            if (hiddenRows.includes(excelRowNum)) return; 

            const meta = sliceMeta({
                data: row,
                bg: rawTable.colors[index],
                fc: rawTable.fontColors[index],
                fw: rawTable.fontWeights[index]
            }, area);

            if (localHeaderCount < headerRowCount) {
                headers.push(meta);
                localHeaderCount++;
            } else {
                body.push(meta);
            }
        });

        while (body.length > 0 && isEmptyMetaRow(body[body.length - 1])) {
            body.pop();
        }

        const colWidths = rawTable.colWidths
            ? rawTable.colWidths.slice(area.startCol - 1, area.endCol)
            : null;

        return { headers, body, colWidths };
    }

    function buildTableHTML(headers, body, colWidths) {
        let colGroupHtml = '<colgroup>';
        if (colWidths) colWidths.forEach(w => colGroupHtml += `<col style="width: ${w};">`);
        colGroupHtml += '</colgroup>';

        let html = `<table>${colGroupHtml}`;
        if (headers.length > 0) {
            html += '<thead>';
            headers.forEach(r => { 
                html += '<tr>' + r.data.map((c, i) => {
                    const bg = (r.bg[i] === '#ffffff' || r.bg[i] === '#fff') ? '#f0f0f0' : r.bg[i];
                    return `<th style="background-color: ${bg}; color: ${r.fc[i]}; font-weight: ${r.fw[i]}">${escapeHtml(c)}</th>`;
                }).join('') + '</tr>'; 
            });
            html += '</thead>';
        }
        html += '<tbody>';
        body.forEach(r => {
            html += '<tr>' + r.data.map((c, i) => {
                const isNum = (c && !isNaN(c.toString().replace(/[.,]/g, '')) && c.toString().length < 15);
                const align = isNum ? 'right' : 'left';
                const bgStyle = (r.bg[i] !== '#ffffff' && r.bg[i] !== '#fff') ? `background-color: ${r.bg[i]};` : '';
                return `<td style="text-align: ${align}; ${bgStyle} color: ${r.fc[i]}; font-weight: ${r.fw[i]}">${escapeHtml(c)}</td>`;
            }).join('') + '</tr>';
        });
        html += '</tbody></table>';
        return html;
    }

    function showError(e) { statusEl.style.color = 'red'; statusEl.innerText = `Error: ${e.message}`; }
    function columnLetterToIndex(letter) {
        return letter.split('').reduce((sum, char) => (sum * 26) + char.charCodeAt(0) - 64, 0);
    }
    function parsePrintArea(printArea) {
        const fallback = { startCol: 1, endCol: 999, startRow: 1, endRow: Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER };
        if (!printArea) return fallback;
        const match = printArea.toUpperCase().match(/^([A-Z]+)?(\d+)?(?::([A-Z]+)?(\d+)?)?$/);
        if (!match) return fallback;
        return {
            startCol: match[1] ? columnLetterToIndex(match[1]) : 1,
            startRow: match[2] ? parseInt(match[2], 10) : 1,
            endCol: match[3] ? columnLetterToIndex(match[3]) : 999,
            endRow: match[4] ? parseInt(match[4], 10) : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER
        };
    }
    function sliceMeta(meta, area) {
        const from = area.startCol - 1;
        const to = Math.min(area.endCol, meta.data.length);
        return {
            data: meta.data.slice(from, to),
            bg: meta.bg.slice(from, to),
            fc: meta.fc.slice(from, to),
            fw: meta.fw.slice(from, to)
        };
    }
    function isEmptyMetaRow(meta) {
        return meta.data.every(value => String(value || '').trim() === '');
    }
    function escapeHtml(value) {
        return String(value == null ? '' : value)
            .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
            .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
            .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
            .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
            .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
    }
    function parseVba(str) { 
        if(!str) return ''; 
        return str.replace(/&""[^"]+""/g, '').replace(/&[\d]+/g, '').replace(/&[BUI]/g, '').replace(/&C/g, '').replace(/Chr\(10\)/g, '<br>').replace(/&P/g, '<span class="pageNumber"></span>').replace(/"/g, '').trim(); 
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>

DialogBatchRenderer.html

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <base target="_top">
  <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/html2pdf.js/0.10.1/html2pdf.bundle.min.js"></script>
  <style>
    body { font-family: Arial, sans-serif; padding: 20px; background-color: #f4f4f4; text-align: center; }
    #progress-container { width: 100%; background-color: #ddd; margin: 20px 0; border-radius: 4px; }
    #progress-bar { width: 0%; height: 24px; background-color: #04AA6D; text-align: center; line-height: 24px; color: white; border-radius: 4px; }
    .log { font-size: 11px; color: #555; height: 150px; overflow-y: scroll; border: 1px solid #ccc; padding: 5px; text-align: left; background: white; }
    .pdf-page { padding: 0.4in; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 8px; text-align: left; background: white; page-break-after: always; box-sizing: border-box; }
    .pdf-header { text-align: center; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 15px; font-size: 11px; }
    .pdf-footer { position: absolute; bottom: 0.3in; left: 0; width: 100%; text-align: center; font-size: 8px; }
    table { width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; font-size: 7px; margin-bottom: 20px; table-layout: fixed; }
    th, td { border: 0.5px solid #000; padding: 2px; vertical-align: middle; word-wrap: break-word; }
    th { text-align: center; font-weight: bold; }
    #render-stage { position: absolute; left: -9999px; }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <h3>Batch PDF Generator</h3>
  <div id="status">Initializing...</div>
  <div id="progress-container"><div id="progress-bar">0%</div></div>
  <div id="log" class="log"></div>
  <div id="render-stage"></div>

  <script id="batch-data" type="application/json">
    <?!= jsonPayload ?>
  </script>

  <script>
    let BATCH_DATA;
    try {
        BATCH_DATA = JSON.parse(document.getElementById('batch-data').textContent);
    } catch(e) {
        document.getElementById('status').innerText = "Critical Error: Data Injection Failed.";
    }
    
    let currentIndex = 0;
    const logEl = document.getElementById('log');
    const statusEl = document.getElementById('status');
    const barEl = document.getElementById('progress-bar');

    window.onload = function() {
        if(BATCH_DATA) startProcessing();
    };

    function startProcessing() {
        if (!BATCH_DATA.items || BATCH_DATA.items.length === 0) {
            log("No items found to process.");
            setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 3000);
            return;
        }
        log(`Found ${BATCH_DATA.items.length} files. Starting...`);
        processNext();
    }

    function processNext() {
        if (currentIndex >= BATCH_DATA.items.length) {
            statusEl.innerText = "Completed!";
            barEl.style.width = "100%";
            barEl.innerText = "100%";
            log("All files created.");
            setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 3000);
            return;
        }

        const item = BATCH_DATA.items[currentIndex];
        const percent = Math.round((currentIndex / BATCH_DATA.items.length) * 100) + "%";
        barEl.style.width = percent;
        barEl.innerText = percent;
        statusEl.innerText = `Processing: ${item}`;
        
        generatePdfForItem(item);
    }

    function generatePdfForItem(itemVal) {
        const container = document.createElement('div');
        
        // Deckblatts are Portrait, others Landscape
        const orientation = (BATCH_DATA.batchType === "DECKBLATT_BATCH") ? 'portrait' : 'landscape';
        const width = orientation === 'landscape' ? '11.69in' : '8.27in';
        const height = orientation === 'landscape' ? '8.27in' : '11.69in';
        
        let hasData = false;

        BATCH_DATA.rawData.forEach(rawTable => {
            const sheetDef = (BATCH_DATA.sheetConfigs && BATCH_DATA.sheetConfigs[rawTable.sheetName]) || {};
            const area = parsePrintArea(sheetDef.printArea);
            const colWidths = rawTable.colWidths
                ? rawTable.colWidths.slice(area.startCol - 1, Math.min(area.endCol, rawTable.colWidths.length))
                : null;

            // --- BRANCHING LOGIC ---
            
            // Branch A: Deckblatt (Whole Sheet Mode)
            if (BATCH_DATA.batchType === "DECKBLATT_BATCH") {
                // If this rawTable is NOT the current itemVal (Sheet Name), skip it
                if (rawTable.sheetName !== itemVal) return;
                
                const hiddenRows = sheetDef.hideRows || [];
                const filteredBody = [];
                rawTable.values.forEach((row, idx) => {
                    const excelRowNum = idx + 1;
                    if (excelRowNum < area.startRow || excelRowNum > area.endRow) return;
                    if (hiddenRows.includes(excelRowNum)) return;

                    const meta = sliceMeta({
                        data: row, bg: rawTable.colors[idx], fc: rawTable.fontColors[idx], fw: rawTable.fontWeights[idx]
                    }, area);
                    filteredBody.push(meta);
                });

                while (filteredBody.length > 0 && isEmptyMetaRow(filteredBody[filteredBody.length - 1])) {
                    filteredBody.pop();
                }
                
                if (filteredBody.length > 0) {
                    hasData = true;
                    const page = buildPage(width, height, rawTable.sheetName, "", filteredBody, colWidths);
                    container.appendChild(page);
                }
            } 
            // Branch B: Standard Reports (Supplier Filter Mode)
            else {
                let filterColIndex = -1;
                if (BATCH_DATA.batchType === "GL_EK_INT_QUAL") filterColIndex = 3; 
                else if (BATCH_DATA.batchType === "GL_EK_INT_SORT") filterColIndex = 2; 
                else if (BATCH_DATA.batchType === "GL_EK_INT_SONST") filterColIndex = 3;
                else if (BATCH_DATA.batchType === "EKL_DE") filterColIndex = 2; 

                if (filterColIndex === -1) return;

                const filteredBody = [];
                const headers = [];
                const headerCount = Number.isInteger(sheetDef.headerRows) ? sheetDef.headerRows : 2;
                let localHeaderCount = 0;
                
                rawTable.values.forEach((row, idx) => {
                    const excelRowNum = idx + 1;
                    if (excelRowNum < area.startRow || excelRowNum > area.endRow) return;

                    const meta = sliceMeta({
                        data: row, bg: rawTable.colors[idx], fc: rawTable.fontColors[idx], fw: rawTable.fontWeights[idx]
                    }, area);

                    if (localHeaderCount < headerCount) {
                        headers.push(meta);
                        localHeaderCount++;
                    }
                    else if (row[filterColIndex] == itemVal) filteredBody.push(meta);
                });

                while (filteredBody.length > 0 && isEmptyMetaRow(filteredBody[filteredBody.length - 1])) {
                    filteredBody.pop();
                }

                if (filteredBody.length > 0) {
                    hasData = true;
                    // Note: In Batch, we construct a generic header/footer
                    const page = buildPage(width, height, rawTable.sheetName, itemVal, filteredBody, colWidths, headers);
                    container.appendChild(page);
                }
            }
        });

        if (!hasData) {
            log(`Skipping ${itemVal}: No data.`);
            currentIndex++;
            processNext();
            return;
        }

        document.getElementById('render-stage').innerHTML = ''; 
        document.getElementById('render-stage').appendChild(container);

        // Filename Logic
        let filename = "";
        if (BATCH_DATA.batchType === "DECKBLATT_BATCH") {
            // Look for KW in the table (usually cell T1/L1, which are in the first few rows we skipped or in raw values)
            // Simplified:
            filename = `01_Statistik_ASM_${itemVal.replace(/ /g, '_')}.pdf`;
        } else {
            filename = `Statistik_${BATCH_DATA.batchType}_${itemVal}.pdf`;
        }

        const opt = {
            margin: 0, filename: filename,
            image: { type: 'jpeg', quality: 0.98 },
            html2canvas: { scale: 1.5, logging: false, useCORS: true }, 
            jsPDF: { unit: 'in', format: 'a4', orientation: orientation }
        };

        html2pdf().from(container).set(opt).output('datauristring').then(function(pdfBase64) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(() => {
                    log(`Saved: ${filename}`);
                    currentIndex++;
                    processNext();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(logError)
                .uploadPDFBlobToDrive(pdfBase64, filename, BATCH_DATA.targetFolderId);
        });
    }

    function buildPage(w, h, title, subtitle, body, widths, headers=[]) {
        const page = document.createElement('div');
        page.className = 'pdf-page';
        page.style.width = w;
        page.style.height = h;
        
        // Simplified Headers for Batch
        const headTxt = parseVba(`&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&14${title}`);
        const footTxt = parseVba(`&C&""Lidl Font Pro""&9${subtitle}`);

        page.innerHTML = `<div class="pdf-header">${headTxt}</div>` + 
                         buildTableHTML(headers, body, widths) + 
                         `<div class="pdf-footer">${footTxt}</div>`;
        return page;
    }

    function buildTableHTML(headers, body, colWidths) {
        let h = '<table><colgroup>';
        if (colWidths) colWidths.forEach(w => h += `<col style="width: ${w};">`);
        h += '</colgroup><thead>';
        headers.forEach(r => { 
            h += '<tr>' + r.data.map((c,i) => {
                const bg = (r.bg[i] === '#ffffff' || r.bg[i] === '#fff') ? '#f0f0f0' : r.bg[i];
                return `<th style="background:${bg}; color: ${r.fc[i]}; font-weight: ${r.fw[i]}">${escapeHtml(c)}</th>`;
            }).join('') + '</tr>'; 
        });
        h += '</thead><tbody>';
        body.forEach(r => { 
            h += '<tr>' + r.data.map((c,i) => {
                const bg = (r.bg[i] !== '#ffffff' && r.bg[i] !== '#fff') ? r.bg[i] : '';
                const text = String(c == null ? '' : c);
                const align = (!isNaN(text.replace(/[.,]/g, '')) && text.length < 15) ? 'right' : 'left';
                return `<td style="background:${bg}; color: ${r.fc[i]}; font-weight: ${r.fw[i]}; text-align:${align}">${escapeHtml(c)}</td>`;
            }).join('') + '</tr>'; 
        });
        h += '</tbody></table>';
        return h;
    }
    function columnLetterToIndex(letter) {
        return letter.split('').reduce((sum, char) => (sum * 26) + char.charCodeAt(0) - 64, 0);
    }
    function parsePrintArea(printArea) {
        const fallback = { startCol: 1, endCol: 999, startRow: 1, endRow: Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER };
        if (!printArea) return fallback;
        const match = printArea.toUpperCase().match(/^([A-Z]+)?(\d+)?(?::([A-Z]+)?(\d+)?)?$/);
        if (!match) return fallback;
        return {
            startCol: match[1] ? columnLetterToIndex(match[1]) : 1,
            startRow: match[2] ? parseInt(match[2], 10) : 1,
            endCol: match[3] ? columnLetterToIndex(match[3]) : 999,
            endRow: match[4] ? parseInt(match[4], 10) : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER
        };
    }
    function sliceMeta(meta, area) {
        const from = area.startCol - 1;
        const to = Math.min(area.endCol, meta.data.length);
        return {
            data: meta.data.slice(from, to),
            bg: meta.bg.slice(from, to),
            fc: meta.fc.slice(from, to),
            fw: meta.fw.slice(from, to)
        };
    }
    function isEmptyMetaRow(meta) {
        return meta.data.every(value => String(value || '').trim() === '');
    }
    function escapeHtml(value) {
        return String(value == null ? '' : value)
            .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
            .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
            .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
            .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
            .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
    }
    function parseVba(str) { return str.replace(/&""[^"]+""/g, '').replace(/&[\d]+/g, '').replace(/&[BUI]/g, '').replace(/&C/g, '').replace(/Chr\(10\)/g, '<br>').replace(/"/g, ''); }
    function log(msg) { const d = document.createElement('div'); d.innerText = msg; logEl.appendChild(d); logEl.scrollTop = logEl.scrollHeight; }
    function logError(e) { log("Error: " + e.message); }
  </script>
</body>
</html>

/**
 * 🖨️ EXPORT FOOD GESAMT (Merged PDF)
 * Combines 5 Food sheets into a single, merged LANDSCAPE PDF.
 * Reuses the 'multi-page-support-pdf-lib' frontend engine.
 */

function export_food_gesamt() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");

  if (!sheetExport) {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. RESOLVE FOLDER ---
  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
    DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId); 
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert("Ordner Fehler", "Der Zielordner konnte nicht gefunden werden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // Get KW explicitly from Food Qualitätsfälle cell S5 as per VBA (Modul14)
  const kwSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Qualitätsfälle");
  const kwValue = kwSheet ? kwSheet.getRange("N5").getValue() : "XX";

  ss.toast("Prüfe 5 Tabellenblätter... Bitte warten.", "Schritt 1/3", 15);

  // --- 2. FETCH DASHBOARD DATA (B31:D144) ---
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  // --- 3. CONFIGURATIONS FOR THE 5 SHEETS ---
  const configs = [
    {
      name: "Food Sortimentswünsche", dataRowStart: 6, keepCols: 17, // Print Area A:Q
      keys: {
        htl: "Food Sortimentswünsche header left", htc: "Food Sortimentswünsche header center", htr: "Food Sortimentswünsche header right",
        fbl: "Food Sortimentswünsche footer left", fbc: "Food Sortimentswünsche footer center", fbr: "Food Sortimentswünsche footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung", dataRowStart: 6, keepCols: 17, // Print Area A:Q
      keys: {
        htl: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung header left", htc: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung header center", htr: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung header right",
        fbl: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer left", fbc: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer center", fbr: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche", dataRowStart: 8, keepCols: 11, // Print Area A:K
      keys: {
        htl: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header left", htc: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header center", htr: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header right",
        fbl: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer left", fbc: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer center", fbr: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen", dataRowStart: 7, keepCols: 15, // Print Area A:O
      keys: {
        htl: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header left", htc: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header center", htr: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header right",
        fbl: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer left", fbc: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer center", fbr: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "Food Qualitätsfälle", dataRowStart: 6, keepCols: 22, // Print Area A:V
      keys: {
        htl: "Food Qualitätsfälle header left", htc: "Food Qualitätsfälle header center", htr: "Food Qualitätsfälle header right",
        fbl: "Food Qualitätsfälle footer left", fbc: "Food Qualitätsfälle footer center", fbr: "Food Qualitätsfälle footer right"
      }
    }
  ];

  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const pdfParts = [];
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  // --- 4. PREPARE BASE PDFs (Landscape, Skips Empty) ---
  for (const config of configs) {
    const liveSheet = ss.getSheetByName(config.name);
    if (!liveSheet) continue;

    // Skip if no data (matching VBA check logic)
    const lastRow = liveSheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < config.dataRowStart) {
      console.log(`Skipping ${config.name} - No Data`);
      continue; 
    }

    // Clone & Trim
    const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
    const tempSheet = liveSheet.copyTo(ss);
    tempSheet.setName("Temp_Gesamt_" + uniqueSuffix);
    const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
    tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

    try {
      const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
      if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

      const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
      if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

      SpreadsheetApp.flush(); 
      Utilities.sleep(1000); 

      // // Fetch Base PDF (Forced LANDSCAPE via portrait=false)
      // const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
      //   `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}` +
      //   `&size=A4&portrait=false&fitw=true&gridlines=false` +
      //   `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED` +
      //   `&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
      //   `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

      // Fetch Base PDF (Forced LANDSCAPE via portrait=false)
      const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
        `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}` +
        `&size=A4&portrait=false&scale=2&gridlines=false` +
        `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED` +
        `&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
        `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

      const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
        headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      });

      if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        const base64Pdf = Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes());
        
        pdfParts.push({
          sheetName: config.name,
          base64: base64Pdf,
          layout: {
            htl: getDashboardText(config.keys.htl),
            htc: getDashboardText(config.keys.htc),
            htr: getDashboardText(config.keys.htr),
            fbl: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbl),
            fbc: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbc),
            fbr: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbr)
          }
        });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    }
  }

  // --- 5. OPEN HTML FRONTEND ---
  if (pdfParts.length > 0) {
    const finalFilename = `8-Wochen-Statistik_Food_KW${kwValue}.pdf`;
    
    // REUSING the existing HTML engine!
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('multi-page-support-pdf-lib');
    htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
      parts: pdfParts, 
      folderId: folderId, 
      filename: finalFilename,
      tempSheets: tempSheetIds 
    });
    
    const htmlOutput = htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setWidth(500)
      .setHeight(300)
      .setTitle('Generiere Food Gesamt Report...');
      
    ui.showModalDialog(htmlOutput, 'Erstelle Food Gesamt Report...');
  } else {
    ui.alert("Hinweis", "Keine der ausgewählten Tabellen enthält Daten.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    for (const ts of tempSheetIds) {
      const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
      if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
    }
  }
}


ExportAsPDFAndExcelGesamt_html.html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/pdf-lib@1.17.1/dist/pdf-lib.min.js"></script>
    <style>
      body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
      .spinner { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #e67e22; border-radius: 50%; width: 30px; height: 30px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 10px auto; }
      @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
      .log { height: 250px; overflow-y: auto; background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px solid #ccc; margin-top: 15px; padding: 10px; text-align: left; font-size: 12px; font-family: monospace; }
      .log-item { margin-bottom: 4px; border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; }
      .ok-msg { color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; }
      .skip-msg { color: #f39c12; font-weight: bold; }
      .error-msg { color: #e74c3c; font-weight: bold; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h3>Generating Food Gesamt Report</h3>
    <div id="loader" class="spinner"></div>
    <div id="status">Starting threads...</div>
    <div id="log" class="log"></div>

    <script>
      const { PDFDocument } = PDFLib;

      window.onload = function() { startProcess(); };

      async function startProcess() {
        log("Launching 5 parallel threads for PDF parts...");
        
        // Fire 5 requests simultaneously
        const promises = [
          getPart(1),
          getPart(2),
          getPart(3),
          getPart(4),
          getPart(5)
        ];

        try {
          // Wait for all 5 to complete
          const results = await Promise.all(promises);
          log("All parts received. Merging...");
          
          await mergeAndSave(results);

        } catch (e) {
          log(`<span class="error-msg">FATAL ERROR: ${e.message}</span>`);
          document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none";
        }
      }

      function getPart(num) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler((res) => {
              if (res.blobData) {
                log(`Part ${num} generated.`);
              } else {
                log(`<span class="skip-msg">Part ${num} skipped (No Data).</span>`);
              }
              resolve(res);
            })
            .withFailureHandler((err) => {
              log(`<span class="error-msg">Error Part ${num}: ${err.message}</span>`);
              reject(err);
            })
            .getFoodGesamtPart(num);
        });
      }

      async function mergeAndSave(results) {
        // Sort results by part number just in case
        results.sort((a, b) => a.partNumber - b.partNumber);

        const mergedPdf = await PDFDocument.create();
        let hasContent = false;
        let filename = "Food_Gesamt.pdf";
        let folderId = "";

        for (const res of results) {
          if (res.blobData) {
            hasContent = true;
            filename = res.filename; // Use filename from server
            folderId = res.folderId;
            
            const pdfSrc = await PDFDocument.load(res.blobData);
            const copiedPages = await mergedPdf.copyPages(pdfSrc, pdfSrc.getPageIndices());
            copiedPages.forEach((page) => mergedPdf.addPage(page));
          }
        }

        if (!hasContent) {
          log("No data found in any sheet. Nothing to save.");
          finish();
          return;
        }

        updateStatus("Saving final PDF...");
        const mergedBytes = await mergedPdf.saveAsBase64();

        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(() => {
            log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Success! File saved: ${filename}</span>`);
            finish();
          })
          .saveFoodGesamtPdf(mergedBytes, filename, folderId);
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { const div = document.getElementById("log"); div.innerHTML += `<div class="log-item">${msg}</div>`; div.scrollTop = div.scrollHeight; }
      function finish() { document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none"; updateStatus("Complete!"); }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

/**
 * SERVER SIDE: ExportFoodGesamtEKLDE
 * Generates batch Food Gesamt reports filtered by EKL DE (Col C).
 * - "Sonstiges" includes blanks alongside the specific EKL.
 * - "Allgemeine" is always included.
 * - Uses Client-Side pdf-lib rendering for perfect layout & merging.
 */

function openFoodGesamtEKLDEDialog() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");
  
  if (!sheetExport) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // Fetch Dashboard Texts once
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
  } catch (e) {
    folderId = folderUrl; 
  }

  // Get KW explicitly from Food Qualitätsfälle cell S5 as per VBA
  const qualiSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Food Qualitätsfälle");
  const kwValue = qualiSheet ? qualiSheet.getRange("S5").getValue() : "XX";

  // Package layout data for all 5 sheets
  const layouts = {
    food: {
      htl: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche header left"), htc: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche header center"), htr: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche header right"),
      fbl: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche footer left"), fbc: "Statistik KW " + kwValue + "\n- [PAGE] -", fbr: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche footer right")
    },
    aenderung: {
      htl: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung header left"), htc: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung header center"), htr: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung header right"),
      fbl: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer left"), fbc: "Statistik KW " + kwValue + "\n- [PAGE] -", fbr: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer right")
    },
    allgemeine: {
      htl: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header left"), htc: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header center"), htr: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header right"),
      fbl: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer left"), fbc: "Statistik KW " + kwValue + "\n- [PAGE] -", fbr: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer right")
    },
    sonstiges: {
      htl: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header left"), htc: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header center"), htr: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header right"),
      fbl: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer left"), fbc: "Statistik KW " + kwValue + "\n- [PAGE] -", fbr: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer right")
    },
    quali: {
      htl: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle header left"), htc: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle header center"), htr: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle header right"),
      fbl: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle footer left"), fbc: "Statistik KW " + kwValue + "\n- [PAGE] -", fbr: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle footer right")
    }
  };

  const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('ExportFoodGesamtEKLDE_HTML');
  htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
    layouts: layouts, 
    folderId: folderId,
    kwValue: kwValue
  });
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(
    htmlTemplate.evaluate().setWidth(600).setHeight(500), 
    'Generating Food Gesamt Reports (EKL DE)...'
  );
}

/**
 * Gets unique EKL DE recipients from Mapping Col K (Index 11)
 */
function getEklRecipients() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Mapping");
  if (!sheet) throw new Error("Sheet 'Mapping' nicht gefunden.");
  
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return [];
  
  const data = sheet.getRange(2, 11, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues().flat();
  return [...new Set(data)].filter(String).sort();
}

/**
 * Server-side generation of Base PDFs for a specific EKL DE recipient
 */
function getPdfDataForEkl(recipient) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  // Configurations for all 5 sheets (EKL DE is usually Col C -> Index 3)
  const configs = [
    { id: "food", name: "Food Sortimentswünsche", filterCol: 3, includeBlanks: false, headerRows: 5, keepCols: 18 },
    { id: "aenderung", name: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung", filterCol: 3, includeBlanks: false, headerRows: 5, keepCols: 18 },
    { id: "allgemeine", name: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche", filterCol: null, includeBlanks: false, headerRows: 7, keepCols: 11 },
    { id: "sonstiges", name: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen", filterCol: 3, includeBlanks: true, headerRows: 6, keepCols: 15 }, // Includes blanks per VBA Modul12
    { id: "quali", name: "Food Qualitätsfälle", filterCol: 3, includeBlanks: false, headerRows: 5, keepCols: 22 }
  ];

  const parts = [];

  for (const config of configs) {
    const liveSheet = ss.getSheetByName(config.name);
    if (!liveSheet) continue;

    const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
    const tempSheet = liveSheet.copyTo(ss);
    tempSheet.setName(`Temp_${config.id}_${uniqueSuffix}`);
    const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
    tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

    try {
      const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
      if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

      const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
      if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

      // Filtering Logic
      let hasData = true;
      const lastRow = tempSheet.getLastRow();

      if (config.filterCol && lastRow > config.headerRows) {
        const values = tempSheet.getRange(config.headerRows + 1, config.filterCol, lastRow - config.headerRows, 1).getValues().flat();
        const deleteRequests = [];
        let startDelete = -1;
        let dataCount = 0;

        for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
          const cellVal = String(values[i]).trim();
          let keepRow = false;

          // Rule: Keep if exact match, OR keep if blank (if includeBlanks is true)
          if (cellVal === recipient) {
            keepRow = true;
          } else if (config.includeBlanks && cellVal === "") {
            keepRow = true;
          }

          if (!keepRow) {
            if (startDelete === -1) startDelete = i;
          } else {
            if (startDelete !== -1) {
              deleteRequests.push({ deleteDimension: { range: { sheetId: sheetId, dimension: "ROWS", startIndex: config.headerRows + startDelete, endIndex: config.headerRows + i } } });
              startDelete = -1;
            }
            dataCount++;
          }
        }
        
        if (startDelete !== -1) {
          deleteRequests.push({ deleteDimension: { range: { sheetId: sheetId, dimension: "ROWS", startIndex: config.headerRows + startDelete, endIndex: config.headerRows + values.length } } });
        }
        if (deleteRequests.length > 0) {
          deleteRequests.reverse();
          Sheets.Spreadsheets.batchUpdate({ requests: deleteRequests }, ss.getId());
        }
        
        if (dataCount === 0) hasData = false;
      } else if (lastRow <= config.headerRows) {
        hasData = false;
      }

      SpreadsheetApp.flush();

      // Only fetch the URL if there's actually data to print
      // if (hasData) {
      //   const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
      //     `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}&size=A4&portrait=false&fitw=true&gridlines=false` +
      //     `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
      //     `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

      if (hasData) {
        const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
          `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}&size=A4&portrait=false&scale=2&gridlines=false` +
          `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
          `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

        const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token }, muteHttpExceptions: true });
        
        if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
          parts.push({
            id: config.id,
            base64: Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes())
          });
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    }
  }

  return { parts: parts, tempSheets: tempSheetIds };
}

function saveEklPdfToDrive_batch(base64Data, filename, folderId, tempSheets) {
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId);
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  if (base64Data) {
    const decodedBytes = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(decodedBytes, 'application/pdf', filename);
    folder.createFile(blob);
  }

  // Cleanup temp sheets
  for (const ts of tempSheets) {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
    if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
  }
  return true;
}

    <script>
      const CONCURRENCY = 5; 
      const { PDFDocument } = PDFLib;

      window.onload = function() { startBatchProcess(); };

      async function startBatchProcess() {
        log("Fetching EKL recipient list...");
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(runQueue).withFailureHandler(handleError).getEklRecipients();
      }

      function runQueue(recipients) {
        log(`Found ${recipients.length} EKLs. Starting queue...`);
        let index = 0; let activeWorkers = 0; let completed = 0;
        const total = recipients.length;

        if(total === 0) { finish(); return; }

        const next = () => {
          if (index >= total && activeWorkers === 0) { finish(); return; }
          while (activeWorkers < CONCURRENCY && index < total) {
            const recipient = recipients[index++];
            activeWorkers++;
            updateStatus(`Processing: ${activeWorkers} active | ${total - index} pending`);

              activeWorkers--; completed++; updateProgress(completed, total); next();
            });
          }
        };
        next();
      }

      function processRecipient(recipient) {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(async (res) => {

                resolve(); return;
              }

                const mergedPdf = await PDFDocument.create();

                  if (!base64) return;
                  const pdfSrc = await PDFDocument.load(base64);
                  const copiedPages = await mergedPdf.copyPages(pdfSrc, pdfSrc.getPageIndices());
                  copiedPages.forEach((page) => mergedPdf.addPage(page));
                };

                // Merge Order: Sortimentswünsche -> Änderung -> Allgemeine -> Sonstiges -> Quali
                await loadAndCopy(res.part1);
                await loadAndCopy(res.part2);
                await loadAndCopy(res.part3);
                await loadAndCopy(res.part4);
                await loadAndCopy(res.part5);

                const mergedBytes = await mergedPdf.saveAsBase64();
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(() => {
                  log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Saved: ${recipient}</span>`);
                  resolve();
                }).saveMergedPdfToDrive(mergedBytes, res.filename, res.folderId);

              } catch(e) {
                log(`<span class="error-msg">❌ Merge Error ${recipient}: ${e.message}</span>`);
                resolve();
              }
            })
            .withFailureHandler((err) => {
              log(`<span class="error-msg">❌ Server Error ${recipient}: ${err.message}</span>`);
              resolve();
            })
            .getPdfDataForEkl(recipient);
        });
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { const div = document.getElementById("log"); div.innerHTML += `<div class="log-item">${msg}</div>`; div.scrollTop = div.scrollHeight; }
      function updateProgress(current, total) { document.getElementById("bar").style.width = Math.round((current / total) * 100) + "%"; }
      function handleError(e) { log(`FATAL ERROR: ${e.message}`); }
      function finish() { document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none"; updateStatus("Batch Processing Complete!"); }
    </script>
  </body>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/pdf-lib/dist/pdf-lib.min.js"></script>
    <style>
      body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
      .spinner { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #3498db; border-radius: 50%; width: 30px; height: 30px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 10px auto; }
      @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
      .progress-container { width: 100%; background-color: #ddd; margin-top: 20px; border-radius: 5px; }
      .progress-bar { width: 0%; height: 20px; background-color: #3498db; border-radius: 5px; transition: width 0.3s; }
      .log { height: 250px; overflow-y: auto; background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px solid #ccc; margin-top: 15px; padding: 10px; text-align: left; font-size: 12px; font-family: monospace; }
      .log-item { margin-bottom: 4px; border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; padding-bottom: 2px;}
      .ok-msg { color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; }
      .skip-msg { color: #f39c12; font-weight: bold; }
      .error-msg { color: #e74c3c; font-weight: bold; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h3>Generating Food Gesamt Reports (EKL DE)</h3>
    <div id="loader" class="spinner"></div>
    <div id="status">Initializing...</div>
    <div class="progress-container"><div id="bar" class="progress-bar"></div></div>
    <div id="log" class="log"></div>

    <script>
      const payloadData = <?!= payload ?>;
      const { PDFDocument, StandardFonts, rgb } = PDFLib;
      const CONCURRENCY = 3; 

      window.onload = function() { startBatchProcess(); };

      async function startBatchProcess() {
        log("Fetching EKL recipients from Mapping tab...");
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(runQueue)
          .withFailureHandler(handleError)
          .getEklRecipients();
      }

      function sanitizeText(text) {
        if (!text) return "";
        return text.toString().normalize('NFC'); 
      }

      function base64ToUint8(base64) {
        const binary_string = window.atob(base64);
        const len = binary_string.length;
        const bytes = new Uint8Array(len);
        for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) { bytes[i] = binary_string.charCodeAt(i); }
        return bytes;
      }

      function uint8ToBase64(uint8) {
        let binary = '';
        for (let i = 0; i < uint8.byteLength; i++) { binary += String.fromCharCode(uint8[i]); }
        return window.btoa(binary);
      }

      async function runQueue(recipients) {
        log(`Found ${recipients.length} recipients. Starting processing...`);
        let index = 0;
        let activeWorkers = 0;
        let completed = 0;
        const total = recipients.length;

        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          const next = () => {
            if (index >= total && activeWorkers === 0) {
              finish();
              resolve();
              return;
            }

            while (activeWorkers < CONCURRENCY && index < total) {
              const recipient = recipients[index++];
              activeWorkers++;
              updateStatus(`Queue: ${activeWorkers} active | ${total - index} pending`);

              processSingleRecipient(recipient)
                .then((res) => {
                  if (res === "SKIPPED") {
                    log(`<span class="skip-msg">⚠️ Skipped: ${recipient} (No Parts generated)</span>`);
                  } else {
                    log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Saved: ${recipient}</span>`);
                  }
                })
                .catch((err) => log(`<span class="error-msg">❌ Error ${recipient}: ${err.message}</span>`))
                .finally(() => {
                  activeWorkers--;
                  completed++;
                  updateProgress(completed, total);
                  next();
                });
            }
          };
          next();
        });
      }

      function processSingleRecipient(recipient) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(async (response) => {
              try {
                if (!response.parts || response.parts.length === 0) {
                  // Will gracefully skip ONLY if the backend returned absolutely zero parts
                  resolve("SKIPPED");
                  return;
                }

                const masterPdf = await PDFDocument.create();
                let globalPageCounter = 1;

                for (const part of response.parts) {
                  const partPdfBytes = base64ToUint8(part.base64);
                  const partPdf = await PDFDocument.load(partPdfBytes);
                  
                  // Embed fonts directly into the part
                  const fontRegular = await partPdf.embedFont(StandardFonts.Helvetica);
                  const fontBold = await partPdf.embedFont(StandardFonts.HelveticaBold);

                  const pages = partPdf.getPages();
                  const layoutConfig = payloadData.layouts[part.id]; // Map layout via ID

                  for (let i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {
                    const page = pages[i];
                    const { width, height } = page.getSize(); 
                    const pageNumStr = globalPageCounter.toString();

                    const headerSize = 7.5; 
                    const centerSize = 12;  
                    const footerSize = 8;   
                    const xMargin = 30;             
                    const yTop = height - 20;     
                    const yBottom = 25;           

                    const regex = /\[PAGEA?\]|\[PAGE A\]/gi;
                    const htl = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.htl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const htc = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.htc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const htr = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.htr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const fbl = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.fbl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const fbc = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.fbc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const fbr = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.fbr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);

                    const drawTextMultiline = (text, align, isHeader, startY, fontSize, textFont) => {
                      if (!text) return;
                      const lines = text.split('\n');
                      const lineHeight = fontSize * 1.25;
                      let currentY = isHeader ? startY : startY + ((lines.length - 1) * lineHeight);

                      lines.forEach(line => {
                        let xPos = xMargin; 
                        if (align === 'center') {
                          xPos = (width - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize)) / 2;
                        } else if (align === 'right') {
                          xPos = width - xMargin - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize);
                        }
                        page.drawText(line, { x: xPos, y: currentY, size: fontSize, font: textFont, color: rgb(0,0,0) });
                        currentY -= lineHeight; 
                      });
                    };

                    drawTextMultiline(htl, 'left',   true, yTop, headerSize, fontBold);
                    drawTextMultiline(htc, 'center', true, yTop - 15, centerSize, fontBold);
                    drawTextMultiline(htr, 'right',  true, yTop - 5, headerSize, fontBold);
                    drawTextMultiline(fbl, 'left',   false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                    drawTextMultiline(fbc, 'center', false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                    drawTextMultiline(fbr, 'right',  false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);

                    globalPageCounter++;
                  }

                  const copiedPages = await masterPdf.copyPages(partPdf, partPdf.getPageIndices());
                  copiedPages.forEach((p) => masterPdf.addPage(p));
                }

                const finalPdfBytes = await masterPdf.save();
                const finalBase64 = uint8ToBase64(finalPdfBytes);
                // Naming convention exactly matching VBA Modul12
                const finalFilename = `Statistik_ASM Food KW ${payloadData.kwValue}_${recipient}.pdf`;

                google.script.run
                  .withSuccessHandler(resolve)
                  .withFailureHandler(reject)
                  .saveEklPdfToDrive_batch(finalBase64, finalFilename, payloadData.folderId, response.tempSheets);

              } catch (err) {
                reject(err);
              }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(reject)
            .getPdfDataForEkl(recipient);
        });
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { 
        const div = document.getElementById("log"); 
        div.innerHTML += `<div class="log-item">${msg}</div>`; 
        div.scrollTop = div.scrollHeight; 
      }
      function updateProgress(current, total) { 
        document.getElementById("bar").style.width = Math.round((current / total) * 100) + "%"; 
      }
      function handleError(e) { log(`FATAL ERROR: ${e.message}`); }
      function finish() { 
        document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none"; 
        updateStatus("Batch Processing Complete! Cleaning up..."); 
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(() => { setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 2000); })
          .cleanUpOrphanedTempSheets();
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

ExportFoodQualitätsfälleGLEKINT.gs
