/**
 * SERVER SIDE: ExportFoodQualitätsfälleGLEKINT
 * Generates batch Quality reports filtered by GL-EK INT (Col D).
 * HARDCODED SPLIT: If recipient is "BM", it splits into "Eigenmarke" (Col X = "EM") 
 * and "Marke" (Col X = "M") as per VBA Modul11.
 */

function openFoodQualiGLEKINTDialog() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");
  
  if (!sheetExport) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // Fetch Dashboard Texts once
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
  } catch (e) {
    folderId = folderUrl; 
  }

  // Get KW explicitly from Food Qualitätsfälle cell S5
  const qualiSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Food Qualitätsfälle");
  const kwValue = qualiSheet ? qualiSheet.getRange("S5").getValue() : "XX";

  // Package layout data
  const layout = {
    htl: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle header left"), 
    htc: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle header center"), 
    htr: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle header right"),
    fbl: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle footer left"), // Usually contains "Legende..."
    fbc: "Statistik KW " + kwValue + "\n- [PAGE] -", 
    fbr: getDashboardText("Food Qualitätsfälle footer right")
  };

  const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('ExportFoodQualitätsfälleGLEKINT_HTML');
  htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
    layout: layout, 
    folderId: folderId,
    kwValue: kwValue
  });
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(
    htmlTemplate.evaluate().setWidth(600).setHeight(500), 
    'Generating Quality Reports (GL-EK INT)...'
  );
}

/**
 * Gets unique recipients from Mapping Col J (Index 10)
 * Replaces "BM" with two distinct tasks for the HTML queue.
 */
function getQualiIntTasks() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Mapping");
  if (!sheet) throw new Error("Sheet 'Mapping' nicht gefunden.");
  
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return [];
  
  const data = sheet.getRange(2, 10, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues().flat();
  const unique = [...new Set(data)].filter(String).sort();

  const tasks = [];
  unique.forEach(recipient => {
    if (recipient === "BM") {
      tasks.push("BM_Eigenmarke");
      tasks.push("BM_Marke");
    } else {
      tasks.push(recipient);
    }
  });

  return tasks;
}

/**
 * Server-side generation of Base PDF for a specific task
 */
function getQualiPdfDataForTask(task) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  const config = { 
    name: "Food Qualitätsfälle", 
    filterColD: 4,     // Column D (GL-EK INT)
    filterColX: 24,    // Column X (EM/M flag)
    headerRows: 5,     // Data starts at Row 6
    keepCols: 22       // Print Area A:V
  };

  const liveSheet = ss.getSheetByName(config.name);
  if (!liveSheet) return { skipped: true, task: task };

  const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
  const tempSheet = liveSheet.copyTo(ss);
  tempSheet.setName("Temp_Quali_" + uniqueSuffix);
  const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
  tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

  // Interpret Task
  let targetRecipient = task;
  let targetEMFlag = null;

  if (task === "BM_Eigenmarke") {
    targetRecipient = "BM";
    targetEMFlag = "EM";
  } else if (task === "BM_Marke") {
    targetRecipient = "BM";
    targetEMFlag = "M";
  }

  try {
    const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
    if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

    // Expand columns temporarily to ensure we can read Col X if it's hidden
    tempSheet.showColumns(1, tempSheet.getMaxColumns());

    const lastRow = tempSheet.getLastRow();
    let hasData = true;

    if (lastRow > config.headerRows) {
      // Read data before deleting columns
      const valuesD = tempSheet.getRange(config.headerRows + 1, config.filterColD, lastRow - config.headerRows, 1).getValues().flat();
      
      // Ensure the sheet is wide enough to read Col X
      let valuesX = [];
      if (tempSheet.getMaxColumns() >= config.filterColX) {
         valuesX = tempSheet.getRange(config.headerRows + 1, config.filterColX, lastRow - config.headerRows, 1).getValues().flat();
      }

      const deleteRequests = [];
      let startDelete = -1;
      let dataCount = 0;

      for (let i = 0; i < valuesD.length; i++) {
        let keepRow = false;

        // Matching Logic
        if (valuesD[i] === targetRecipient) {
          if (!targetEMFlag) {
            keepRow = true; // Normal recipient
          } else if (targetEMFlag === "EM" && valuesX[i] === "EM") {
            keepRow = true; // BM Eigenmarke
          } else if (targetEMFlag === "M" && valuesX[i] === "M") {
            keepRow = true; // BM Marke
          }
        }

        // Deletion batching
        if (!keepRow) {
          if (startDelete === -1) startDelete = i;
        } else {
          if (startDelete !== -1) {
            deleteRequests.push({ deleteDimension: { range: { sheetId: sheetId, dimension: "ROWS", startIndex: config.headerRows + startDelete, endIndex: config.headerRows + i } } });
            startDelete = -1;
          }
          dataCount++;
        }
      }
      
      if (startDelete !== -1) {
        deleteRequests.push({ deleteDimension: { range: { sheetId: sheetId, dimension: "ROWS", startIndex: config.headerRows + startDelete, endIndex: config.headerRows + valuesD.length } } });
      }
      if (deleteRequests.length > 0) {
        deleteRequests.reverse();
        Sheets.Spreadsheets.batchUpdate({ requests: deleteRequests }, ss.getId());
      }
      
      if (dataCount === 0) hasData = false;
    } else {
      hasData = false;
    }

    // Now it's safe to trim the extra columns (W, X, Y, Z...) to lock the print area to A:V
    const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
    if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

    SpreadsheetApp.flush();

    // Skip if empty
    if (!hasData) {
      ss.deleteSheet(tempSheet);
      return { skipped: true, task: task };
    }

    // // Fetch Base PDF (LANDSCAPE mode)
    // const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
    //   `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}&size=A4&portrait=false&fitw=true&gridlines=false` +
    //   `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
    //   `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

    // Fetch Base PDF (LANDSCAPE mode)
    const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
      `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}&size=A4&portrait=false&scale=2&gridlines=false` +
      `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
      `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

    const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token }, muteHttpExceptions: true });
    
    if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
      return {
        skipped: false,
        task: task,
        base64: Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes()),
        tempSheets: tempSheetIds
      };
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.error(e);
  }

  // Fallback cleanup
  if (ss.getSheetByName("Temp_Quali_" + uniqueSuffix)) {
    ss.deleteSheet(ss.getSheetByName("Temp_Quali_" + uniqueSuffix));
  }
  return { skipped: true, task: task };
}

function saveQualiPdfToDrive_batch(base64Data, filename, folderId, tempSheets) {
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId);
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  if (base64Data) {
    const decodedBytes = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(decodedBytes, 'application/pdf', filename);
    folder.createFile(blob);
  }

  // Cleanup temp sheets
  for (const ts of tempSheets) {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
    if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
  }
  return true;
}

ExportFoodQualitätsfälleGLEKINT_HTML.html

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/pdf-lib/dist/pdf-lib.min.js"></script>
    <style>
      body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
      .spinner { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #e74c3c; border-radius: 50%; width: 30px; height: 30px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 10px auto; }
      @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
      .progress-container { width: 100%; background-color: #ddd; margin-top: 20px; border-radius: 5px; }
      .progress-bar { width: 0%; height: 20px; background-color: #c0392b; border-radius: 5px; transition: width 0.3s; }
      .log { height: 250px; overflow-y: auto; background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px solid #ccc; margin-top: 15px; padding: 10px; text-align: left; font-size: 12px; font-family: monospace; }
      .log-item { margin-bottom: 4px; border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; padding-bottom: 2px;}
      .ok-msg { color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; }
      .skip-msg { color: #f39c12; font-weight: bold; }
      .error-msg { color: #e74c3c; font-weight: bold; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h3>Generating Quality Reports (GL-EK INT)</h3>
    <div id="loader" class="spinner"></div>
    <div id="status">Initializing...</div>
    <div class="progress-container"><div id="bar" class="progress-bar"></div></div>
    <div id="log" class="log"></div>

    <script>
      const payloadData = <?!= payload ?>;
      const { PDFDocument, StandardFonts, rgb } = PDFLib;
      const CONCURRENCY = 3; 

      window.onload = function() { startBatchProcess(); };

      async function startBatchProcess() {
        log("Fetching recipients from Mapping tab...");
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(runQueue)
          .withFailureHandler(handleError)
          .getQualiIntTasks();
      }

      function sanitizeText(text) {
        if (!text) return "";
        return text.toString().normalize('NFC'); 
      }

      function base64ToUint8(base64) {
        const binary_string = window.atob(base64);
        const len = binary_string.length;
        const bytes = new Uint8Array(len);
        for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) { bytes[i] = binary_string.charCodeAt(i); }
        return bytes;
      }

      function uint8ToBase64(uint8) {
        let binary = '';
        for (let i = 0; i < uint8.byteLength; i++) { binary += String.fromCharCode(uint8[i]); }
        return window.btoa(binary);
      }

      async function runQueue(tasks) {
        log(`Found ${tasks.length} tasks. Starting processing...`);
        let index = 0;
        let activeWorkers = 0;
        let completed = 0;
        const total = tasks.length;

        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          const next = () => {
            if (index >= total && activeWorkers === 0) {
              finish();
              resolve();
              return;
            }

            while (activeWorkers < CONCURRENCY && index < total) {
              const task = tasks[index++];
              activeWorkers++;
              updateStatus(`Queue: ${activeWorkers} active | ${total - index} pending`);

              processSingleTask(task)
                .then((res) => {
                  if (res === "SKIPPED") {
                    log(`<span class="skip-msg">⚠️ Skipped: ${task} (No Data)</span>`);
                  } else {
                    log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Saved: ${task}</span>`);
                  }
                })
                .catch((err) => log(`<span class="error-msg">❌ Error ${task}: ${err.message}</span>`))
                .finally(() => {
                  activeWorkers--;
                  completed++;
                  updateProgress(completed, total);
                  next();
                });
            }
          };
          next();
        });
      }

      function processSingleTask(task) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(async (response) => {
              try {
                if (response.skipped) {
                  resolve("SKIPPED");
                  return;
                }

                const pdfBytes = base64ToUint8(response.base64);
                const pdfDoc = await PDFDocument.load(pdfBytes);
                
                const fontRegular = await pdfDoc.embedFont(StandardFonts.Helvetica);
                const fontBold = await pdfDoc.embedFont(StandardFonts.HelveticaBold);

                const pages = pdfDoc.getPages();

                for (let i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {
                  const page = pages[i];
                  const { width, height } = page.getSize(); 
                  const pageNumStr = (i + 1).toString();

                  const headerSize = 7.5; 
                  const centerSize = 12;  
                  const footerSize = 8;   
                  const xMargin = 30;             
                  const yTop = height - 20;     
                  const yBottom = 25;           

                  const regex = /\[PAGEA?\]|\[PAGE A\]/gi;
                  const htl = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.htl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const htc = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.htc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const htr = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.htr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const fbl = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.fbl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const fbc = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.fbc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const fbr = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.fbr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);

                  const drawTextMultiline = (text, align, isHeader, startY, fontSize, textFont) => {
                    if (!text) return;
                    const lines = text.split('\n');
                    const lineHeight = fontSize * 1.25;
                    // Because footers like the "Legende" can be very tall, we calculate Y carefully.
                    let currentY = isHeader ? startY : startY + ((lines.length - 1) * lineHeight);

                    lines.forEach(line => {
                      let xPos = xMargin; 
                      if (align === 'center') {
                        xPos = (width - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize)) / 2;
                      } else if (align === 'right') {
                        xPos = width - xMargin - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize);
                      }
                      page.drawText(line, { x: xPos, y: currentY, size: fontSize, font: textFont, color: rgb(0,0,0) });
                      currentY -= lineHeight; 
                    });
                  };

                  drawTextMultiline(htl, 'left',   true, yTop, headerSize, fontBold);
                  drawTextMultiline(htc, 'center', true, yTop - 15, centerSize, fontBold);
                  drawTextMultiline(htr, 'right',  true, yTop - 5, headerSize, fontBold);
                  drawTextMultiline(fbl, 'left',   false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                  drawTextMultiline(fbc, 'center', false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                  drawTextMultiline(fbr, 'right',  false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                }

                const finalPdfBytes = await pdfDoc.save();
                const finalBase64 = uint8ToBase64(finalPdfBytes);
                const finalFilename = `04_Statistik_Food_Qualitätsreklamationen_${task}_KW${payloadData.kwValue}_INT.pdf`;

                google.script.run
                  .withSuccessHandler(resolve)
                  .withFailureHandler(reject)
                  .saveQualiPdfToDrive_batch(finalBase64, finalFilename, payloadData.folderId, response.tempSheets);

              } catch (err) {
                reject(err);
              }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(reject)
            .getQualiPdfDataForTask(task);
        });
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { 
        const div = document.getElementById("log"); 
        div.innerHTML += `<div class="log-item">${msg}</div>`; 
        div.scrollTop = div.scrollHeight; 
      }
      function updateProgress(current, total) { 
        document.getElementById("bar").style.width = Math.round((current / total) * 100) + "%"; 
      }
      function handleError(e) { log(`FATAL ERROR: ${e.message}`); }
      function finish() { 
        document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none"; 
        updateStatus("Batch Processing Complete! Cleaning up..."); 
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(() => { setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 2000); })
          .cleanUpOrphanedTempSheets();
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

ExportPDFOGGesamt.gs
// /**
//  * SERVER SIDE: ExportPDFOGGesamt (O+G Gesamt)
//  * Generates 4 parts for the O+G report and saves them as 2 different files (per VBA logic).
//  */

// function ExportPDFOGGesamt_new() {
//   const html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('ExportPDFOGGesamt_HTML')
//       .setWidth(500)
//       .setHeight(400);
//   SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, 'Generating O+G Gesamt Report...');
// }

// /**
//  * Generates a specific part (1-4) of the report
//  */
// function getOGGesamtPart(partNumber) {
//   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
//   const year = new Date().getFullYear();
  
//   // Get KW

/**
 * 🖨️ EXPORT O+G GESAMT (Merged PDF - Dual Output)
 * Combines 4 O+G sheets into a single merged Landscape PDF.
 * Saves TWO identical copies with different filenames per VBA Modul15 logic.
 */

function export_og_gesamt() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");

  if (!sheetExport) {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. RESOLVE FOLDER ---
  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
    DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId); 
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert("Ordner Fehler", "Der Zielordner konnte nicht gefunden werden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // Get KW explicitly from O+G Qualitätsfälle cell N5 as per VBA
  const kwSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Qualitätsfälle");
  const kwValue = kwSheet ? kwSheet.getRange("N5").getValue() : "XX";

  ss.toast("Prüfe 4 O+G Tabellenblätter... Bitte warten.", "Schritt 1/3", 15);

  // --- 2. FETCH DASHBOARD DATA (B31:D144) ---
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  // --- 3. CONFIGURATIONS FOR THE 4 SHEETS ---
  const configs = [
    {
      name: "O+G Sortimentswünsche", dataRowStart: 7, keepCols: 11,
      keys: {
        htl: "O+G Sortimentswünsche header left", htc: "O+G Sortimentswünsche header center", htr: "O+G Sortimentswünsche header right",
        fbl: "O+G Sortimentswünsche footer left", fbc: "O+G Sortimentswünsche footer center", fbr: "O+G Sortimentswünsche footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "O+G Sonstiges", dataRowStart: 7, keepCols: 11,
      keys: {
        htl: "O+G Sonstiges header left", htc: "O+G Sonstiges header center", htr: "O+G Sonstiges header right",
        fbl: "O+G Sonstiges footer left", fbc: "O+G Sonstiges footer center", fbr: "O+G Sonstiges footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "O+G Qualitätsfälle", dataRowStart: 6, keepCols: 15,
      keys: {
        htl: "O+G Qualitätsfälle header left", htc: "O+G Qualitätsfälle header center", htr: "O+G Qualitätsfälle header right",
        fbl: "O+G Qualitätsfälle footer left", fbc: "O+G Qualitätsfälle footer center", fbr: "O+G Qualitätsfälle footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN", dataRowStart: 6, keepCols: 15,
      keys: {
        htl: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN header left", htc: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN header center", htr: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN header right",
        fbl: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN footer left", fbc: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN footer center", fbr: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN footer right"
      }
    }
  ];

  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const pdfParts = [];
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  // --- 4. PREPARE BASE PDFs ---
  for (const config of configs) {
    const liveSheet = ss.getSheetByName(config.name);
    if (!liveSheet) continue;

    const lastRow = liveSheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < config.dataRowStart) continue; 

    const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
    const tempSheet = liveSheet.copyTo(ss);
    tempSheet.setName("Temp_OG_Gesamt_" + uniqueSuffix);
    const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
    tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

    try {
      const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
      if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

      const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
      if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

      SpreadsheetApp.flush(); 
      Utilities.sleep(1000); 

      const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
        `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}&size=A4&portrait=false&scale=2&gridlines=false` +
        `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
        `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

      const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token }, muteHttpExceptions: true });

      if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        pdfParts.push({
          sheetName: config.name,
          base64: Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes()),
          layout: {
            htl: getDashboardText(config.keys.htl), htc: getDashboardText(config.keys.htc), htr: getDashboardText(config.keys.htr),
            fbl: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbl), fbc: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbc), fbr: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbr)
          }
        });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    }
  }

  // --- 5. OPEN DEDICATED HTML FRONTEND ---
  if (pdfParts.length > 0) {
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('ExportPDFOGGesamt_HTML');
    htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
      parts: pdfParts, 
      folderId: folderId, 
      kwValue: kwValue, 
      tempSheets: tempSheetIds 
    });
    
    const htmlOutput = htmlTemplate.evaluate().setWidth(500).setHeight(300).setTitle('Generiere O+G Gesamt Report...');
    ui.showModalDialog(htmlOutput, 'Erstelle O+G Gesamt Report...');
  } else {
    ui.alert("Hinweis", "Keine der ausgewählten O+G Tabellen enthält Daten.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    for (const ts of tempSheetIds) {
      const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
      if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
    }
  }
}

/**
 * UNIQUE BACKEND CALLBACK: Saves the exact same PDF twice with two distinct names.
 */
function saveOGGesamtDualPdfs(base64Data, kwValue, folderId, tempSheets) {
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId);
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  if (base64Data) {
    const decodedBytes = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
    
    // Create File 1
    const file1Name = `8-Wochen-Statistik_O+G_KW${kwValue}.pdf`;
    const blob1 = Utilities.newBlob(decodedBytes, 'application/pdf', file1Name);
    folder.createFile(blob1);

    // Create File 2 (Identical contents, different name)
    const file2Name = `05_Statistik_O+G_komplett_KW${kwValue}.pdf`;
    const blob2 = Utilities.newBlob(decodedBytes, 'application/pdf', file2Name);
    folder.createFile(blob2);
  }

  // Clean up Temp Sheets
  for (const ts of tempSheets) {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
    if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
  }

  cleanUpOrphanedTempSheets();
  
  return true;
}

ExportPDFOGGesamt_HTML.html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <base target="_top">
  <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/pdf-lib/dist/pdf-lib.min.js"></script>
  <style>
    body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; color: #333; }
    .loader { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #e67e22; border-radius: 50%; width: 40px; height: 40px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 20px auto; }
    @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
    #status { font-size: 14px; margin-top: 10px; }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  
  <h3>O+G PDF wird zusammengeführt...</h3>
  <div class="loader" id="spinner"></div>
  <div id="status">Lese Dokumententeile... Bitte warten.</div>

  <script>
    const payloadData = <?!= payload ?>;
    
    function uint8ToBase64(uint8) {
      let binary = '';
      for (let i = 0; i < uint8.byteLength; i++) { binary += String.fromCharCode(uint8[i]); }
      return window.btoa(binary);
    }

    function base64ToUint8(base64) {
      const binary_string = window.atob(base64);
      const len = binary_string.length;
      const bytes = new Uint8Array(len);
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) { bytes[i] = binary_string.charCodeAt(i); }
      return bytes;
    }

    function sanitizeText(text) {
      if (!text) return "";
      return text.toString().normalize('NFC'); 
    }

    async function processMergedPdf() {
      const { PDFDocument, StandardFonts } = PDFLib;
      document.getElementById('status').innerText = "Stemple und kombiniere Seiten...";

      try {
        const masterPdf = await PDFDocument.create();
        let globalPageCounter = 1;

        for (const part of payloadData.parts) {
          const partPdfBytes = base64ToUint8(part.base64);
          const partPdf = await PDFDocument.load(partPdfBytes);
          
          const fontRegular = await partPdf.embedFont(StandardFonts.Helvetica);
          const fontBold = await partPdf.embedFont(StandardFonts.HelveticaBold);

          const pages = partPdf.getPages();

          for (let i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {
            const page = pages[i];
            const { width, height } = page.getSize(); 
            const pageNumStr = globalPageCounter.toString();

            const headerSize = 7.5; 
            const centerSize = 12;  
            const footerSize = 8;   
            const xMargin = 30;             
            const yTop = height - 20;     
            const yBottom = 25;           
            
            const regex = /\[PAGEA?\]|\[PAGE A\]/gi;
            const htl = sanitizeText(part.layout.htl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
            const htc = sanitizeText(part.layout.htc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
            const htr = sanitizeText(part.layout.htr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
            const fbl = sanitizeText(part.layout.fbl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
            const fbc = sanitizeText(part.layout.fbc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
            const fbr = sanitizeText(part.layout.fbr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);

            const drawTextMultiline = (text, align, isHeader, startY, fontSize, textFont) => {
              if (!text) return;
              const lines = text.split('\n');
              const lineHeight = fontSize * 1.25;
              let currentY = isHeader ? startY : startY + ((lines.length - 1) * lineHeight);

              lines.forEach(line => {
                let xPos = xMargin; 
                if (align === 'center') {
                  xPos = (width - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize)) / 2;
                } else if (align === 'right') {
                  xPos = width - xMargin - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize);
                }
                page.drawText(line, { x: xPos, y: currentY, size: fontSize, font: textFont });
                currentY -= lineHeight; 
              });
            };

            drawTextMultiline(htl, 'left',   true, yTop, headerSize, fontBold);
            drawTextMultiline(htc, 'center', true, yTop - 15, centerSize, fontBold);
            drawTextMultiline(htr, 'right',  true, yTop - 5, headerSize, fontBold);
            drawTextMultiline(fbl, 'left',   false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
            drawTextMultiline(fbc, 'center', false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
            drawTextMultiline(fbr, 'right',  false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);

            globalPageCounter++;
          }

          const copiedPages = await masterPdf.copyPages(partPdf, partPdf.getPageIndices());
          copiedPages.forEach((p) => masterPdf.addPage(p));
        }

        const finalPdfBytes = await masterPdf.save();
        const finalBase64 = uint8ToBase64(finalPdfBytes);

        document.getElementById('status').innerText = "Speichere beide PDFs in Google Drive...";
        
        // CAUTION: Calls the specific O+G Callback!
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler((result) => {
            document.getElementById('spinner').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('status').innerHTML = `<b>Erfolg!</b> Beide Dokumente wurden gespeichert. Fenster schließt sich...`;
            setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 2500);
          })
          .withFailureHandler((err) => {
            document.getElementById('spinner').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('status').innerText = "Fehler beim Speichern: " + err.message;
          })
          .saveOGGesamtDualPdfs(finalBase64, payloadData.kwValue, payloadData.folderId, payloadData.tempSheets);

      } catch (error) {
        document.getElementById('spinner').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('status').innerText = "Fehler beim Rendering: " + error.message;
      }
    }

    window.onload = processMergedPdf;
  </script>
</body>
</html>

/**
 * 🖨️ EXPORT QUALITÄTSFÄLLE FOOD GESAMT
 * Exports the "Food Qualitätsfälle" sheet as a single Landscape PDF.
 * Reuses the 'multi-page-support-pdf-lib' frontend engine for perfect rendering.
 */

function ExportQualitätsfälleFoodGesamt_new() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");

  if (!sheetExport) {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. RESOLVE FOLDER ---
  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
    DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId); 
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert("Ordner Fehler", "Der Zielordner konnte nicht gefunden werden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // Get KW explicitly from Food Qualitätsfälle cell S5 as per VBA (Modul7)
  const qualiSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Food Qualitätsfälle");
  if (!qualiSheet) {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'Food Qualitätsfälle' nicht gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }
  const kwValue = qualiSheet.getRange("S5").getValue() || "XX";

  ss.toast("Prüfe Tabellenblatt... Bitte warten.", "Export", 5);

  // --- 2. FETCH DASHBOARD DATA (B31:D144) ---
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  // --- 3. CONFIGURATION ---
  const config = {
    name: "Food Qualitätsfälle", 
    dataRowStart: 6, // Data starts at row 6
    keepCols: 22,    // Print Area A:V (22 columns)
    keys: {
      htl: "Food Qualitätsfälle header left", htc: "Food Qualitätsfälle header center", htr: "Food Qualitätsfälle header right",
      fbl: "Food Qualitätsfälle footer left", fbc: "Food Qualitätsfälle footer center", fbr: "Food Qualitätsfälle footer right"
    }
  };

  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const pdfParts = [];
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  // --- 4. PREPARE BASE PDF ---
  const lastRow = qualiSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < config.dataRowStart) {
    ui.alert("Hinweis", "Keine Daten zum Exportieren gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return; 
  }

  // Clone & Trim
  const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
  const tempSheet = qualiSheet.copyTo(ss);
  tempSheet.setName("Temp_Quali_" + uniqueSuffix);
  const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
  tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

  try {
    const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
    if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

    const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
    if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

    SpreadsheetApp.flush(); 
    Utilities.sleep(1000); 

    // Fetch Base PDF (LANDSCAPE via portrait=false)
    const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
      `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}` +
      `&size=A4&portrait=false&scale=2&gridlines=false` +
      `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED` +
      `&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
      `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

    const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
      headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    });

    if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
      const base64Pdf = Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes());
      
      pdfParts.push({
        sheetName: config.name,
        base64: base64Pdf,
        layout: {
          htl: getDashboardText(config.keys.htl),
          htc: getDashboardText(config.keys.htc),
          htr: getDashboardText(config.keys.htr),
          fbl: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbl),
          fbc: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbc),
          fbr: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbr)
        }
      });
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.error(e);
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Fehler beim Exportieren: " + e.message, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  }

  // --- 5. OPEN HTML FRONTEND ---
  if (pdfParts.length > 0) {
    // Filename matching VBA: 04_Statistik_Food_Qualitätsreklamationen_KW[S5]_DE
    const finalFilename = `04_Statistik_Food_Qualitätsreklamationen_KW${kwValue}_DE.pdf`;
    
    // REUSING the existing HTML engine!
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('multi-page-support-pdf-lib');
    htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
      parts: pdfParts, 
      folderId: folderId, 
      filename: finalFilename,
      tempSheets: tempSheetIds 
    });
    
    const htmlOutput = htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setWidth(500)
      .setHeight(300)
      .setTitle('Generiere Food Qualitätsfälle Report...');
      
    ui.showModalDialog(htmlOutput, 'Erstelle Food Qualitätsfälle Report...');
  } else {
    // Cleanup on failure
    const sheetToDelete = ss.getSheetByName(tempSheetIds[0].name);
    if (sheetToDelete) ss.deleteSheet(sheetToDelete);
  }
}

ExportQualitätsfälleFoodGesamt_HTML.html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <style>
      body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
      .spinner { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #2980b9; border-radius: 50%; width: 30px; height: 30px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 10px auto; }
      @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
      .status { font-weight: bold; color: #555; }
      .ok-msg { color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; margin-top: 15px;}
      .error-msg { color: #c0392b; font-weight: bold; margin-top: 15px;}
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h3>Generating Quality Report (DE)</h3>
    <div id="loader" class="spinner"></div>
    <div id="status" class="status">Processing...</div>
    <div id="result"></div>

    <script>
      window.onload = function() { startProcess(); };

      function startProcess() {
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler((res) => {
            if (res.success) {
              document.getElementById("status").innerText = "Saving file...";
              google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(() => {
                document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none";
                document.getElementById("status").style.display = "none";
                document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = `<div class="ok-msg">✅ Success!<br>${res.filename} saved.</div>`;
              }).saveQualiPdf(res.blobData, res.filename, res.folderId);
            } else {
              document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none";
              document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = `<div class="error-msg">❌ Error: ${res.message}</div>`;
            }
          })
          .withFailureHandler((err) => {
            document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = `<div class="error-msg">❌ System Error: ${err.message}</div>`;
          })
          .getQualiFoodPdf();
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

/**
 * 🖨️ EXPORT QUALITÄTSFÄLLE O+G GESAMT (Merged PDF)
 * Combines 2 O+G Quality sheets into a single merged Landscape PDF.
 * Reuses the 'multi-page-support-pdf-lib' frontend engine.
 */

function ExportQualitätsfälleOGGesamt_new() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");

  if (!sheetExport) {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. RESOLVE FOLDER ---
  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
    DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId); 
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert("Ordner Fehler", "Der Zielordner konnte nicht gefunden werden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- STRICT VBA PARITY: Get KW explicitly from O+G Qualitätsfälle cell N5 ---
  const kwSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Qualitätsfälle");
  const kwValue = kwSheet ? kwSheet.getRange("N5").getValue() : "XX";

  ss.toast("Prüfe O+G Qualitätsfälle Tabellen... Bitte warten.", "Schritt 1/3", 15);

  // --- 2. FETCH DASHBOARD DATA (B31:D144) ---
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  // --- 3. CONFIGURATIONS FOR THE 2 SHEETS ---
  const configs = [
    {
      name: "O+G Qualitätsfälle", dataRowStart: 6, keepCols: 15, // Print Area A:O
      keys: {
        htl: "O+G Qualitätsfälle header left", htc: "O+G Qualitätsfälle header center", htr: "O+G Qualitätsfälle header right",
        fbl: "O+G Qualitätsfälle footer left", fbc: "O+G Qualitätsfälle footer center", fbr: "O+G Qualitätsfälle footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN", dataRowStart: 6, keepCols: 15, // Print Area A:O
      keys: {
        htl: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN header left", htc: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN header center", htr: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN header right",
        fbl: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN footer left", fbc: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN footer center", fbr: "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN footer right"
      }
    }
  ];

  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const pdfParts = [];
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  // --- 4. PREPARE BASE PDFs (Landscape, Skips Empty) ---
  for (const config of configs) {
    const liveSheet = ss.getSheetByName(config.name);
    if (!liveSheet) continue;

    // Skip if no data (matching VBA check logic)
    const lastRow = liveSheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < config.dataRowStart) {
      console.log(`Skipping ${config.name} - No Data`);
      continue; 
    }

    // Clone & Trim
    const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
    const tempSheet = liveSheet.copyTo(ss);
    tempSheet.setName("Temp_OGQuali_" + uniqueSuffix);
    const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
    tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

    try {
      const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
      if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

      const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
      if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

      SpreadsheetApp.flush(); 
      Utilities.sleep(1000); 

      // Fetch Base PDF (Forced LANDSCAPE via portrait=false)
      const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
        `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}` +
        `&size=A4&portrait=false&scale=2&gridlines=false` +
        `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED` +
        `&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
        `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

      const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
        headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      });

      if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        const base64Pdf = Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes());
        
        pdfParts.push({
          sheetName: config.name,
          base64: base64Pdf,
          layout: {
            htl: getDashboardText(config.keys.htl),
            htc: getDashboardText(config.keys.htc),
            htr: getDashboardText(config.keys.htr),
            fbl: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbl),
            fbc: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbc),
            fbr: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbr)
          }
        });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    }
  }

  // --- 5. OPEN HTML FRONTEND ---
  if (pdfParts.length > 0) {
    const finalFilename = `05_Statistik_O+G_Qualitätsreklamationen_KW${kwValue}.pdf`;
    
    // REUSING the existing HTML engine!
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('multi-page-support-pdf-lib');
    htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
      parts: pdfParts, 
      folderId: folderId, 
      filename: finalFilename,
      tempSheets: tempSheetIds 
    });
    
    const htmlOutput = htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setWidth(500)
      .setHeight(300)
      .setTitle('Generiere O+G Qualitätsfälle Report...');
      
    ui.showModalDialog(htmlOutput, 'Erstelle O+G Qualitätsfälle Report...');
  } else {
    ui.alert("Hinweis", "Keine der ausgewählten O+G Tabellen enthält Daten.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    // Cleanup temp sheets on failure
    for (const ts of tempSheetIds) {
      const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
      if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
    }
  }
}

ExportQualitätsfälleOGGesamt_HTML.html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/pdf-lib@1.17.1/dist/pdf-lib.min.js"></script>
    <style>
      body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
      .spinner { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #16a085; border-radius: 50%; width: 30px; height: 30px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 10px auto; }
      @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
      .log { height: 250px; overflow-y: auto; background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px solid #ccc; margin-top: 15px; padding: 10px; text-align: left; font-size: 12px; font-family: monospace; }
      .log-item { margin-bottom: 4px; border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; }
      .ok-msg { color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; }
      .skip-msg { color: #f39c12; font-weight: bold; }
      .error-msg { color: #e74c3c; font-weight: bold; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h3>Generating O+G Quality Report (Gesamt)</h3>
    <div id="loader" class="spinner"></div>
    <div id="status">Starting...</div>
    <div id="log" class="log"></div>

    <script>
      const { PDFDocument } = PDFLib;

      window.onload = function() { startProcess(); };

      async function startProcess() {
        log("Generating 2 Parts...");
        
        const promises = [
          getPart(1),
          getPart(2)
        ];

        try {
          const results = await Promise.all(promises);
          log("Parts received. Merging...");
          await mergeAndSave(results);

        } catch (e) {
          log(`<span class="error-msg">FATAL ERROR: ${e.message}</span>`);
          document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none";
        }
      }

      function getPart(num) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler((res) => {
              if (res.blobData) {
                log(`Part ${num} generated.`);
              } else {
                log(`<span class="skip-msg">Part ${num} skipped (No Data).</span>`);
              }
              resolve(res);
            })
            .withFailureHandler((err) => {
              log(`<span class="error-msg">Error Part ${num}: ${err.message}</span>`);
              reject(err);
            })
            .getOGQualiPart(num);
        });
      }

      async function mergeAndSave(results) {
        results.sort((a, b) => a.partNumber - b.partNumber);

        const mergedPdf = await PDFDocument.create();
        let hasContent = false;
        let filename = "OG_Quali_Gesamt.pdf";
        let folderId = "";

        for (const res of results) {
          if (res.blobData) {
            hasContent = true;
            filename = res.filename; 
            folderId = res.folderId;
            const pdfSrc = await PDFDocument.load(res.blobData);
            const copiedPages = await mergedPdf.copyPages(pdfSrc, pdfSrc.getPageIndices());
            copiedPages.forEach((page) => mergedPdf.addPage(page));
          }
        }

        if (!hasContent) {
          log("No data found in either sheet. Nothing to save.");
          finish();
          return;
        }

        updateStatus("Saving final PDF...");
        const mergedBytes = await mergedPdf.saveAsBase64();

        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(() => {
            log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Success! File saved: ${filename}</span>`);
            finish();
          })
          .saveOGQualiGesamtPdf(mergedBytes, filename, folderId);
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { const div = document.getElementById("log"); div.innerHTML += `<div class="log-item">${msg}</div>`; div.scrollTop = div.scrollHeight; }
      function finish() { document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none"; updateStatus("Complete!"); }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

/**
 * 🖨️ EXPORT SONSTIGES FOOD GESAMT 
 * Exports the "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen" sheet as a single Landscape PDF.
 * Reuses the 'multi-page-support-pdf-lib' frontend engine.
 */

function export_sonstiges_food_gesamt() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");

  if (!sheetExport) {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. RESOLVE FOLDER ---
  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
    DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId); 
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert("Ordner Fehler", "Der Zielordner konnte nicht gefunden werden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // Get KW explicitly from Sonstiges sheet (Cell N6) as per VBA Modul6
  const sonstigesSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen");
  if (!sonstigesSheet) {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen' nicht gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }
  const kwValue = sonstigesSheet.getRange("N6").getValue() || "XX";

  ss.toast("Prüfe Tabellenblatt... Bitte warten.", "Export", 5);

  // --- 2. FETCH DASHBOARD DATA (B31:D144) ---
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  // --- 3. CONFIGURATION ---
  const config = {
    name: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen", 
    dataRowStart: 7, // Data starts at row 7
    keepCols: 15,    // Print Area A:O (15 columns)
    keys: {
      htl: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header left", htc: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header center", htr: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header right",
      fbl: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer left", fbc: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer center", fbr: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer right"
    }
  };

  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const pdfParts = [];
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  // --- 4. PREPARE BASE PDF ---
  const lastRow = sonstigesSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < config.dataRowStart) {
    ui.alert("Hinweis", "Keine Daten zum Exportieren gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return; 
  }

  // Clone & Trim
  const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
  const tempSheet = sonstigesSheet.copyTo(ss);
  tempSheet.setName("Temp_Sonst_" + uniqueSuffix);
  const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
  tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

  try {
    const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
    if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

    const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
    if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

    SpreadsheetApp.flush(); 
    Utilities.sleep(1000); 

    // Fetch Base PDF (LANDSCAPE via portrait=false)
    const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
      `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}` +
      `&size=A4&portrait=false&scale=2&gridlines=false` +
      `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED` +
      `&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
      `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

    const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
      headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    });

    if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
      const base64Pdf = Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes());
      
      pdfParts.push({
        sheetName: config.name,
        base64: base64Pdf,
        layout: {
          htl: getDashboardText(config.keys.htl),
          htc: getDashboardText(config.keys.htc),
          htr: getDashboardText(config.keys.htr),
          fbl: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbl),
          fbc: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbc),
          fbr: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbr)
        }
      });
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.error(e);
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Fehler beim Exportieren: " + e.message, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  }

  // --- 5. OPEN HTML FRONTEND ---
  if (pdfParts.length > 0) {
    const finalFilename = `03_Statistik_Food_Sonstiges Food_KW${kwValue}_DE.pdf`;
    
    // REUSING the existing HTML engine!
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('multi-page-support-pdf-lib');
    htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
      parts: pdfParts, 
      folderId: folderId, 
      filename: finalFilename,
      tempSheets: tempSheetIds 
    });
    
    const htmlOutput = htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setWidth(500)
      .setHeight(300)
      .setTitle('Generiere Sonstiges Food Report...');
      
    ui.showModalDialog(htmlOutput, 'Erstelle Sonstiges Food Report...');
  } else {
    // Cleanup on failure
    const sheetToDelete = ss.getSheetByName(tempSheetIds[0].name);
    if (sheetToDelete) ss.deleteSheet(sheetToDelete);
  }
}

ExportSonstigesFoodGesamt_HTML.html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/pdf-lib@1.17.1/dist/pdf-lib.min.js"></script>
    <style>
      body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
      .spinner { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #27ae60; border-radius: 50%; width: 30px; height: 30px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 10px auto; }
      @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
      .progress-container { width: 100%; background-color: #ddd; margin-top: 20px; border-radius: 5px; }
      .progress-bar { width: 0%; height: 20px; background-color: #2ecc71; border-radius: 5px; transition: width 0.3s; }
      .log { height: 250px; overflow-y: auto; background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px solid #ccc; margin-top: 15px; padding: 10px; text-align: left; font-size: 12px; font-family: monospace; }
      .log-item { margin-bottom: 4px; border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; }
      .skip-msg { color: #f39c12; font-weight: bold; }
      .ok-msg { color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; }
      .error-msg { color: #e74c3c; font-weight: bold; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h3>Generating Sonstiges Food Reports</h3>
    <div id="loader" class="spinner"></div>
    <div id="status">Initializing...</div>
    <div class="progress-container"><div id="bar" class="progress-bar"></div></div>
    <div id="log" class="log"></div>

    <script>
      const CONCURRENCY = 5; 

      window.onload = function() { startBatchProcess(); };

      async function startBatchProcess() {
        log("Fetching recipients from Col D...");
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(runQueue).withFailureHandler(handleError).getSonstigesRecipients();
      }

      function runQueue(recipients) {
        log(`Found ${recipients.length} recipients. Starting queue...`);
        let index = 0; let activeWorkers = 0; let completed = 0;
        const total = recipients.length;

        if(total === 0) { finish(); return; }

        const next = () => {
          if (index >= total && activeWorkers === 0) { finish(); return; }
          while (activeWorkers < CONCURRENCY && index < total) {
            const recipient = recipients[index++];
            activeWorkers++;
            updateStatus(`Processing: ${activeWorkers} active | ${total - index} pending`);
            
            processRecipient(recipient).finally(() => {
              activeWorkers--; completed++; updateProgress(completed, total); next();
            });
          }
        };
        next();
      }

      function processRecipient(recipient) {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler((res) => {
              if (res.skipped) {
                log(`<span class="skip-msg">⚠️ Skipped: ${recipient} (No Data)</span>`);
                resolve(); return;
              }
              // Save directly, no merge needed
              google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(() => {
                log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Saved: ${recipient}</span>`);
                resolve();
              }).saveSonstigesPdf(res.blobData, res.filename, res.folderId);
            })
            .withFailureHandler((err) => {
              log(`<span class="error-msg">❌ Server Error ${recipient}: ${err.message}</span>`);
              resolve();
            })
            .getSonstigesPdfData(recipient);
        });
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { const div = document.getElementById("log"); div.innerHTML += `<div class="log-item">${msg}</div>`; div.scrollTop = div.scrollHeight; }
      function updateProgress(current, total) { document.getElementById("bar").style.width = Math.round((current / total) * 100) + "%"; }
      function handleError(e) { log(`FATAL ERROR: ${e.message}`); }
      function finish() { document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none"; updateStatus("Batch Processing Complete!"); }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

/**
 * SERVER SIDE: ExportSonstigesGLEKINT
 * Generates batch reports for 'Sonstiges Food' filtered by GL-EK INT.
 * Uses the 'Mapping' sheet for recipients as per VBA Modul10.
 */

function openSonstigesGLEKINTDialog() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");
  
  if (!sheetExport) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // Fetch Dashboard Texts once
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
  } catch (e) {
    folderId = folderUrl; 
  }

  // Get KW explicitly from Sonstiges sheet (Cell N6) as per VBA
  const sonstigesSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen");
  const kwValue = sonstigesSheet ? sonstigesSheet.getRange("N6").getValue() : "XX";

  // Package layout data
  const layout = {
    htl: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header left"), 
    htc: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header center"), 
    htr: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen header right"),
    fbl: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer left"), 
    fbc: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer center"), 
    fbr: getDashboardText("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen footer right")
  };

  const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('ExportSonstigesGLEKINT_HTML');
  htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
    layout: layout, 
    folderId: folderId,
    kwValue: kwValue
  });
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(
    htmlTemplate.evaluate().setWidth(600).setHeight(500), 
    'Generating Sonstiges Reports (GL-EK INT)...'
  );
}

/**
 * STRICT VBA PARITY: Gets unique recipients from 'Mapping' Col J (Index 10)
 */
function getSonstigesIntRecipients() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Mapping");
  if (!sheet) throw new Error("Sheet 'Mapping' nicht gefunden.");
  
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return [];
  
  const data = sheet.getRange(2, 10, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues().flat();
  return [...new Set(data)].filter(String).sort();
}

/**
 * Server-side generation of Base PDF for a specific recipient
 */
function getSonstigesPdfDataForRecipient(recipient) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  const config = { 
    name: "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen", 
    filterCol: 4,     // Column D (GL-EK INT)
    headerRows: 6,    // Data starts at Row 7
    keepCols: 15      // Print Area A:O
  };

  const liveSheet = ss.getSheetByName(config.name);
  if (!liveSheet) return { skipped: true, recipient: recipient };

  const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
  const tempSheet = liveSheet.copyTo(ss);
  tempSheet.setName("Temp_Sonst_" + uniqueSuffix);
  const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
  tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

  try {
    const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
    if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

    const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
    if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

    // Filtering Logic
    let hasData = true;
    const lastRow = tempSheet.getLastRow();

    if (lastRow > config.headerRows) {
      const values = tempSheet.getRange(config.headerRows + 1, config.filterCol, lastRow - config.headerRows, 1).getValues().flat();
      const deleteRequests = [];
      let startDelete = -1;
      let dataCount = 0;

      for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
        // Bereinige Strings um Leerzeichen zu ignorieren
        const cellValue = String(values[i]).trim();
        const targetRecipient = String(recipient).trim();

        // NEUE LOGIK: Lösche die Zeile NUR, wenn sie nicht dem Empfänger gehört UND nicht leer ist.
        // Leerzeichen oder leere Strings ("") bleiben somit erhalten!
        if (cellValue !== targetRecipient && cellValue !== "") {
          if (startDelete === -1) startDelete = i;
        } else {
          // Behalte diese Zeile (gehört zum Empfänger oder ist leer)
          if (startDelete !== -1) {
            deleteRequests.push({ deleteDimension: { range: { sheetId: sheetId, dimension: "ROWS", startIndex: config.headerRows + startDelete, endIndex: config.headerRows + i } } });
            startDelete = -1;
          }
          dataCount++;
        }
      }
      if (startDelete !== -1) {
        deleteRequests.push({ deleteDimension: { range: { sheetId: sheetId, dimension: "ROWS", startIndex: config.headerRows + startDelete, endIndex: config.headerRows + values.length } } });
      }
      if (deleteRequests.length > 0) {
        deleteRequests.reverse();
        Sheets.Spreadsheets.batchUpdate({ requests: deleteRequests }, ss.getId());
      }
      
      // dataCount zählt jetzt sowohl Treffer als auch leere Zeilen.
      // Wenn dataCount 0 ist, gibt es Weder Treffer NOCH leere Zeilen.
      if (dataCount === 0) hasData = false;
    } else {
      hasData = false;
    }

    SpreadsheetApp.flush();

    // Skip if empty (no matches AND no blank lines)
    if (!hasData) {
      ss.deleteSheet(tempSheet);
      return { skipped: true, recipient: recipient };
    }

    // Fetch Base PDF (LANDSCAPE mode)
    const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
      `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}&size=A4&portrait=false&scale=2&gridlines=false` +
      `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
      `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

    const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token }, muteHttpExceptions: true });
    
    if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
      return {
        skipped: false,
        recipient: recipient,
        base64: Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes()),
        tempSheets: tempSheetIds
      };
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.error(e);
  }

  // Fallback cleanup
  if (ss.getSheetByName("Temp_Sonst_" + uniqueSuffix)) {
    ss.deleteSheet(ss.getSheetByName("Temp_Sonst_" + uniqueSuffix));
  }
  return { skipped: true, recipient: recipient };
}

function saveSonstigesPdfToDrive_batch(base64Data, filename, folderId, tempSheets) {
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId);
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  if (base64Data) {
    const decodedBytes = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(decodedBytes, 'application/pdf', filename);
    folder.createFile(blob);
  }

  // Cleanup temp sheets
  for (const ts of tempSheets) {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
    if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
  }

  return true;
}

ExportSonstigesGLEKINT_HTML.html
<!-- <!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/pdf-lib@1.17.1/dist/pdf-lib.min.js"></script>
    <style>
      body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
      .spinner { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #e74c3c; border-radius: 50%; width: 30px; height: 30px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 10px auto; }
      @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
      .progress-container { width: 100%; background-color: #ddd; margin-top: 20px; border-radius: 5px; }
      .progress-bar { width: 0%; height: 20px; background-color: #c0392b; border-radius: 5px; transition: width 0.3s; }
      .log { height: 250px; overflow-y: auto; background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px solid #ccc; margin-top: 15px; padding: 10px; text-align: left; font-size: 12px; font-family: monospace; }
      .log-item { margin-bottom: 4px; border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; }
      .skip-msg { color: #f39c12; font-weight: bold; }
      .ok-msg { color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; }
      .error-msg { color: #e74c3c; font-weight: bold; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h3>Generating Sonstiges Food Reports (GL-EK INT)</h3>
    <div id="loader" class="spinner"></div>
    <div id="status">Initializing...</div>
    <div class="progress-container"><div id="bar" class="progress-bar"></div></div>
    <div id="log" class="log"></div>

    <script>
      const CONCURRENCY = 5; 

      window.onload = function() { startBatchProcess(); };

      async function startBatchProcess() {
        log("Fetching recipients from Col D...");
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(runQueue).withFailureHandler(handleError).getSonstigesIntRecipients();
      }

      function runQueue(recipients) {
        log(`Found ${recipients.length} recipients. Starting queue...`);
        let index = 0; let activeWorkers = 0; let completed = 0;
        const total = recipients.length;

        if(total === 0) { finish(); return; }

        const next = () => {
          if (index >= total && activeWorkers === 0) { finish(); return; }
          while (activeWorkers < CONCURRENCY && index < total) {
            const recipient = recipients[index++];
            activeWorkers++;
            updateStatus(`Processing: ${activeWorkers} active | ${total - index} pending`);
            
            processRecipient(recipient).finally(() => {
              activeWorkers--; completed++; updateProgress(completed, total); next();
            });
          }
        };
        next();
      }

      function processRecipient(recipient) {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler((res) => {
              if (res.skipped) {
                log(`<span class="skip-msg">⚠️ Skipped: ${recipient} (No Data)</span>`);
                resolve(); return;
              }
              // Save directly
              google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(() => {
                log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Saved: ${recipient}</span>`);
                resolve();
              }).saveSonstigesIntPdf(res.blobData, res.filename, res.folderId);
            })
            .withFailureHandler((err) => {
              log(`<span class="error-msg">❌ Server Error ${recipient}: ${err.message}</span>`);
              resolve();
            })
            .getSonstigesIntPdf(recipient);
        });
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { const div = document.getElementById("log"); div.innerHTML += `<div class="log-item">${msg}</div>`; div.scrollTop = div.scrollHeight; }
      function updateProgress(current, total) { document.getElementById("bar").style.width = Math.round((current / total) * 100) + "%"; }
      function handleError(e) { log(`FATAL ERROR: ${e.message}`); }
      function finish() { document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none"; updateStatus("Batch Processing Complete!"); }
    </script>
  </body>
</html> -->


<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/pdf-lib/dist/pdf-lib.min.js"></script>
    <style>
      body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
      .spinner { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #e74c3c; border-radius: 50%; width: 30px; height: 30px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 10px auto; }
      @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
      .progress-container { width: 100%; background-color: #ddd; margin-top: 20px; border-radius: 5px; }
      .progress-bar { width: 0%; height: 20px; background-color: #c0392b; border-radius: 5px; transition: width 0.3s; }
      .log { height: 250px; overflow-y: auto; background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px solid #ccc; margin-top: 15px; padding: 10px; text-align: left; font-size: 12px; font-family: monospace; }
      .log-item { margin-bottom: 4px; border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; padding-bottom: 2px;}
      .ok-msg { color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; }
      .skip-msg { color: #f39c12; font-weight: bold; }
      .error-msg { color: #e74c3c; font-weight: bold; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h3>Generating Sonstiges Reports (GL-EK INT)</h3>
    <div id="loader" class="spinner"></div>
    <div id="status">Initializing...</div>
    <div class="progress-container"><div id="bar" class="progress-bar"></div></div>
    <div id="log" class="log"></div>

    <script>
      const payloadData = <?!= payload ?>;
      const { PDFDocument, StandardFonts, rgb } = PDFLib;
      const CONCURRENCY = 3; 

      window.onload = function() { startBatchProcess(); };

      async function startBatchProcess() {
        log("Fetching recipients from Mapping tab...");
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(runQueue)
          .withFailureHandler(handleError)
          .getSonstigesIntRecipients();
      }

      function sanitizeText(text) {
        if (!text) return "";
        return text.toString().normalize('NFC'); 
      }

      function base64ToUint8(base64) {
        const binary_string = window.atob(base64);
        const len = binary_string.length;
        const bytes = new Uint8Array(len);
        for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) { bytes[i] = binary_string.charCodeAt(i); }
        return bytes;
      }

      function uint8ToBase64(uint8) {
        let binary = '';
        for (let i = 0; i < uint8.byteLength; i++) { binary += String.fromCharCode(uint8[i]); }
        return window.btoa(binary);
      }

      async function runQueue(recipients) {
        log(`Found ${recipients.length} recipients. Starting processing...`);
        let index = 0;
        let activeWorkers = 0;
        let completed = 0;
        const total = recipients.length;

        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          const next = () => {
            if (index >= total && activeWorkers === 0) {
              finish();
              resolve();
              return;
            }

            while (activeWorkers < CONCURRENCY && index < total) {
              const recipient = recipients[index++];
              activeWorkers++;
              updateStatus(`Queue: ${activeWorkers} active | ${total - index} pending`);

              processSingleRecipient(recipient)
                .then((res) => {
                  if (res === "SKIPPED") {
                    log(`<span class="skip-msg">⚠️ Skipped: ${recipient} (No Data)</span>`);
                  } else {
                    log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Saved: ${recipient}</span>`);
                  }
                })
                .catch((err) => log(`<span class="error-msg">❌ Error ${recipient}: ${err.message}</span>`))
                .finally(() => {
                  activeWorkers--;
                  completed++;
                  updateProgress(completed, total);
                  next();
                });
            }
          };
          next();
        });
      }

      function processSingleRecipient(recipient) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(async (response) => {
              try {
                if (response.skipped) {
                  resolve("SKIPPED");
                  return;
                }

                // Since this is a single sheet, we can just load the base PDF directly
                const pdfBytes = base64ToUint8(response.base64);
                const pdfDoc = await PDFDocument.load(pdfBytes);
                
                const fontRegular = await pdfDoc.embedFont(StandardFonts.Helvetica);
                const fontBold = await pdfDoc.embedFont(StandardFonts.HelveticaBold);

                const pages = pdfDoc.getPages();

                for (let i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {
                  const page = pages[i];
                  const { width, height } = page.getSize(); 
                  const pageNumStr = (i + 1).toString();

                  const headerSize = 7.5; 
                  const centerSize = 12;  
                  const footerSize = 8;   
                  const xMargin = 30;             
                  const yTop = height - 20;     
                  const yBottom = 25;           

                  const regex = /\[PAGEA?\]|\[PAGE A\]/gi;
                  const htl = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.htl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const htc = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.htc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const htr = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.htr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const fbl = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.fbl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const fbc = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.fbc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                  const fbr = sanitizeText(payloadData.layout.fbr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);

                  const drawTextMultiline = (text, align, isHeader, startY, fontSize, textFont) => {
                    if (!text) return;
                    const lines = text.split('\n');
                    const lineHeight = fontSize * 1.25;
                    let currentY = isHeader ? startY : startY + ((lines.length - 1) * lineHeight);

                    lines.forEach(line => {
                      let xPos = xMargin; 
                      if (align === 'center') {
                        xPos = (width - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize)) / 2;
                      } else if (align === 'right') {
                        xPos = width - xMargin - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize);
                      }
                      page.drawText(line, { x: xPos, y: currentY, size: fontSize, font: textFont, color: rgb(0,0,0) });
                      currentY -= lineHeight; 
                    });
                  };

                  drawTextMultiline(htl, 'left',   true, yTop, headerSize, fontBold);
                  drawTextMultiline(htc, 'center', true, yTop - 15, centerSize, fontBold);
                  drawTextMultiline(htr, 'right',  true, yTop - 5, headerSize, fontBold);
                  drawTextMultiline(fbl, 'left',   false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                  drawTextMultiline(fbc, 'center', false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                  drawTextMultiline(fbr, 'right',  false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                }

                const finalPdfBytes = await pdfDoc.save();
                const finalBase64 = uint8ToBase64(finalPdfBytes);
                const finalFilename = `03_Statistik_Food_Sonstiges Food_${recipient}_KW${payloadData.kwValue}_INT.pdf`;

                google.script.run
                  .withSuccessHandler(resolve)
                  .withFailureHandler(reject)
                  .saveSonstigesPdfToDrive_batch(finalBase64, finalFilename, payloadData.folderId, response.tempSheets);

              } catch (err) {
                reject(err);
              }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(reject)
            .getSonstigesPdfDataForRecipient(recipient);
        });
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { 
        const div = document.getElementById("log"); 
        div.innerHTML += `<div class="log-item">${msg}</div>`; 
        div.scrollTop = div.scrollHeight; 
      }
      function updateProgress(current, total) { 
        document.getElementById("bar").style.width = Math.round((current / total) * 100) + "%"; 
      }
      function handleError(e) { log(`FATAL ERROR: ${e.message}`); }
      function finish() { 
        document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none"; 
        updateStatus("Batch Processing Complete! Cleaning up..."); 
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(() => { setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 2000); })
          .cleanUpOrphanedTempSheets();
      }
    </script>

                   await loadAndCopy(response.part2);
