    <script>
      const { PDFDocument } = PDFLib;
      
      // CONFIGURATION
      const CONCURRENCY = 3; // Number of simultaneous requests. Warning: >5 may crash Sheets.

      window.onload = function() {
        startBatchProcess();
      };

      async function startBatchProcess() {
        log("Fetching recipient list...");
        
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(runQueue)
          .withFailureHandler(handleError)
          .getGlekIntRecipients();
      }

      // --- PARALLEL QUEUE LOGIC ---
      async function runQueue(recipients) {
        log(`Found ${recipients.length} recipients. Starting parallel queue (${CONCURRENCY} threads)...`);
        
        let index = 0;
        let activeWorkers = 0;
        let completed = 0;
        const total = recipients.length;

        // Promise that resolves when all items are processed
        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          
          const next = () => {
            // Check if done
            if (index >= total && activeWorkers === 0) {
              finish();
              resolve();
              return;
            }

            // Start new workers if we have capacity and items left
            while (activeWorkers < CONCURRENCY && index < total) {
              const recipient = recipients[index++];
              activeWorkers++;
              
              updateStatus(`Queue: ${activeWorkers} active | ${total - index} pending`);

              processSingleRecipient(recipient)
                .then((res) => {
                  if (res === "SKIPPED") {
                    log(`<span class="skip-msg">⚠️ Skipped: ${recipient}</span>`);
                  } else {
                    log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Saved: ${recipient}</span>`);
                  }
                })
                .catch((err) => {
                  log(`<span class="error-msg">❌ Error ${recipient}: ${err.message}</span>`);
                })
                .finally(() => {
                  activeWorkers--;
                  completed++;
                  updateProgress(completed, total);
                  next(); // Trigger next item
                });
            }
          };

          // Start the loop
          next();
        });
      }

      function processSingleRecipient(recipient) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          // log(`> Starting: ${recipient}`); // Optional verbose log
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(async (response) => {
              try {
                if (response.skipped) {
                  resolve("SKIPPED");
                  return;
                }

                const mergedPdf = await PDFDocument.create();
                
                const loadAndCopy = async (base64) => {
                  if (!base64) return; 
                  const pdfSrc = await PDFDocument.load(base64);
                  const copiedPages = await mergedPdf.copyPages(pdfSrc, pdfSrc.getPageIndices());
                  copiedPages.forEach((page) => mergedPdf.addPage(page));
                };

                // Merge Order: Part 1 -> Part 3 -> Part 2
                if (response.part1) await loadAndCopy(response.part1);
                await loadAndCopy(response.part3); 
                if (response.part2) await loadAndCopy(response.part2);

                const mergedBytes = await mergedPdf.saveAsBase64();

                google.script.run
                  .withSuccessHandler(resolve)
                  .withFailureHandler(reject)
                  .saveMergedPdfToDrive(mergedBytes, response.filename, response.folderId);
                  
              } catch (err) {
                reject(err);
              }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(reject)
            .getPdfDataForRecipient(recipient);
        });
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { 
        const div = document.getElementById("log");

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/pdf-lib/dist/pdf-lib.min.js"></script>
    <style>
      body { font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
      .spinner { border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #2ecc71; border-radius: 50%; width: 30px; height: 30px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 10px auto; }
      @keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
      .progress-container { width: 100%; background-color: #ddd; margin-top: 20px; border-radius: 5px; }
      .progress-bar { width: 0%; height: 20px; background-color: #4CAF50; border-radius: 5px; transition: width 0.3s; }
      .log { height: 250px; overflow-y: auto; background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px solid #ccc; margin-top: 15px; padding: 10px; text-align: left; font-size: 12px; font-family: monospace; }
      .log-item { margin-bottom: 4px; border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; padding-bottom: 2px;}
      .ok-msg { color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; }
      .error-msg { color: #e74c3c; font-weight: bold; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h3>Generating GL-EK INT Reports</h3>
    <div id="loader" class="spinner"></div>
    <div id="status">Initializing...</div>
    <div class="progress-container"><div id="bar" class="progress-bar"></div></div>
    <div id="log" class="log"></div>

    <script>
      const payloadData = <?!= payload ?>;
      const { PDFDocument, StandardFonts, rgb } = PDFLib;
      const CONCURRENCY = 3; 

      window.onload = function() { startBatchProcess(); };

      async function startBatchProcess() {
        log("Fetching recipient list...");
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(runQueue)
          .withFailureHandler(handleError)
          .getGlekIntRecipients();
      }

      function sanitizeText(text) {
        if (!text) return "";
        return text.toString().normalize('NFC'); 
      }

      function base64ToUint8(base64) {
        const binary_string = window.atob(base64);
        const len = binary_string.length;
        const bytes = new Uint8Array(len);
        for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) { bytes[i] = binary_string.charCodeAt(i); }
        return bytes;
      }

      function uint8ToBase64(uint8) {
        let binary = '';
        for (let i = 0; i < uint8.byteLength; i++) { binary += String.fromCharCode(uint8[i]); }
        return window.btoa(binary);
      }

      async function runQueue(recipients) {
        log(`Found ${recipients.length} recipients. Starting processing...`);
        let index = 0;
        let activeWorkers = 0;
        let completed = 0;
        const total = recipients.length;

        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          const next = () => {
            if (index >= total && activeWorkers === 0) {
              finish();
              resolve();
              return;
            }

            while (activeWorkers < CONCURRENCY && index < total) {
              const recipient = recipients[index++];
              activeWorkers++;
              updateStatus(`Queue: ${activeWorkers} active | ${total - index} pending`);

              processSingleRecipient(recipient)
                .then(() => log(`<span class="ok-msg">✅ Saved: ${recipient}</span>`))
                .catch((err) => log(`<span class="error-msg">❌ Error ${recipient}: ${err.message}</span>`))
                .finally(() => {
                  activeWorkers--;
                  completed++;
                  updateProgress(completed, total);
                  next();
                });
            }
          };
          next();
        });
      }

      function processSingleRecipient(recipient) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(async (response) => {
              try {
                const masterPdf = await PDFDocument.create();
                let globalPageCounter = 1;

                for (const part of response.parts) {
                  const partPdfBytes = base64ToUint8(part.base64);
                  const partPdf = await PDFDocument.load(partPdfBytes);
                  
                  // Embed fonts directly into the part
                  const fontRegular = await partPdf.embedFont(StandardFonts.Helvetica);
                  const fontBold = await partPdf.embedFont(StandardFonts.HelveticaBold);

                  const pages = partPdf.getPages();
                  const layoutConfig = payloadData.layouts[part.id];

                  for (let i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {
                    const page = pages[i];
                    const { width, height } = page.getSize(); 
                    const pageNumStr = globalPageCounter.toString();

                    const headerSize = 7.5; 
                    const centerSize = 12;  
                    const footerSize = 8;   
                    const xMargin = 30;             
                    const yTop = height - 20;     
                    const yBottom = 25;           

                    const regex = /\[PAGEA?\]|\[PAGE A\]/gi;
                    const htl = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.htl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const htc = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.htc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const htr = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.htr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const fbl = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.fbl).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const fbc = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.fbc).replace(regex, pageNumStr);
                    const fbr = sanitizeText(layoutConfig.fbr).replace(regex, pageNumStr);

                    const drawTextMultiline = (text, align, isHeader, startY, fontSize, textFont) => {
                      if (!text) return;
                      const lines = text.split('\n');
                      const lineHeight = fontSize * 1.25;
                      let currentY = isHeader ? startY : startY + ((lines.length - 1) * lineHeight);

                      lines.forEach(line => {
                        let xPos = xMargin; 
                        if (align === 'center') {
                          xPos = (width - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize)) / 2;
                        } else if (align === 'right') {
                          xPos = width - xMargin - textFont.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize);
                        }
                        page.drawText(line, { x: xPos, y: currentY, size: fontSize, font: textFont, color: rgb(0,0,0) });
                        currentY -= lineHeight; 
                      });
                    };

                    drawTextMultiline(htl, 'left',   true, yTop, headerSize, fontBold);
                    drawTextMultiline(htc, 'center', true, yTop - 15, centerSize, fontBold);
                    drawTextMultiline(htr, 'right',  true, yTop - 5, headerSize, fontBold);
                    drawTextMultiline(fbl, 'left',   false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                    drawTextMultiline(fbc, 'center', false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);
                    drawTextMultiline(fbr, 'right',  false, yBottom, footerSize, fontRegular);

                    globalPageCounter++;
                  }

                  const copiedPages = await masterPdf.copyPages(partPdf, partPdf.getPageIndices());
                  copiedPages.forEach((p) => masterPdf.addPage(p));
                }

                const finalPdfBytes = await masterPdf.save();
                const finalBase64 = uint8ToBase64(finalPdfBytes);
                const finalFilename = `02_Statistik_Food_Sortimentswünsche_KW${payloadData.kwValue}_DE_${recipient}.pdf`;

                google.script.run
                  .withSuccessHandler(resolve)
                  .withFailureHandler(reject)
                  .saveMergedPdfToDrive_batch(finalBase64, finalFilename, payloadData.folderId, response.tempSheets);

              } catch (err) {
                reject(err);
              }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(reject)
            .getPdfDataForRecipient(recipient);
        });
      }

      function updateStatus(msg) { document.getElementById("status").innerText = msg; }
      function log(msg) { 
        const div = document.getElementById("log"); 
        div.innerHTML += `<div class="log-item">${msg}</div>`; 
        div.scrollTop = div.scrollHeight; 
      }
      function updateProgress(current, total) { 
        document.getElementById("bar").style.width = Math.round((current / total) * 100) + "%"; 
      }
      function handleError(e) { log(`FATAL ERROR: ${e.message}`); }
      function finish() { 
        document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none"; 
        updateStatus("Batch Processing Complete! Cleaning up..."); 
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(() => { setTimeout(() => google.script.host.close(), 2000); })
          .cleanUpOrphanedTempSheets();
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
Food Sortimentswünsche.gs
/**
 * Imports and processes data from 'Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche' to 'Food Sortimentswünsche'.
 * V4: Fixes "setFormulasR1C1" parameter error by correctly building a 2D array of formulas.
 * This version preserves all formatting and correctly applies all logic.
 */
function importToFoodAssortmentWishes() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sourceSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche");
  const destSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Food Sortimentswünsche");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importToFoodAssortmentWishes (V4 - Correct R1C1 Usage) ---");

  if (!sourceSheet || !destSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find the source ("Rohdaten...") or destination ("Food Sortimentswünsche") sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  const sourceLastRow = sourceSheet.getLastRow();
  if (sourceLastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'The "Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche" sheet has no data to import.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process on the source sheet.');
    return;
  }

  try {
    // --- 1. Clear Old Data Content ---
    const destLastRow = destSheet.getLastRow();
    if (destLastRow >= 6) {
      Logger.log(`Clearing old content from A6:R${destLastRow} in 'Food Sortimentswünsche'.`);
      destSheet.getRange("A6:R" + destLastRow).clearContent();
    }

    // --- 2. Read, Re-order, and De-duplicate Data in Memory ---
    Logger.log("Reading source data...");
    const sourceRange = sourceSheet.getRange("A8:H" + sourceLastRow);
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();

    const uniqueArtikels = new Set();
    const processedData = [];

    Logger.log("Processing and de-duplicating data...");
    for (const row of sourceValues) {
      const artikelNummer = row[4]; // Column E (Artikelnummer)
      
      if (!uniqueArtikels.has(artikelNummer)) {
        processedData.push([
          row[0], // Column A -> A
          row[1], // Column B -> B
          row[2], // Column C -> C
          row[3], // Column D -> D
          row[5], // Column F -> E
          row[4], // Column E -> F (The key for de-duplication)
          row[7], // Column H -> G
        ]);
        uniqueArtikels.add(artikelNummer);
      }
    }
    Logger.log(`Finished processing. Found ${processedData.length} unique rows.`);
    
    if (processedData.length === 0) {
        ui.alert('No Data', 'No unique data rows were found to import.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        return;
    }

    // --- 3. Write Processed Data to Destination ---
    Logger.log("Writing processed data to 'Food Sortimentswünsche' sheet (A:G).");
    destSheet.getRange(6, 1, processedData.length, 7).setValues(processedData);
    
    const newLastRow = 5 + processedData.length;

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas using a Format-Preserving Method (Corrected) ---
    Logger.log(`Applying formulas from H3:R3 to H6:R${newLastRow} using R1C1 notation.`);
    const formulaTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("H3:R3");
    const templateFormulas = formulaTemplateRange.getFormulasR1C1()[0]; // Get the 1D array of formula strings

    if (templateFormulas.join('').length > 0) {
        const numRows = newLastRow - 5;
        const formulasForRange = [];
        // Build a 2D array by repeating the template row for each destination row
        for (let i = 0; i < numRows; i++) {
            formulasForRange.push(templateFormulas);
        }
        
        const formulaDestinationRange = destSheet.getRange("H6:R" + newLastRow);
        // setFormulasR1C1 expects a 2D array matching the range dimensions. This is now correct.
        formulaDestinationRange.setFormulasR1C1(formulasForRange);
    } else {
        Logger.log("Warning: No formulas found in template range H3:R3.");
    }
    
    // --- 5. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(5000);

    Logger.log(`Converting formulas in H6:R${newLastRow} to static values.`);
    const rangeToConvert = destSheet.getRange("H6:R" + newLastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 6. Apply Formatting (Mimicking VBA) ---
    // Although setFormulasR1C1 preserves format, the VBA explicitly reapplies it.
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from template row A6:R6 to all new rows.");
    const formatTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:R6");
    if (newLastRow > 6) {
        const formatDestination = destSheet.getRange("A7:R" + newLastRow);
        formatTemplateRange.copyTo(formatDestination, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
    }

    // --- 7. Sort the Data ---
    Logger.log("Sorting the data...");
    const fullDataRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:R" + newLastRow);
    
    fullDataRange.sort({ column: 7, ascending: true }); // First sort: by Column G
    fullDataRange.sort([ // Second sort: multi-level
        { column: 1, ascending: true },
        { column: 2, ascending: true },
        { column: 3, ascending: true }
    ]);

    // --- 8. Cleanup: Lösche alles unterhalb der deduplizierten Daten ---
    const maxRows = destSheet.getMaxRows();
    if (maxRows > newLastRow) {
        // Löscht alles ab der ersten leeren Zeile bis ganz unten. 
        // Spalten A bis R = 18 Spalten
        destSheet.getRange(newLastRow + 1, 1, maxRows - newLastRow, 18).clear();
        Logger.log(`Tabelle von Zeile ${newLastRow + 1} bis ${maxRows} komplett gesäubert.`);
    }

    // --- Abschluss ---
    destSheet.getRange("E2").activate();
    navigateOnSuccess();
    Logger.log("--- Finished importToFoodAssortmentWishes ---");

  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
}
GENERATE_DATA_OG_SONSTIGES.gs


/**
 * ⚙️ Generates processed data for 'O+G Sonstiges'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'OGSonstigesDatenGenerieren' (Modul38).
 *
 * This script FIRST sets a new user-defined formula in the template row C4:J4,
 * THEN sorts, de-duplicates, copies/autofills all template formulas (B4:K4) down,
 * converts to values, sorts, and formats.
 */
function generateOGOtherData() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  Logger.log("--- Starting generateOGOtherData ---");

  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Sonstiges");
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen"); // Needed for formula

  if (!targetSheet || !settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "O+G Sonstiges" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row (for the formula) ---
  // This is a guess; change "searchFileName" if the formula uses a different file
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_O+G_DE_Sonstiges"; 
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; 
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
        return;
      }
      break; 
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  
  // Find last row based on Column A ("Grund") as per VBA
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getRange("A" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
  Logger.log(`Last row with data found in column A is: ${lastRow}`);
  if (lastRow < 7) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'No imported data found in Column A (rows 7 or below) to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 6.');
    return;
  }

  try {

    // --- 2. De-duplicate Data (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log(`De-duplicating range A7:K${lastRow} based on Column A.`);
    const dataRange = targetSheet.getRange("A7:K" + lastRow);
    dataRange.removeDuplicates([1]); // Column A is the 1st column in this range

    const newLastRow = targetSheet.getRange("A" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
    Logger.log(`New last row after de-duplication is: ${newLastRow}`);
    
    if (newLastRow < 7) {
        Logger.log("No data remaining after de-duplication.");
        return;
    }

    // --- 3. SET TEMPLATE FORMULA (User Request) ---
    Logger.log("Setting user-defined formula in template row C4:J4...");

    const formulaForC4 = `=IFERROR(IF(IF(C$3=C$2;INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$O$100");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$100");0);MATCH(C$3;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$K$1");0));IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$O$100");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$100");0);MATCH(C$3;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$K$1");0)));0)+IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$O$100");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$100");0);MATCH(C$2;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$K$1");0)));0))=0;"";IF(C$3=C$2;INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$O$100");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$100");0);MATCH(C$3;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$K$1");0));IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$O$100");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$100");0);MATCH(C$3;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$K$1");0)));0)+IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$O$100");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$100");0);MATCH(C$2;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$K$1");0)));0)));"")`; // <<< PASTE YOUR FORMULA HERE

    if (formulaForC4 === `=""`) {
      Logger.log("Formula for C4 is blank. Please edit the script and paste your formula.");
      // You can uncomment the lines below to force an error if the formula is missing.
      // ui.alert("Script Error", "The formula for C4 is missing in the script.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      // return;
    }

    const templateFormulaCell = targetSheet.getRange("C4");
    if (formulaForC4 !== `=""`) { // Only set formula if it's not blank
      templateFormulaCell.setFormula(formulaForC4);
    
      // Autofill it across to J4 (as per user request)
      const templateRangeCtoJ = targetSheet.getRange("C4:J4");
      templateFormulaCell.autoFill(templateRangeCtoJ, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      Logger.log("Template formula set for C4:J4.");
    } else {
      Logger.log("Skipping template formula set for C4:J4 as it was blank.");
    }
    
    // --- 4. Clear Formula Columns (as per VBA's copy/paste) ---
    Logger.log("Clearing target columns B:K...");
    // Clear all formula columns from row 7 down to be safe
    targetSheet.getRange("B7:K" + newLastRow).clearContent();

    // --- 5. Apply Formulas from Template Row 4 (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Copying full template row B4:K4 to B7...");
    const formulaTemplateRange = targetSheet.getRange("B4:K4"); // B:K (10 columns)
    const formulaStartRow = targetSheet.getRange("B7");
    formulaTemplateRange.copyTo(formulaStartRow, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);

    // --- 6. Autofill Formula Columns ---
    Logger.log("Autofilling formula columns down to row " + newLastRow);
    const rangeB7toK7 = targetSheet.getRange("B7:K7");

    if (newLastRow > 7) { // VBA: lr > 7
      // Autofill B:K
      rangeB7toK7.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("B7:K" + newLastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }
    
    // --- 7. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for all formulas to calculate...");
    ss.toast("Waiting for formulas to calculate, please wait 15s", "Calculating", 15);
    Utilities.sleep(15000); // Allow time for IMPORTRANGE

    Logger.log("Converting formulas in B7:K" + newLastRow + " to static values.");
    const rangeToConvert = targetSheet.getRange("B7:K" + newLastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 8. Apply Formatting (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from template row A7:K7 to all data rows.");
    const formatTemplateRow = targetSheet.getRange("A7:K7"); // VBA uses A7 as template
    const formatDestination = targetSheet.getRange("A7:K" + newLastRow);
    formatTemplateRow.copyTo(formatDestination, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);

    // --- 9. Sort Data ---
    // FIX: Nutze newLastRow anstatt lastRow, damit keine leeren Zeilen mitsortiert werden!
    Logger.log("Sorting data range A7:K" + newLastRow + " by Column A...");
    const sortRange = targetSheet.getRange("A7:K" + newLastRow); 
    sortRange.sort({ column: 1, ascending: true }); // Sort by Column A

    // --- 10. Cleanup: Lösche alles unterhalb der deduplizierten Daten ---
    const maxRows = targetSheet.getMaxRows();
    if (maxRows > newLastRow) {
        // Löscht alles ab der ersten leeren Zeile bis ganz unten (Spalten A bis K = 11 Spalten)
        targetSheet.getRange(newLastRow + 1, 1, maxRows - newLastRow, 11).clear();
        Logger.log(`Tabelle von Zeile ${newLastRow + 1} bis ${maxRows} komplett gesäubert.`);
    }

    // --- 11. Display Appropriate Message ---
    targetSheet.getRange("A1").activate(); // As per VBA
    navigateOnSuccess();
    
    // Optional: Activate next sheet
    // const nextSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Sonstiges");
    // if (nextSheet) nextSheet.activate();

  } catch (e) {
    const processingError = `An error occurred while generating data: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', processingError, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR during processing: ${e.stack}`);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log("--- Finished generateOGOtherData ---");
}

GENERATE_DATA_OG_Sortimentswunche.gs
/**
 * ⚙️ Generates processed data for 'O+G Sortimentswünsche'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'OGSortimentswünscheDatenGenerieren' (Modul36).
 *
 * This script FIRST sets a new user-defined formula in the template row C4:J4,
 * THEN de-duplicates, copies/autofills all template formulas (B4:K4) down,
 * converts to values, sorts, and formats.
 */
function generateOGAssortmentWishesData() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  Logger.log("--- Starting generateOGAssortmentWishesData ---");

  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Sortimentswünsche");
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen"); // Needed for formula

  if (!targetSheet || !settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "O+G Sortimentswünsche" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row (for the formula) ---
  // This is a guess based on your request; adjust if the formula uses a different file
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_O+G_DE_Sortimentswünsche"; 
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; 
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
        return;
      }
      break; 
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  
  // Find last row based on Column A ("Grund") as per VBA
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getRange("A" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
  Logger.log(`Last row with data found in column A is: ${lastRow}`);
  if (lastRow < 7) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'No imported data found in Column A (rows 7 or below) to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 6.');
    return;
  }

  try {
    // --- 2. De-duplicate Data (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log(`De-duplicating range A7:K${lastRow} based on Column A.`);
    const dataRange = targetSheet.getRange("A7:K" + lastRow);
    dataRange.removeDuplicates([1]); // Column A is the 1st column in this range

    const newLastRow = targetSheet.getRange("A" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
    Logger.log(`New last row after de-duplication is: ${newLastRow}`);
    
    if (newLastRow < 7) {
        Logger.log("No data remaining after de-duplication.");
        return;
    }

    // --- 3. SET TEMPLATE FORMULA (User Request) ---
    Logger.log("Setting user-defined formula in template row C4:J4...");

    // !!! PASTE YOUR FORMULA FOR CELL C4 HERE, using semicolons for EU locale !!!
    // It should reference $A7 (for autofill) and use 'foundRowNumber' or 'sourceFileId'.
    // Example: `="=IFERROR(VLOOKUP($A7; IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};...); 2; 0))"`
    const formulaForC4 = `=IFERROR(IF(IF(C$3=C$2;INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$M$1000");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$1000");0);MATCH(C$3;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$M$1");0));IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$M$1000");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$1000");0);MATCH(C$3;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$M$1");0)));0)+IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$M$1000");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$1000");0);MATCH(C$2;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$M$1");0)));0))=0;"";IF(C$3=C$2;INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$M$1000");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$1000");0);MATCH(C$3;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$M$1");0));IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$M$1000");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$1000");0);MATCH(C$3;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$M$1");0)));0)+IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$M$1000");MATCH($A4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$1000");0);MATCH(C$2;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$M$1");0)));0)));"")`; // <<< PASTE YOUR FORMULA HERE

    if (formulaForC4 === `=""`) {
      Logger.log("Formula for C4 is blank. Please edit the script and paste your formula.");
      // ui.alert("Script Error", "The formula for C4 is missing in the script.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      // return;
    }

    const templateFormulaCell = targetSheet.getRange("C4");
    if (formulaForC4 !== `=""`) { // Only set formula if it's not blank
      templateFormulaCell.setFormula(formulaForC4);
    
      // Autofill it across to J4 (as per user request)
      const templateRangeCtoJ = targetSheet.getRange("C4:J4");
      templateFormulaCell.autoFill(templateRangeCtoJ, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      Logger.log("Template formula set for C4:J4.");
    } else {
      Logger.log("Skipping template formula set for C4:J4 as it was blank.");
    }
    
    // --- 4. Clear Formula Columns (as per VBA's copy/paste) ---
    // VBA copies B4:K4 to B7, so we clear B8:K<newLastRow>
    Logger.log("Clearing target columns B:K...");
    if (newLastRow >= 8) { // Only clear if there are rows below 7
      targetSheet.getRange("B8:K" + newLastRow).clearContent();
    }

    // --- 5. Apply Formulas from Template Row 4 (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Copying full template row B4:K4 to B7...");
    const formulaTemplateRange = targetSheet.getRange("B4:K4");
    const formulaStartRow = targetSheet.getRange("B7");
    formulaTemplateRange.copyTo(formulaStartRow, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);

    // --- 6. Autofill Formula Columns ---
    Logger.log("Autofilling formula columns down to row " + newLastRow);
    const rangeB7toK7 = targetSheet.getRange("B7:K7");

    if (newLastRow > 7) { // VBA: lr > 7
      // Autofill B:K
      rangeB7toK7.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("B7:K" + newLastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }
    
    // --- 7. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for all formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(10000); // Allow time for IMPORTRANGE

    Logger.log("Converting formulas in B7:K" + newLastRow + " to static values.");
    const rangeToConvert = targetSheet.getRange("B7:K" + newLastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 8. Apply Formatting (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from template row A7:K7 to all data rows.");
    const formatTemplateRow = targetSheet.getRange("A7:K7"); // VBA uses A7 as template
    const formatDestination = targetSheet.getRange("A7:K" + newLastRow);
    formatTemplateRow.copyTo(formatDestination, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);

    // --- 9. Sort the Data (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Sorting the data (A6:K)...");
    const sortRange = targetSheet.getRange("A6:K" + newLastRow); // VBA sorts from Row 6
    sortRange.sort({ column: 1, ascending: true }); // Sort by Column A

    // --- 10. Cleanup: Lösche alles unterhalb der formatierten/sortierten Daten ---
    const maxRows = targetSheet.getMaxRows();
    if (maxRows > newLastRow) {
        // Löscht alles ab der ersten leeren Zeile bis ganz unten. 
        // Spalten A bis K = 11 Spalten
        targetSheet.getRange(newLastRow + 1, 1, maxRows - newLastRow, 11).clear();
        Logger.log(`Tabelle von Zeile ${newLastRow + 1} bis ${maxRows} komplett gesäubert.`);
    }

    // --- 11. Display Appropriate Message ---
    targetSheet.getRange("A1").activate(); // As per VBA
    navigateOnSuccess();
    
    // Optional: Activate next sheet
    // const nextSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Sonstiges");
    // if (nextSheet) nextSheet.activate();

  } catch (e) {
    const processingError = `An error occurred while generating data: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', processingError, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR during processing: ${e.stack}`);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log("--- Finished generateOGAssortmentWishesData ---");
}

GENERATE_DATA_ROHDATEN_OG_QUALITATSFALLE.gs
/**
 * ⚙️ Generates processed data for 'Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsfälle'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'RohdatenOGQualitätsfälleFormelnKopieren' (Modul40).
 *
 * This script FIRST sets a new user-defined formula in the template row H6:O6,
 * THEN copies/autofills all template formulas (A6:Q6) down,
 * and finally converts all results to static values.
 */
function generateRawOGQualityCases() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  Logger.log("--- Starting generateRawOGQualityCases ---");

  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsfälle");
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen"); // Needed for formula

  if (!targetSheet || !settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsfälle" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row (for the formula) ---
  ss.toast("Executing Step 1", "1", 3);
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_O+G_DE_Qualitätsfälle"; // As defined in Modul39
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; 
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
        return;
      }
      break; 
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  
  // Find last row based on Column E (Artikel) as per VBA
  const columnEValues = targetSheet.getRange("E1:E" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let lastRow = 0;
  for (let i = columnEValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (String(columnEValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      lastRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  Logger.log(`Last row with data found in column E is: ${lastRow}`);
  if (lastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'No imported data found in Column E (rows 8 or below) to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 7.');
    return;
  }

  ss.toast("Executing Step 2", "2", 3);
  try {
    // --- 2. SET TEMPLATE FORMULA (User Request) ---
    Logger.log("Setting user-defined formula in template row H6:O6...");

    const formulaForH6 = `=ARRAY_CONSTRAIN(ARRAYFORMULA(IFERROR(IF(H$5<>H$4;(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$3:$O$500");XMATCH(1;($B6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$500"))*($D6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$500"))*($E6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$D$3:$D$500"))*($F6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$E$500"))*($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$F$3:$F$500")));XMATCH(H$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$1:$O$1"))))+(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$3:$O$500");XMATCH(1;($B6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$500"))*($D6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$500"))*($E6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$D$3:$D$500"))*($F6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$E$500"))*($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$F$3:$F$500")));XMATCH(H$4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$1:$O$1"))));INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$3:$O$500");XMATCH(1;($B6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$500"))*($D6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$500"))*($E6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$D$3:$D$500"))*($F6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$E$500"))*($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$F$3:$F$500")));XMATCH(H$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$1:$O$1"))));"")); 1; 1)`; // <<< PASTE YOUR FORMULA HERE

    if (formulaForH6 === `=""`) {
      Logger.log("Formula for H6 is blank. Please edit the script and paste your formula.");
      // You can uncomment the lines below to force an error if the formula is missing.
      // ui.alert("Script Error", "The formula for H6 is missing in the script.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      // return;
    }

    const templateFormulaCell = targetSheet.getRange("H6");
    if (formulaForH6 !== `=""`) { // Only set formula if it's not blank
      templateFormulaCell.setFormula(formulaForH6);
    
      // Autofill it across to O6 (as per user request H,I,J,K,L,M,N,O)
      const templateRangeHtoO = targetSheet.getRange("H6:O6");
      templateFormulaCell.autoFill(templateRangeHtoO, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      Logger.log("Template formula set for H6:O6.");
    } else {
      Logger.log("Skipping template formula set for H6:O6 as it was blank.");
    }

    // --- 3. Clear Specific Columns (as per VBA) ---
    ss.toast("Executing Step 3", "3", 3);
    Logger.log("Clearing target columns A and H:Q...");
    targetSheet.getRange("A8:A" + lastRow).clearContent();
    targetSheet.getRange("H8:Q" + lastRow).clearContent();

    // // --- 4. Apply Formulas from Template Row 6 (as per VBA) ---
    // ss.toast("Executing Step 4", "4", 3);
    // Logger.log("Copying full template row A6:Q6 to A8...");
    // const formulaTemplateRange = targetSheet.getRange("A6:Q6"); // A:Q (17 columns)
    // const formulaStartRow = targetSheet.getRange("A8");
    // formulaTemplateRange.copyTo(formulaStartRow, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);
    // ss.toast("Step 4 copy formulas executing, give it 10s");
    // Utilities.sleep(10000); // Allow time for IMPORTRANGE


    // // --- 5. Autofill Formula Columns ---
    // ss.toast("Executing Step 5", "5", 3);
    // Logger.log("Autofilling formula columns down to row " + lastRow);
    // const rangeA8 = targetSheet.getRange("A8");
    // const rangeH8toQ8 = targetSheet.getRange("H8:Q8");

    // if (lastRow > 8) {
    //   // Autofill A
    //   rangeA8.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("A8:A" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    //   // Autofill H:Q
    //   rangeH8toQ8.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("H8:Q" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    // }

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas from Template Row 6 ---
    ss.toast("Executing Step 4", "4", 3);
    Logger.log("Copying specific template formulas (A6 and H6:Q6) to Row 8...");

    // Handle Column A
    const templateA6 = targetSheet.getRange("A6");
    const targetA8 = targetSheet.getRange("A8");
    templateA6.copyTo(targetA8, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);

    // Handle Columns H through Q
    const templateH6Q6 = targetSheet.getRange("H6:Q6");
    const targetH8Q8 = targetSheet.getRange("H8:Q8");
    templateH6Q6.copyTo(targetH8Q8, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);

    // --- 5. Autofill Formula Columns ---
    ss.toast("Executing Step 5", "5", 3);
    Logger.log("Autofilling formula columns down to row " + lastRow);

    if (lastRow > 8) {
      // Autofill Column A
      targetA8.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("A8:A" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      
      // Autofill Columns H through Q
      targetH8Q8.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("H8:Q" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }

    // --- 6. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    ss.toast("Executing Step 6", "6", 3);
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for all formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(10000); // Allow time for IMPORTRANGE

    Logger.log("Converting formulas in A8:Q" + lastRow + " to static values.");
    const rangeToConvert = targetSheet.getRange("A8:Q" + lastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 7. Check for Warnings (None in VBA for this macro) ---
    // VBA Modul40 does not have a warning check.

    // --- 8. Display Appropriate Message ---
    targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate(); // As per VBA
    navigateOnSuccess();
    
    // Optional: Activate next sheet
    // const nextSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Qualitätsfälle");
    // if (nextSheet) nextSheet.activate();

  } catch (e) {
    const processingError = `An error occurred while generating data: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', processingError, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR during processing: ${e.stack}`);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log("--- Finished generateRawOGQualityCases ---");
}

GENERATE_DATA_Rohdaten Allg. Sortimentsw..gs

/**
 * ⚙️ Generates processed data for General Assortment Wishes ('Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche').
 * V2: Implements the correct complex lookup formula for C:K, uses dynamic source ID,
 * preserves original formatting, and performs all steps as per VBA logic.
 */
function generateRawGeneralAssortmentData() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  Logger.log("--- Starting generateRawGeneralAssortmentData (V2 - Correct Formula & Formatting) ---");

  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Allg. Sortimentsw.");
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");

  if (!targetSheet || !settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Rohdaten Allg. Sortimentsw." sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: Target or Settings sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // Find last row based on Column B (imported data) as per VBA
  const columnBValues = targetSheet.getRange("B1:B" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let lastRow = 0;
  for (let i = columnBValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (String(columnBValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      lastRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  Logger.log(`Last row with data found in column B is: ${lastRow}`);
  if (lastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'No imported data found in Column B (rows 8 or below) to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 7.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID for the Formulas ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  // --- CHANGE: Use the correct source file name for this sheet's formulas ---
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche"; 
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' };
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileUrl) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file URL for "${searchFileName}" used by the formulas. Check 'Einstellungen'.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File URL for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found source file URL for formulas on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
  
  try {
    const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
    if (match && match[1]) {
      sourceFileId = match[1]; 
      Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID for formulas: ${sourceFileId}`);
    } else {
      throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
    }
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
    return;
  }
  
  // Define sheet name used in IMPORTRANGE within the formula
  const formulaSheetName = 'In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F'; 

  try {
    // --- 2. Clear Specific Columns ---
    Logger.log("Clearing target columns A and C:K...");
    targetSheet.getRange("A8:A" + lastRow).clearContent();
    targetSheet.getRange("C8:K" + lastRow).clearContent();

    // --- 3. Apply Formulas ---
    Logger.log("Applying formulas from template row 6 to A8:A and C8:K...");
    
    // Apply formula for Column A
    const formulaStartRangeA = targetSheet.getRange("A8");
    targetSheet.getRange("A6").copyTo(formulaStartRangeA); // Copy A6 to A8 first
    if(lastRow > 8) {
      formulaStartRangeA.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("A8:A" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }

    // --- NEW: Apply the complex formula for C8:K ---
    // Construct the formula dynamically using the extracted sourceFileId
    // Based on the user-provided formula for C6, adapted for C8 and EU locale (semicolons)
    const newFormulaForC8 = `=IFERROR(IF(C$5=C$4;INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!B3:Q500");MATCH($B8;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!A3:A500");0);MATCH(C$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!B1:Q1");0));IFERROR(VALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!B3:Q500");MATCH($B8;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!A3:A500");0);MATCH(C$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!B1:Q1");0)));0)+IFERROR(VALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!B3:Q500");MATCH($B8;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!A3:A500");0);MATCH(C$4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!B1:Q1");0)));0));"")`;

    Logger.log(`Generated formula for C8: ${newFormulaForC8}`);
    targetSheet.getRange("C8").setFormula(newFormulaForC8);

    // Autofill across C8:K8 first
    const firstDataRowRangeCJ = targetSheet.getRange("C8:J8");
    targetSheet.getRange("C8").autoFill(firstDataRowRangeCJ, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);

    const formulaStartRangeK = targetSheet.getRange("K8");
    targetSheet.getRange("K6").copyTo(formulaStartRangeK); // Copy K6 to K8 first
    
    const firstDataRowRangeCK = targetSheet.getRange("C8:K8");

    // Autofill down C8:K<lastRow>
    if(lastRow > 8) {
       firstDataRowRangeCK.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("C8:K" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }


    // --- 4. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for all formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(10000); // Allow time for IMPORTRANGE calculations

    Logger.log("Converting formulas in A8:K" + lastRow + " to static values.");
    const rangeToConvert = targetSheet.getRange("A8:K" + lastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 5. Check for Warnings ('-' in Column A) ---
    Logger.log("Checking for '-' warnings in Column A...");
    const columnAValues = targetSheet.getRange("A8:A" + lastRow).getValues();
    let warningFound = false;
    for (let i = 0; i < columnAValues.length; i++) {
      if (columnAValues[i][0] === "-") {
        warningFound = true;
        Logger.log(`Warning: Found '-' in cell A${8 + i}`);
        // Consider highlighting the cell here if needed
        // targetSheet.getRange(8 + i, 1).setBackground("#f4cccc"); // Example: Light red
      }
    }
    
    // --- Step 6: Apply Formatting REMOVED to preserve original formats ---
    Logger.log("Original formatting preserved.");


    // --- 7. Display Appropriate Message ---
    targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate(); // As per VBA
    if (warningFound) {
      Logger.log("Warning message triggered due to '-' found in Column A.");
      ss.toast('WARNUNG: Für einige Datensätze fehlt die Deutsche Übersetzung zum Grund (siehe Spalte A). Bitte trage die Werte manuell ein und ergänze das "Mapping".', "Achtung!", 15); 
    } else {
       navigateOnSuccess();
      // Optional: Activate the next sheet
      // const nextSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche");
      // if (nextSheet) nextSheet.activate();
    }

  } catch (e) {
    const processingError = `An error occurred while generating data: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', processingError, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR during processing: ${e.stack}`);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log("--- Finished generateRawGeneralAssortmentData ---");
}

GENERATE_DATA_Rohdaten Food Qualitätsfälle.gs
/**
 * ⚙️ Generates processed data for 'Rohdaten Food Qualitätsfälle'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'RohdatenFoodQualitätsfälleFormelnKopieren' (Modul33).
 *
 * This script FIRST sets a new user-defined formula in the template row O6:V6,
 * THEN copies/autofills all template formulas (A:Y) down,
 * and finally converts all results to static values.
 */
function generateRawFoodQualityCases() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  Logger.log("--- Starting generateRawFoodQualityCases ---");

  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Food Qualitätsfälle");
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen"); // Needed for formula

  if (!targetSheet || !settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Rohdaten Food Qualitätsfälle" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row (for the formula) ---
  // Assuming the formula needs the same file as the import
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Qualitätsfälle"; 
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; 
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
        return;
      }
      break; 
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  
  // Find last row based on Column K ("LFN") as per VBA
  const columnKValues = targetSheet.getRange("K1:K" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let lastRow = 0;
  for (let i = columnKValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (String(columnKValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      lastRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  Logger.log(`Last row with data found in column K is: ${lastRow}`);
  if (lastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'No imported data found in Column K (rows 8 or below) to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 7.');
    return;
  }

  try {
    // --- 2. SET TEMPLATE FORMULA (User Request) ---
    Logger.log("Setting user-defined formula in template row O6:V6...");

    // !!! PASTE YOUR FORMULA FOR CELL O6 HERE, using semicolons for EU locale !!!
    // It should reference $G6, $H6, etc. and the 'sourceFileId' variable.
    const formulaForO6 = `=ARRAY_CONSTRAIN(ARRAYFORMULA(IFERROR(IF(O$5=O$4;INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$I$3:$T$1000");MATCH(1;($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$1000"))*($H6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$B$1000"))*($I6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$1000"))*($J6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$D$3:$D$1000"))*($K6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$E$1000"))*($L6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$F$3:$F$1000"))*($M6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$3:$G$1000"))*($N6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$H$3:$H$1000"));0);MATCH(O$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$I$1:$T$1");0));IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$I$3:$T$1000");MATCH(1;($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$1000"))*($H6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$B$1000"))*($I6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$1000"))*($J6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$D$3:$D$1000"))*($K6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$E$1000"))*($L6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$F$3:$F$1000"))*($M6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$3:$G$1000"))*($N6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$H$3:$H$1000"));0);MATCH(O$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$I$1:$T$1");0)));0)+IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$I$3:$T$1000");MATCH(1;($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$1000"))*($H6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$B$1000"))*($I6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$1000"))*($J6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$D$3:$D$1000"))*($K6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$E$1000"))*($L6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$F$3:$F$1000"))*($M6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$3:$G$1000"))*($N6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$H$3:$H$1000"));0);MATCH(O$4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$I$1:$T$1");0)));0));"")); 1; 1)`; // <<< PASTE YOUR FORMULA HERE

    if (formulaForO6 === `=""`) {
      Logger.log("Formula for O6 is blank. Please edit the script and paste your formula.");
      // You might want to stop the script here if the formula is required
      // ui.alert("Script Error", "The formula for O6 is missing in the script.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      // return;
    }

    const templateFormulaCell = targetSheet.getRange("O6");
    templateFormulaCell.setFormula(formulaForO6);
    
    // Autofill it across to V6
    const templateRangeOtoV = targetSheet.getRange("O6:V6");
    templateFormulaCell.autoFill(templateRangeOtoV, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    Logger.log("Template formula set for O6:V6.");

    // --- 3. Clear Specific Columns (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Clearing target columns A:F and O:Y...");
    targetSheet.getRange("A8:F" + lastRow).clearContent();
    targetSheet.getRange("O8:Y" + lastRow).clearContent();

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas from Template Row 6 (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Copying formula sections from template row 6 to row 8...");
    // --- FIX: Copy *only* the formula sections, leave G:N untouched ---
    targetSheet.getRange("A6:F6").copyTo(targetSheet.getRange("A8:F8"), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);
    targetSheet.getRange("O6:Y6").copyTo(targetSheet.getRange("O8:Y8"), SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);


    // --- 5. Autofill Formula Columns ---
    Logger.log("Autofilling formula columns down to row " + lastRow);
    const rangeA8toF8 = targetSheet.getRange("A8:F8");
    const rangeO8toY8 = targetSheet.getRange("O8:Y8");

    if (lastRow > 8) {
      // Autofill A:F
      rangeA8toF8.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("A8:F" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      // Autofill O:Y
      rangeO8toY8.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("O8:Y" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }
    
    // --- 6. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for all formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(1000); // Allow time for IMPORTRANGE

    Logger.log("Converting formulas in A8:Y" + lastRow + " to static values.");
    const rangeToConvert = targetSheet.getRange("A8:Y" + lastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 7. Check for Warnings (Blanks in A:E or '-' in X) ---
    Logger.log("Checking for warnings...");
    const warningRangeAE = targetSheet.getRange("A8:E" + lastRow).getValues();
    const warningRangeX = targetSheet.getRange("X8:X" + lastRow).getValues();
    let warningFound = false;

    for (let r = 0; r < warningRangeAE.length; r++) {
      // Check A:E
      for (let c = 0; c < warningRangeAE[r].length; c++) {
        if (String(warningRangeAE[r][c]).trim() === "") {
          warningFound = true;
          Logger.log(`Warning: Found blank cell at row ${r + 8}, col ${c + 1}`);
          break;
        }
      }
      if (warningFound) break;

      // Check X
      if (warningRangeX[r][0] === "-") {
         warningFound = true;
         Logger.log(`Warning: Found '-' in cell X${r + 8}`);
         break;
      }
    }

    // --- 8. Display Appropriate Message ---
    targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate(); // As per VBA
    if (warningFound) {
      Logger.log("Warning message triggered.");
      ss.toast('WARNUNG: Für einige Datensätze fehlt der GF-EK DE/BL DE/EKL DE/GL-EK INT/EKL INT oder die Deutsche Übersetzung zum Grund.', "Achtung!", 15);
    } else {
      navigateOnSuccess();
      // Optional: Activate next sheet
      // const nextSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Food Qualitätsfälle");
      // if (nextSheet) nextSheet.activate();
    }

  } catch (e) {
    const processingError = `An error occurred while generating data: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', processingError, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR during processing: ${e.stack}`);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log("--- Finished generateRawFoodQualityCases ---");
}

GENERATE_DATA_Rohdaten_Anderungswunsche_Sort.gs
/**
 * ⚙️ Generates processed data for Sorting Arrangement Wishes.
 * V22: Uses the user-provided, working LET/FILTER/INDEX/MATCH formula.
 * Applies it row-by-row via autofill and finalizes data correctly.
 */
function generateChangeWishesData() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  Logger.log("--- Starting generateChangeWishesData (V22 - User Formula) ---");

  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Änderungswünsche Sort.");
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");

  if (!targetSheet || !settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Rohdaten Änderungswünsche Sort." sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

// Grab all values in Column I at once (bypasses the ghost data issue)
  const columnIValues = targetSheet.getRange("I1:I" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let lastRow = 0;

  // Loop backwards from the bottom of the array
  for (let i = columnIValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    // Check if the cell actually contains visible text/numbers
    if (String(columnIValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      lastRow = i + 1; // +1 because arrays start at 0, but sheet rows start at 1
      break;
    }
  }

  Logger.log(`Last row with true data found in column I is: ${lastRow}`);

  if (lastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'No data found in rows 8 or below to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 7.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File URL and Extract the ID ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Änderungswünsche Sortierung";
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' };
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileUrl) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file URL for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File URL for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
  
  try {
    const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
    if (match && match[1]) {
      sourceFileId = match[1]; // Use ID for IMPORTRANGE
      Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
    } else {
      throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
    }
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
    return;
  }

  const sheetName = 'In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F';
  const urlCellReference = `Einstellungen!F${foundRowNumber}`; // Reference for the formula

  try {
    // --- 2. Clear & Prepare ---
    Logger.log("Clearing old data and formatting...");
    const rangeAtoE = targetSheet.getRange("A8:E" + lastRow);
    const rangeJtoY = targetSheet.getRange("J8:Y" + lastRow);
    rangeAtoE.clear({ contentsOnly: true, formatOnly: true });
    rangeJtoY.clearContent();

    // --- 3. Apply ALL Formulas ---
    Logger.log("Applying formulas...");
    const formulaTemplateBlock1 = targetSheet.getRange("A6:E6");
    formulaTemplateBlock1.copyTo(targetSheet.getRange("A8:E" + lastRow));

    // --- USER'S WORKING FORMULA (Adapted for script and EU locale) ---
    // Note: Using sourceFileId directly in IMPORTRANGE is generally more robust than referencing the URL via Einstellungen!F{row}
    const newFormulaForJ8 = `=LET(
    url; Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};
    sheet_name; "In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F";
    data_range; IMPORTRANGE(url; "'"&sheet_name&"'!E3:Q1000");
    criteria1_range; IMPORTRANGE(url; "'"&sheet_name&"'!B3:B1000");
    criteria2_range; IMPORTRANGE(url; "'"&sheet_name&"'!C3:C1000");
    header_range; IMPORTRANGE(url; "'"&sheet_name&"'!E1:Q1");

    IFERROR(
        INDEX(
            FILTER(
                data_range;
                TRIM(TO_TEXT(criteria1_range)) = TRIM(TO_TEXT($G8));
                TRIM(TO_TEXT(criteria2_range)) = TRIM(TO_TEXT($H8))
            );
            1;
            MATCH(J$5; header_range; 0)
        );
    "")
)`;
    
    Logger.log(`Generated user's LET formula for J8.`);
    targetSheet.getRange("J8").setFormula(newFormulaForJ8);

    // Autofill the formula across and down
    const firstDataRowRangeJQ = targetSheet.getRange("J8:Q8");
    targetSheet.getRange("J8").autoFill(firstDataRowRangeJQ, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
     if (lastRow > 8) {
      firstDataRowRangeJQ.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("J8:Q" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }

    targetSheet.getRange("R8").setFormula(`=ARRAYFORMULA(IF(LEN(G8:G${lastRow}); MMULT(IFERROR(VALUE(J8:Q${lastRow}); 0); SEQUENCE(8; 1; 1; 0)); ))`);
    
    // --- 4. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for all formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(12000); // Allow ample time for IMPORTRANGE

    Logger.log("Converting formulas in A8:R" + lastRow + " to static values.");
    const fullRangeToConvert = targetSheet.getRange("A8:R" + lastRow);
    fullRangeToConvert.copyTo(fullRangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 5. Apply Formatting to Static Values (Robust Method) ---
    Logger.log("Applying formatting rules to the static data in A8:E" + lastRow);
    rangeAtoE.setBackground("#ffffff").setFontColor("#000000");
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();

    const redFillRule = SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenCellEmpty()
      .setBackground("#ff0000")
      .setRanges([rangeAtoE])
      .build();

    const allRules = targetSheet.getConditionalFormatRules();
    allRules.push(redFillRule);
    targetSheet.setConditionalFormatRules(allRules);
    Logger.log("Successfully applied all formatting rules.");

    // --- 6. Run Diagnostic Logging ---
    logAdvancedDiagnosticInfo(targetSheet, lastRow, sourceFileId, sheetName); 

  } catch (e) {
    const processingError = `An error occurred while generating data: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', processingError, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR during processing: ${e.stack}`);
    return;
  }

  navigateOnSuccess();
  Logger.log("--- Finished generateChangeWishesData ---");
}


/**
 * 🧑‍💻 Performs a full "code equivalent" simulation of the formula logic for verbose comparison.
 * Logs every variable, data type, and calculation step to compare against the sheet's output.
 */
function logAdvancedDiagnosticInfo(sheet, lastRow, sourceFileId, sourceSheetName) {
  if (lastRow < 8) return;
  Logger.log("\n\n--- Starting Hyper-Verbose Diagnostic Log (Code Simulation) ---");

  // --- 1. Fetch ALL necessary data in one go ---
  let sourceHeader, sourceValuesB, sourceValuesC, sourceDataRange;
  try {
    const sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
    const sourceSheet = sourceSs.getSheetByName(sourceSheetName);
    if (!sourceSheet) {
      Logger.log(`CRITICAL LOGGING ERROR: Source sheet "${sourceSheetName}" not found.`);
      return;
    }
    const sourceLastRow = sourceSheet.getLastRow();
    sourceHeader = sourceSheet.getRange("E1:Q1").getDisplayValues()[0]; 
    sourceValuesB = sourceSheet.getRange("B3:B" + sourceLastRow).getDisplayValues();
    sourceValuesC = sourceSheet.getRange("C3:C" + sourceLastRow).getDisplayValues();
    sourceDataRange = sourceSheet.getRange("E3:Q" + sourceLastRow).getDisplayValues();
    Logger.log(`Successfully fetched ${sourceValuesB.length} data rows and headers for logging.`);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`CRITICAL LOGGING ERROR: Could not open or read source file. Error: ${e.message}`);
    return;
  }

  // Fetch target data
  const targetCriteria = sheet.getRange("G8:H" + lastRow).getDisplayValues();
  const targetHeaders4 = sheet.getRange("J4:Q4").getDisplayValues()[0];
  const targetHeaders5 = sheet.getRange("J5:Q5").getDisplayValues()[0];

  for (let i = 0; i < targetCriteria.length; i++) {
    const rowNum = i + 8;
    const criteriaG = targetCriteria[i][0].trim();
    const criteriaH = targetCriteria[i][1].trim();
    
    Logger.log(`\n================== SIMULATING LOGIC FOR TARGET ROW ${rowNum} ==================`);
    Logger.log(`  ➡️ STEP 1: FINDING ROW MATCH...`);
    Logger.log(`     - Target Criteria: Artikelnummer='${criteriaG}', Artikel='${criteriaH}'`);

    let matchFoundOnSourceRowIndex = -1; // This will be the 0-based index for our arrays
    for (let j = 0; j < sourceValuesB.length; j++) {
      if (sourceValuesB[j][0].trim() === criteriaG && sourceValuesC[j][0].trim() === criteriaH) {
        matchFoundOnSourceRowIndex = j;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (matchFoundOnSourceRowIndex === -1) {
      Logger.log(`  ❗️ RESULT: FAILURE! No matching row found in source data. Expected output for this row is blank.`);
      continue;
    }
    const matchedRowData = sourceDataRange[matchFoundOnSourceRowIndex];
    Logger.log(`  ✅ RESULT: SUCCESS! Row match found at source index ${matchFoundOnSourceRowIndex} (Sheet Row ${matchFoundOnSourceRowIndex + 3}).`);
    Logger.log(`     - Full Data Row Found: [${matchedRowData.join(', ')}]`);
    
    Logger.log(`\n  ➡️ STEP 2: CALCULATING VALUES FOR EACH COLUMN (J through Q)...`);
    
    for (let colIdx = 0; colIdx < targetHeaders5.length; colIdx++) {
      const colLetter = String.fromCharCode('J'.charCodeAt(0) + colIdx);
      const currentHeaderVal = targetHeaders5[colIdx];
      const prevHeaderVal = targetHeaders4[colIdx];
      
      Logger.log(`\n     --- Simulating Column ${colLetter} ---`);
      Logger.log(`       - Target Header (Current): "${currentHeaderVal}" | (Previous): "${prevHeaderVal}"`);

      let valueCurrent = 0;
      let valuePrev = 0;

      // Find column index for CURRENT week
      const colIndexCurrent = sourceHeader.findIndex(h => h.includes(currentHeaderVal));
      if (colIndexCurrent !== -1) {
        const rawVal = matchedRowData[colIndexCurrent];
