        Logger.log(`       - Match (Current): Found '${currentHeaderVal}' in source header '${sourceHeader[colIndexCurrent]}'.`);
        Logger.log(`       - Raw Value from Source: "${rawVal}" (Data Type: ${typeof rawVal})`);
        valueCurrent = parseFloat(String(rawVal).replace(',', '.')) || 0;
        Logger.log(`       - Converted Value (Current): ${valueCurrent}`);
      } else {
        Logger.log(`       - Match (Current): ❗️ FAILED to find '${currentHeaderVal}' in source headers.`);
      }

      // Find column index for PREVIOUS week
      if (currentHeaderVal !== prevHeaderVal) {
        const colIndexPrev = sourceHeader.findIndex(h => h.includes(prevHeaderVal));
         if (colIndexPrev !== -1) {
          const rawVal = matchedRowData[colIndexPrev];
          Logger.log(`       - Match (Previous): Found '${prevHeaderVal}' in source header '${sourceHeader[colIndexPrev]}'.`);
          Logger.log(`       - Raw Value from Source: "${rawVal}" (Data Type: ${typeof rawVal})`);
          valuePrev = parseFloat(String(rawVal).replace(',', '.')) || 0;
          Logger.log(`       - Converted Value (Previous): ${valuePrev}`);
        } else {
          Logger.log(`       - Match (Previous): ❗️ FAILED to find '${prevHeaderVal}' in source headers.`);
        }
      }
      
      // Perform final calculation
      let finalValue;
      if (currentHeaderVal === prevHeaderVal) {
        finalValue = valueCurrent;
        Logger.log(`       - LOGIC: Headers are equal.`);
      } else {
        finalValue = valueCurrent + valuePrev;
        Logger.log(`       - LOGIC: Headers are different. Summing: ${valueCurrent} + ${valuePrev}.`);
      }
      Logger.log(`       - ✅ FINAL CALCULATED VALUE for ${colLetter}${rowNum}: ${finalValue}`);
    }
  }
  Logger.log("\n================== END OF DIAGNOSTIC LOG ==================");
}

GENERATE_DATA_Rohdaten_Food_Sortimentswünsche.gs
/**
 * ⚙️ Generates processed data for Food Assortment Wishes.
 * V15: Final version. Fixes the "Ranges must have at least one range" error by using a more stable, sheet-level approach for applying conditional formatting.
 * This version correctly calculates, converts to values, and then applies all formatting.
 */
function generateFoodAssortmentData() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  Logger.log("--- Starting generateFoodAssortmentData (v15 - Robust Formatting) ---");

  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche");
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");

  if (!targetSheet || !settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // Grab all values in Column I at once (bypasses the ghost data issue)
  const columnIValues = targetSheet.getRange("I1:I" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let lastRow = 0;

  // Loop backwards from the bottom of the array
  for (let i = columnIValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    // Check if the cell actually contains visible text/numbers
    if (String(columnIValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      lastRow = i + 1; // +1 because arrays start at 0, but sheet rows start at 1
      break;
    }
  }

  Logger.log(`Last row with true data found in column I is: ${lastRow}`);

  if (lastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'No data found in rows 8 or below to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 7.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Sortimentswünsche";
  let foundRowNumber = -1;
  let sourceFileId = null; 

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' };
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileId = settingsValues[i][4]; // Column E
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found source file configuration on row: ${foundRowNumber} with ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
  
  const sheetName = 'In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F';

  try {
    // --- 2. Clear & Prepare ---
    Logger.log("Clearing old data and formatting...");
    const rangeAtoE = targetSheet.getRange("A8:E" + lastRow);
    const rangeJtoY = targetSheet.getRange("J8:Y" + lastRow); 
    rangeAtoE.clear({contentsOnly: true, formatOnly: true});
    rangeJtoY.clearContent();

    // --- 3. Apply ALL Formulas at Once ---
    Logger.log("Applying all formulas to ranges A:E and J:R...");
    const formulaTemplateBlock1 = targetSheet.getRange("A6:E6");
    formulaTemplateBlock1.copyTo(targetSheet.getRange("A8:E" + lastRow));
    
    const newFormulaForJ8 = `=ARRAY_CONSTRAIN(ARRAYFORMULA(IFERROR(IF(J$5=J$4;INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$E$3:$Q$1000");MATCH(1;($G8=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$B$3:$B$1000"))*($H8=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$C$3:$C$1000"));0);MATCH(J$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$E$1:$Q$1");0));IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$E$3:$Q$1000");MATCH(1;($G8=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$B$3:$B$1000"))*($H8=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$C$3:$C$1000"));0);MATCH(J$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$E$1:$Q$1");0)));0)+IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$E$3:$Q$1000");MATCH(1;($G8=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$B$3:$B$1000"))*($H8=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$C$3:$C$1000"));0);MATCH(J$4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"${sheetName}!$E$1:$Q$1");0)));0));"")); 1; 1)`;
    
    targetSheet.getRange("J8").setFormula(newFormulaForJ8);
    const firstDataRowRangeJQ = targetSheet.getRange("J8:Q8");
    targetSheet.getRange("J8").autoFill(firstDataRowRangeJQ, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    if (lastRow > 8) {
      firstDataRowRangeJQ.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("J8:Q" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }

    targetSheet.getRange("R8").setFormula("=SUM(ARRAYFORMULA(IFERROR(VALUE(J8:Q8); 0)))");
    if (lastRow > 8) {
       targetSheet.getRange("R8").autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("R8:R" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }
    
    // --- 4. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for all formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(10000); 

    Logger.log("Converting formulas in A8:R" + lastRow + " to static values.");
    const fullRangeToConvert = targetSheet.getRange("A8:R" + lastRow);
    fullRangeToConvert.copyTo(fullRangeToConvert, {contentsOnly: true});

    // // --- 5. Apply Formatting to Static Values (Robust Method) ---
    // Logger.log("Applying formatting rules to the static data in A8:E" + lastRow);
    
    // // Apply basic formats first, as this is less error-prone
    // rangeAtoE.setBackground("#ffffff").setFontColor("#000000");
    // SpreadsheetApp.flush(); // Ensure basic formats are applied before moving on

    // // Build the new rule, explicitly binding it to the range
    // const redFillRule = SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
    //   .whenCellEmpty()
    //   .setBackground("#ff0000")
    //   .setRanges([rangeAtoE]) // Explicitly set the range for this rule
    //   .build();

    // // Get all existing rules on the sheet
    // const allRules = targetSheet.getConditionalFormatRules();
    // allRules.push(redFillRule); // Add our new rule to the array

    // // Set the complete collection of rules back to the sheet
    // targetSheet.setConditionalFormatRules(allRules);
    // Logger.log("Successfully applied all formatting rules.");
    
    // --- 5. Apply Formatting ---
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from the first data row to all rows...");
    const formatTemplateRange = targetSheet.getRange("A8:R8");
    if (lastRow > 8) {
      const formatDestination = targetSheet.getRange("A9:R" + lastRow);
      formatTemplateRange.copyTo(formatDestination, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
    }

    // --- 6. Run Diagnostic Logging ---
    logAdvancedDiagnosticInfo(targetSheet, lastRow, sourceFileId, sheetName);

  } catch (e) {
    const processingError = `An error occurred while generating data: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', processingError, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR during processing: ${e.stack}`);
    return;
  }
  
  navigateOnSuccess();
  Logger.log("--- Finished generateFoodAssortmentData ---");
}




GENERATE_DATA_Rohdaten_OG_Qualif_o_LFN.gs

/**
 * ⚙️ Generates processed data for 'Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'RohdatenOGQualitätsfälleohneLFNFormelnKopieren' (Modul43).
 *
 * This script FIRST sets a new user-defined formula in the template row H6:Q6,
 * THEN copies/autofills all template formulas (A6:Q6) down,
 * and finally converts all results to static values.
 */
function generateRawOGQualityCasesNoLFN() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  Logger.log("--- Starting generateRawOGQualityCasesNoLFN ---");

  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN");
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen"); // Needed for formula

  if (!targetSheet || !settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row (for the formula) ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_O+G_DE_Qualitätsfälle (ohne LFN)"; // As defined in Modul42
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; 
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
        return;
      }
      break; 
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  
  // // Find last row based on Column E (Artikel) as per VBA
  // const lastRow = targetSheet.getRange("E" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
  // Logger.log(`Last row with data found in column E is: ${lastRow}`);
  // if (lastRow < 8) {
  //   ui.alert('No Data', 'No imported data found in Column E (rows 8 or below) to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  //   Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 7.');
  //   return;
  // }

  //begin of fix

  // Grab all values in Column E at once (much faster than reading cell-by-cell)
  const columnEValues = targetSheet.getRange("E1:E" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let lastRow = 0;

  // Loop backwards from the bottom of the array
  for (let i = columnEValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    // Check if the cell isn't empty after stripping away hidden whitespace
    if (String(columnEValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      lastRow = i + 1; // +1 because arrays start at 0, but sheet rows start at 1
      break;
    }
  }

  Logger.log(`Last row with true data found in column E is: ${lastRow}`);

  if (lastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'No imported data found in Column E (rows 8 or below) to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 7.');
    return;
  }

  //end of fix

  try {
    // --- 2. SET TEMPLATE FORMULA (User Request) ---
    Logger.log("Setting user-defined formula in template row H6:Q6...");

    // !!! PASTE YOUR FORMULA FOR CELL H6 HERE, using semicolons for EU locale !!!
    // It should reference $B6, $C6, etc. and the 'foundRowNumber' variable.
    // Example: `="=IFERROR(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber}; ... ); ... ))"`
    const formulaForH6 = `=ARRAY_CONSTRAIN(ARRAYFORMULA(IFERROR(IF(H$5<>H$4;(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$3:$O$500");XMATCH(1;($B6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$500"))*($D6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$500"))*($E6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$D$3:$D$500"))*($F6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$E$500"))*($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$F$3:$F$500")));XMATCH(H$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$1:$O$1"))))+(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$3:$O$500");XMATCH(1;($B6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$500"))*($D6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$500"))*($E6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$D$3:$D$500"))*($F6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$E$500"))*($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$F$3:$F$500")));XMATCH(H$4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$1:$O$1"))));INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$3:$O$500");XMATCH(1;($B6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$500"))*($D6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$500"))*($E6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$D$3:$D$500"))*($F6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$E$500"))*($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$F$3:$F$500")));XMATCH(H$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$G$1:$O$1"))));"")); 1; 1)`;

    const templateFormulaCell = targetSheet.getRange("H6");
    if (formulaForH6 !== `=""`) { // Only set formula if it's not blank
      templateFormulaCell.setFormula(formulaForH6);
    
      // Autofill it across to Q6 (as per VBA's H:Q range)
      const templateRangeHtoO = targetSheet.getRange("H6:O6");
      templateFormulaCell.autoFill(templateRangeHtoO, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      Logger.log("Template formula set for H6:Q6.");
    } else {
      Logger.log("Skipping template formula set for H6:Q6 as it was blank.");
    }

    // --- 3. Clear Specific Columns (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Clearing target columns A and H:Q...");
    targetSheet.getRange("A8:A" + lastRow).clearContent();
    targetSheet.getRange("H8:Q" + lastRow).clearContent();

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas from Template Row 6 (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Copying full template row A6:Q6 to A8...");
    const formulaTemplateRange = targetSheet.getRange("A6");
    const formulaStartRow = targetSheet.getRange("A8");
    formulaTemplateRange.copyTo(formulaStartRow, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);
    const formulaTemplateRange2 = targetSheet.getRange("H6:Q6");
    const formulaStartRow2 = targetSheet.getRange("H8:Q8");
    formulaTemplateRange2.copyTo(formulaStartRow2, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);

    // --- 5. Autofill Formula Columns ---
    Logger.log("Autofilling formula columns down to row " + lastRow);
    const rangeA8 = targetSheet.getRange("A8");
    const rangeH8toQ8 = targetSheet.getRange("H8:Q8");

    if (lastRow > 8) {
      // Autofill A
      rangeA8.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("A8:A" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      // Autofill H:Q
      rangeH8toQ8.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange("H8:Q" + lastRow), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }
    
    // --- 6. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for all formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(10000); // Allow time for IMPORTRANGE

    Logger.log("Converting formulas in A8:Q" + lastRow + " to static values.");
    const rangeToConvert = targetSheet.getRange("A8:Q" + lastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 7. Check for Warnings (None in VBA for this macro) ---
    // VBA Modul43 does not have a warning check.

    // --- 8. Display Appropriate Message ---
    targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate(); // As per VBA
    navigateOnSuccess();
    
    // Optional: Activate next sheet
    // const nextSheet = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");
    // if (nextSheet) nextSheet.activate();

  } catch (e) {
    const processingError = `An error occurred while generating data: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', processingError, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR during processing: ${e.stack}`);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log("--- Finished generateRawOGQualityCasesNoLFN ---");
}
GENERATE_DATA_Sonstiges_Food_Themen.gs
/**
 * ⚙️ Generates processed data for 'Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'SonstigesFoodundAktuelleThemenDatenGenerieren'.
 *
 * V3: Explicitly sets the user-provided LET formula in G7:Q7,
 * and copies other template formulas, then converts all to values.
 */
function generateRawOtherFoodTopics() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  Logger.log("--- Starting generateRawOtherFoodTopics (V3 - Explicit Formula Set) ---");

  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen");
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");

  if (!targetSheet || !settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Sonstiges und aktuelle Themen"; // Source file name for this sheet
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; 
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      // --- START OF FIX ---
      // Extract the ID from the URL and assign it to sourceFileId
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
        return;
      }
      // --- END OF FIX ---
      break; // Exit loop once found
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileUrl) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file URL for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File URL for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
  
  try {
    const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
    if (match && match[1]) {
      sourceFileId = match[1]; // Use ID for IMPORTRANGE
      Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
    } else {
      throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
    }
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
    return;
  }

  // Find last row based on Column E (imported data) as per VBA
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getRange("E" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
  Logger.log(`Last row with data found in column E is: ${lastRow}`);
  if (lastRow < 7) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'No imported data found in Column E (rows 7 or below) to process.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process below row 6.');
    return;
  }

  try {
    // --- 2. De-duplicate Data (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log(`De-duplicating range A7:R${lastRow} based on Column E.`);
    const dataRange = targetSheet.getRange("A7:R" + lastRow);
    dataRange.removeDuplicates([5]); // Column E is the 5th column in this range

    const newLastRow = targetSheet.getRange("E" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
    Logger.log(`New last row after de-duplication is: ${newLastRow}`);
    
    if (newLastRow < 7) {
        Logger.log("No data remaining after de-duplication.");
        return;
    }
    
    // --- 3. Clear Specific Columns ---
    targetSheet.getRange("A7:D" + newLastRow).clearContent();
    targetSheet.getRange("F7:O" + newLastRow).clearContent();

    // --- EXPLICITLY SET THE USER'S LET FORMULA ---
    // We build the formula string for row 7 (which references E7, G$3, G$2)
    // All semicolons are kept for EU locale.
    const newFormulaForG4 = `=IFERROR(
   LET(
      dataRange; IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber}; "In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$N$100");
      rowHeadersRaw; IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber}; "In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$A$3:$A$100");
      colHeadersRaw; IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber}; "In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$1:$N$1");
      rowHeadersClean; ARRAYFORMULA(TRIM(SUBSTITUTE(rowHeadersRaw; CHAR(160); " ")));
      colHeadersClean; ARRAYFORMULA(TO_TEXT(colHeadersRaw));
      lookupValueClean; TRIM(SUBSTITUTE($E4; CHAR(160); " "));
      rowNum; MATCH(lookupValueClean; rowHeadersClean; 0);
      result; 
      IF(
         G$3=G$2;
         INDEX(dataRange; rowNum; MATCH(G$3; colHeadersClean; 0));
         IFERROR(VALUE(INDEX(dataRange; rowNum; MATCH(G$3; colHeadersClean; 0))); 0) + 
         IFERROR(VALUE(INDEX(dataRange; rowNum; MATCH(G$2; colHeadersClean; 0))); 0)
      );
      IF(result=0; ""; result)
   )
; "")`;

    Logger.log(`Setting complex formula in G4...`);
    targetSheet.getRange("G4").setFormula(newFormulaForG4);

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas ---

    Logger.log("Applying formulas from template row 4 to data rows 7+...");
    
    // Define template ranges from row 4
    const formulaTemplateAtoD = targetSheet.getRange("A4:D4");
    const formulaTemplateFtoO = targetSheet.getRange("F4:O4");
    const formulaTemplateR = targetSheet.getRange("R4");

    // Define destination start row (row 7)
    const destStartRow = 7;
    const destRangeAtoD = targetSheet.getRange(destStartRow, 1, 1, 4); // A7:D7
    const destRangeFtoO = targetSheet.getRange(destStartRow, 6, 1, 10); // F7:O7
    const destRangeR = targetSheet.getRange(destStartRow, 18, 1, 1); // R7
    
    // Copy template formulas to the first data row (row 7)
    formulaTemplateAtoD.copyTo(destRangeAtoD, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);
    formulaTemplateFtoO.copyTo(destRangeFtoO, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);
    formulaTemplateR.copyTo(destRangeR, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMULA, false);

    // --- 5. Autofill all formula rows ---
    Logger.log("Autofilling all formula columns down to row " + newLastRow);
    if (newLastRow > destStartRow) { // Only autofill if there's more than one row
      // Autofill A:D
      destRangeAtoD.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange(destStartRow, 1, newLastRow - destStartRow + 1, 4), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      // Autofill F:N
      destRangeFtoO.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange(destStartRow, 6, newLastRow - destStartRow + 1, 10), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      // Autofill R
      destRangeR.autoFill(targetSheet.getRange(destStartRow, 18, newLastRow - destStartRow + 1, 1), SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
    }
    
    // --- 6. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for all formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(12000); // Increased time for all the IMPORTRANGE calls

    Logger.log("Converting formulas in A7:R" + newLastRow + " to static values.");
    const rangeToConvert = targetSheet.getRange("A7:R" + newLastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 7. Apply Formatting (Mimicking VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from template row A7:R7 to all data rows.");
    const formatTemplateRow = targetSheet.getRange("A7:R7"); // Use the first data row as format template
    if (newLastRow >= 7) {
        formatTemplateRow.copyTo(rangeToConvert, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
    }

    // --- 8. Sort the Data (Two Passes) ---
    Logger.log("Sorting the data (Pass 1)...");
    const sortRange = targetSheet.getRange("A7:R" + newLastRow);
    sortRange.sort([
        { column: 3, ascending: true }, // Col C
        { column: 4, ascending: true }, // Col D
        { column: 5, ascending: true }  // Col E
    ]);

    Logger.log("Sorting the data (Pass 2)...");
    sortRange.sort([
        { column: 18, ascending: true }, // Col R
        { column: 1, ascending: true },  // Col A
        { column: 2, ascending: true }   // Col B
    ]);

    // --- 9. Cleanup: Lösche alles unterhalb der formatierten/sortierten Daten ---
    const maxRows = targetSheet.getMaxRows();
    if (maxRows > newLastRow) {
        // Löscht alles ab der ersten leeren Zeile bis ganz unten. 
        // Spalten A bis R = 18 Spalten
        targetSheet.getRange(newLastRow + 1, 1, maxRows - newLastRow, 18).clear();
        Logger.log(`Tabelle von Zeile ${newLastRow + 1} bis ${maxRows} komplett gesäubert.`);
    }

    // --- 10. Check for Warnings (Blanks in A:D) ---
    Logger.log("Checking for warnings (blanks in A:D)...");
    const warningRange = targetSheet.getRange("A7:D" + newLastRow);
    const warningValues = warningRange.getValues();
    let warningFound = false;
    
    for (let r = 0; r < warningValues.length; r++) {
      for (let c = 0; c < warningValues[r].length; c++) {
        if (String(warningValues[r][c]).trim() === "") {
          warningFound = true;
          Logger.log(`Warning: Found blank cell at row ${r + 7}, col ${c + 1}`);
          break;
        }
      }
      if (warningFound) break;
    }

    // --- 11. Display Appropriate Message ---
    targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate(); // As per VBA
    if (warningFound) {
      Logger.log("Warning message triggered due to blank cells in A:D.");
      ss.toast('WARNUNG: Für einige Datensätze fehlt der GF-EK DE, BL DE, EKL DE oder GL-EK INT. Bitte trage die Werte manuell ein.', "Achtung!", 15);
    } else {
      ss.toast('Die Daten wurden erfolgreich generiert!', 'Erfolg!', 10);
      navigateOnSuccess();
    }

  } catch (e) {
    const processingError = `An error occurred while generating data: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', processingError, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR during processing: ${e.stack}`);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log("--- Finished generateRawOtherFoodTopics ---");
}

IMPORT_DATA_Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche.gs
/**
 * Imports and processes data from 'Rohdaten Allg. Sortimentsw.' to 'Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'Daten_Aus_RohdatenAllgemeineSortimentswünsche_Importieren'.
 * V5: Corrects sort range to exclude header and adjusts formatting application range.
 */
function importToGeneralAssortmentWishes() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sourceSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Allg. Sortimentsw.");
  const destSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importToGeneralAssortmentWishes (V5 - Sort/Format Fix) ---");

  if (!sourceSheet || !destSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find the source ("Rohdaten...") or destination ("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche") sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // Check source sheet using Column B (Grund) as per VBA
  const columnBValues = sourceSheet.getRange("B1:B" + sourceSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let sourceLastRow = 0;
  for (let i = columnBValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (String(columnBValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      sourceLastRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (sourceLastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'The "Rohdaten Allg. Sortimentsw." sheet has no data to import (checked Col B).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process on the source sheet.');
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found data up to row ${sourceLastRow} on source sheet.`);

  try {
    // --- 1. Clear Old Data Content ---
    const destLastRow = destSheet.getLastRow();
    if (destLastRow >= 8) { // Data starts at row 8 in destination
      Logger.log(`Clearing old content from A8:K${destLastRow} in 'Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche'.`);
      destSheet.getRange("A8:K" + destLastRow).clearContent();
    }

    // --- 2. Read, and De-duplicate Data in Memory ---
    Logger.log("Reading source data (Column A)...");
    const sourceRange = sourceSheet.getRange("A8:A" + sourceLastRow); // Only need Column A
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();

    const uniqueGrundDE = new Set();
    const processedData = []; // Will hold only Column A initially

    Logger.log("Processing and de-duplicating data based on Grund DE (Column A)...");
    for (const row of sourceValues) {
      const grundDE = row[0]; // Value from Column A
      
      // If we haven't seen this Grund DE before, add it.
      if (grundDE !== null && String(grundDE).trim() !== '' && !uniqueGrundDE.has(grundDE)) { // Ensure not blank before adding
        processedData.push([grundDE]); // Add just the single value
        uniqueGrundDE.add(grundDE);
      }
    }
    Logger.log(`Finished processing. Found ${processedData.length} unique rows.`);
    
    if (processedData.length === 0) {
        ui.alert('No Data', 'No unique data rows were found to import.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        return;
    }

    // --- 3. Write Processed Data (Column A) to Destination ---
    Logger.log("Writing processed data to 'Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche' sheet (Column A).");
    destSheet.getRange(8, 1, processedData.length, 1).setValues(processedData); // Write to A8 onwards
    
    const newLastRow = 7 + processedData.length; // Row number of the last written data row

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas using a Format-Preserving Method ---
    Logger.log(`Applying formulas from B5:K5 to B8:K${newLastRow} using R1C1 notation.`);
    const formulaTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("B5:K5"); // Template row is 5
    const templateFormulas = formulaTemplateRange.getFormulasR1C1()[0]; // Get the 1D array of formula strings

    if (templateFormulas.join('').length > 0) {
        const numRows = newLastRow - 7; // Number of data rows (from 8 to newLastRow)
        const formulasForRange = [];
        // Build a 2D array by repeating the template row for each destination row
        for (let i = 0; i < numRows; i++) {
            formulasForRange.push(templateFormulas);
        }
        
        const formulaDestinationRange = destSheet.getRange("B8:K" + newLastRow);
        formulaDestinationRange.setFormulasR1C1(formulasForRange);
    } else {
        Logger.log("Warning: No formulas found in template range B5:K5.");
    }
    
    // --- 5. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for formulas to calculate...");
    ss.toast("Waiting 15 seconds for formulas to calculate.", 15);
    Utilities.sleep(15000); // Adjust if needed
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();

    Logger.log(`Converting formulas in B8:K${newLastRow} to static values.`);
    const rangeToConvertToValues = destSheet.getRange("B8:K" + newLastRow);
    rangeToConvertToValues.copyTo(rangeToConvertToValues, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 6. Sort the Data ---
    // --- FIX: Sort range changed from A7 to A8 to exclude header ---
    Logger.log("Sorting the data A8:K" + newLastRow + " by Column A...");
    const fullDataRangeToSort = destSheet.getRange("A8:K" + newLastRow); 
    fullDataRangeToSort.sort({ column: 1, ascending: true }); // Sort by Column A

    // --- 7. Apply Formatting (Mimicking VBA) ---
    // --- FIX: Apply format to the entire data range A8:K<newLastRow> ---
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from template row A8:K8 to all data rows.");
    const formatTemplateRow = destSheet.getRange("A8:K8"); 
    if (newLastRow >= 8) { // Check if there is data to format
      const formatDestination = destSheet.getRange("A8:K" + newLastRow); // Apply to the whole range including row 8
      formatTemplateRow.copyTo(formatDestination, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
    }

    // --- 8. Cleanup: Lösche alles unterhalb der formatierten/sortierten Daten ---
    const maxRows = destSheet.getMaxRows();
    if (maxRows > newLastRow) {
        // Löscht alles ab der ersten leeren Zeile bis ganz unten. 
        // Spalten A bis K = 11 Spalten
        destSheet.getRange(newLastRow + 1, 1, maxRows - newLastRow, 11).clear();
        Logger.log(`Tabelle von Zeile ${newLastRow + 1} bis ${maxRows} komplett gesäubert.`);
    }

    destSheet.getRange("A1").activate(); // Activate A1 as per VBA
    navigateOnSuccess();
    Logger.log("--- Finished importToGeneralAssortmentWishes ---");
    
    // Optional: Activate next sheet
    // const nextSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen");
    // if (nextSheet) nextSheet.activate();


  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
}
IMPORT_DATA_Food Qualitätsfälle.gs

/**
 * Imports and processes data from 'Rohdaten Food Qualitätsfälle' to 'Food Qualitätsfälle'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'Daten_Aus_RohdatenFoodQualitätsfälle_Importieren' (Modul34).
 * De-duplicates based on a 3-column key: "Länder" (G), "LFN" (H), and "Grund DE" (J).
 */
function importToFoodQualityCases() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sourceSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Food Qualitätsfälle");
  const destSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Food Qualitätsfälle");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importToFoodQualityCases ---");

  if (!sourceSheet || !destSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find the source ("Rohdaten...") or destination ("Food Qualitätsfälle") sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // Check source sheet using Column K (LFN) as per VBA
  const columnKValues = sourceSheet.getRange("K1:K" + sourceSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let sourceLastRow = 0;
  for (let i = columnKValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (String(columnKValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      sourceLastRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (sourceLastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'The "Rohdaten Food Qualitätsfälle" sheet has no data to import (checked Col K).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process on the source sheet.');
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found data up to row ${sourceLastRow} on source sheet.`);

  try {
    // --- 1. Clear Old Data Content ---
    const destLastRow = destSheet.getLastRow();
    if (destLastRow >= 6) { // Data starts at row 6
      Logger.log(`Clearing old content from A6:X${destLastRow} in 'Food Qualitätsfälle'.`);
      destSheet.getRange("A6:X" + destLastRow).clearContent();
    }

    // --- 2. Read, Re-order, and De-duplicate Data in Memory ---
    Logger.log("Reading source data...");
    // Read all relevant columns (A to X) from the source sheet at once.
    const sourceRange = sourceSheet.getRange("A8:X" + sourceLastRow);
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();

    const uniqueKeys = new Set(); // Use a Set to track unique combinations
    const processedData = [];

    Logger.log("Processing and de-duplicating data based on 3-column key (Länder, LFN, Grund DE)...");
    for (const row of sourceValues) {
      // Get the values for the 3-column de-duplication key
      const lander = row[8];   // Source Col I ("Länder") -> Dest Col G
      const lfn = row[5];      // Source Col F ("LFN") -> Dest Col H
      const grundDE = row[23]; // Source Col X ("Grund DE") -> Dest Col J

      const uniqueKey = `${lander}|||${lfn}|||${grundDE}`;
      
      if (!uniqueKeys.has(uniqueKey)) {
        processedData.push([
          row[0], // A -> A (GF-EK DE)
          row[1], // B -> B (BL DE)
          row[2], // C -> C (EKL DE)
          row[3], // D -> D (GL-EK INT)
          row[4], // E -> E (EKL INT)
          row[6], // G -> F (LFN QUELLE)
          lander, // I -> G (Länder)
          lfn,    // F -> H (LFN)
          row[10], // K -> I (Artikel)
          grundDE // X -> J (Grund DE)
        ]);
        uniqueKeys.add(uniqueKey);
      }
    }
    Logger.log(`Finished processing. Found ${processedData.length} unique rows.`);
    
    if (processedData.length === 0) {
        ui.alert('No Data', 'No unique data rows were found to import.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        return;
    }

    // --- 3. Write Processed Data (A:J) to Destination ---
    Logger.log("Writing processed data to 'Food Qualitätsfälle' sheet (A:J).");
    destSheet.getRange(6, 1, processedData.length, 10).setValues(processedData); // A6:J<newLastRow>
    
    const newLastRow = 5 + processedData.length; // Row number of the last written data row

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas (K:X) using a Format-Preserving Method ---
    Logger.log(`Applying formulas from K3:X3 to K6:X${newLastRow} using R1C1 notation.`);
    const formulaTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("K3:X3"); // Template row is 3
    const templateFormulas = formulaTemplateRange.getFormulasR1C1()[0]; 

    if (templateFormulas.join('').length > 0) {
        const numRows = newLastRow - 5; // Number of data rows (from 6 to newLastRow)
        const formulasForRange = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < numRows; i++) {
            formulasForRange.push(templateFormulas);
        }
        
        const formulaDestinationRange = destSheet.getRange("K6:X" + newLastRow);
        formulaDestinationRange.setFormulasR1C1(formulasForRange);
    } else {
        Logger.log("Warning: No formulas found in template range K3:X3.");
    }
    
    // --- 5. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for formulas to calculate...");
    ss.toast("Waiting for formulas to calculate - 15s", "Calculating", 15);
    Utilities.sleep(15000);

    Logger.log(`Converting formulas in K6:X${newLastRow} to static values.`);
    const rangeToConvert = destSheet.getRange("K6:X" + newLastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 6. Sort the Data (Two Passes) ---
    Logger.log("Sorting the data (Pass 1)...");
    const fullDataRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:X" + newLastRow); // VBA sorts from row 6 (Header=5)
    
    // Pass 1: G, I, J
    fullDataRange.sort([
        { column: 7, ascending: true }, // Col G
        { column: 9, ascending: true }, // Col I
        { column: 10, ascending: true } // Col J
    ]);

    Logger.log("Sorting the data (Pass 2)...");
    // Pass 2: A, B, C
    fullDataRange.sort([
        { column: 1, ascending: true }, // Col A
        { column: 2, ascending: true }, // Col B
        { column: 3, ascending: true }  // Col C
    ]);

    // --- 7. Apply Formatting (Mimicking VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from template row A6:X6 to all data rows.");
    const formatTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:X6");
    if (newLastRow >= 6) {
        const formatDestination = destSheet.getRange("A6:X" + newLastRow);
        formatTemplateRange.copyTo(formatDestination, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
    }

    // --- 8. Cleanup: Lösche alles unterhalb der formatierten/sortierten Daten ---
    const maxRows = destSheet.getMaxRows();
    if (maxRows > newLastRow) {
        // Löscht alles ab der ersten leeren Zeile bis ganz unten. 
        // Spalten A bis X = 24 Spalten
        destSheet.getRange(newLastRow + 1, 1, maxRows - newLastRow, 24).clear();
        Logger.log(`Tabelle von Zeile ${newLastRow + 1} bis ${maxRows} komplett gesäubert.`);
    }

    // --- Abschluss ---
    destSheet.getRange("A1").activate(); // Activate A1 as per VBA
    navigateOnSuccess();
    Logger.log("--- Finished importToFoodQualityCases ---");

  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
}

IMPORT_DATA_OG_QUALITATSFALLE.gs

/**
 * Imports and processes data from 'Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsfälle' to 'O+G Qualitätsfälle'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'Daten_Aus_RohdatenOGQualitätsfälle_Importieren' (Modul41).
 * De-duplicates based on a 3-column key: "KW" (B), "Grund DE" (C), and "Grund EN" (E).
 */
function importToOGQualityCases() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sourceSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsfälle");
  const destSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Qualitätsfälle");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importToOGQualityCases ---");

  if (!sourceSheet || !destSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find the source ("Rohdaten...") or destination ("O+G Qualitätsfälle") sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // Check source sheet using Column E (Artikel) as per VBA
  const columnEValues = sourceSheet.getRange("E1:E" + sourceSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let sourceLastRow = 0;
  for (let i = columnEValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (String(columnEValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      sourceLastRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (sourceLastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'The "Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsfälle" sheet has no data to import (checked Col E).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process on the source sheet.');
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found data up to row ${sourceLastRow} on source sheet.`);

  try {
    // --- 1. Clear Old Data Content ---
    const destLastRow = destSheet.getLastRow();
    if (destLastRow >= 6) { // Data starts at row 6
      Logger.log(`Clearing old content from A6:O${destLastRow} in 'O+G Qualitätsfälle'.`);
      destSheet.getRange("A6:O" + destLastRow).clearContent();
    }

    // --- 2. Read, Re-order, and De-duplicate Data in Memory ---
    Logger.log("Reading source data...");
    // Read all relevant columns (A, B, C, E, Q) from the source sheet at once.
    const sourceRange = sourceSheet.getRange("A8:Q" + sourceLastRow);
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();

    const uniqueKeys = new Set(); // Use a Set to track unique combinations
    const processedData = [];

    Logger.log("Processing and de-duplicating data based on 3-column key (KW, Grund DE, Grund EN)...");
    for (const row of sourceValues) {
      // Get the values for the 3-column de-duplication key
      const kw = row[2];      // Source Col C -> Dest Col B
      const grundDE = row[0]; // Source Col A -> Dest Col C
      const grundEN = row[16]; // Source Col Q -> Dest Col E

      const uniqueKey = `${kw}|||${grundDE}|||${grundEN}`;
      
      if (!uniqueKeys.has(uniqueKey)) {
        processedData.push([
          row[1], // Source B -> Dest A (LFN QUELLE)
          kw,     // Source C -> Dest B (KW)
          grundDE,// Source A -> Dest C (Grund DE)
          row[4], // Source E -> Dest D (Artikel)
          grundEN // Source Q -> Dest E (Grund EN)
        ]);
        uniqueKeys.add(uniqueKey);
      }
    }
    Logger.log(`Finished processing. Found ${processedData.length} unique rows.`);
    
    if (processedData.length === 0) {
        ui.alert('No Data', 'No unique data rows were found to import.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        return;
    }

    // --- 3. Write Processed Data (A:E) to Destination ---
    Logger.log("Writing processed data to 'O+G Qualitätsfälle' sheet (A:E).");
    destSheet.getRange(6, 1, processedData.length, 5).setValues(processedData); // A6:E<newLastRow>
    
    const newLastRow = 5 + processedData.length; // Row number of the last written data row

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas (F:O) using a Format-Preserving Method ---
    Logger.log(`Applying formulas from F3:O3 to F6:O${newLastRow} using R1C1 notation.`);
    const formulaTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("F3:O3"); // Template row is 3
    const templateFormulas = formulaTemplateRange.getFormulasR1C1()[0]; 

    if (templateFormulas.join('').length > 0) {
        const numRows = newLastRow - 5; // Number of data rows (from 6 to newLastRow)
        const formulasForRange = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < numRows; i++) {
            formulasForRange.push(templateFormulas);
        }
        
        const formulaDestinationRange = destSheet.getRange("F6:O" + newLastRow);
        formulaDestinationRange.setFormulasR1C1(formulasForRange);
    } else {
        Logger.log("Warning: No formulas found in template range F3:O3.");
    }
    
    // --- 5. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(5000);

    Logger.log(`Converting formulas in F6:O${newLastRow} to static values.`);
    const rangeToConvert = destSheet.getRange("F6:O" + newLastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 6. Apply Formatting (Mimicking VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from template row A6:O6 to all data rows.");
    const formatTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:O6");
    if (newLastRow >= 6) {
        const formatDestination = destSheet.getRange("A6:O" + newLastRow);
        formatTemplateRange.copyTo(formatDestination, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
    }

   // --- 7. Sort the Data (Two Passes, as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Sorting the data (Pass 1)...");
    const fullDataRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:O" + newLastRow); // VBA range is A5:O, but data starts at 6
    
    // Pass 1: B, D, E
    fullDataRange.sort([
        { column: 2, ascending: true }, // Col B (KW)
        { column: 4, ascending: true }, // Col D (Artikel)
        { column: 5, ascending: true }  // Col E (Grund EN)
    ]);

    Logger.log("Sorting the data (Pass 2)...");
    // Pass 2: A
    fullDataRange.sort({ column: 1, ascending: true }); // Col A (LFN QUELLE)

    // --- 8. Cleanup: Lösche alles (auch leere Rahmen) unterhalb der neuen Daten ---
    const maxRows = destSheet.getMaxRows(); // Zählt alle Zeilen im Blatt, egal ob leer oder nicht
    
    if (maxRows > newLastRow) {
        // Wir löschen Inhalte UND Formate (Rahmen/Farben) ab der ersten leeren Zeile bis ganz nach unten (Spalten A bis O)
        destSheet.getRange(newLastRow + 1, 1, maxRows - newLastRow, 15).clear();
        Logger.log(`Tabelle von Zeile ${newLastRow + 1} bis ${maxRows} komplett gesäubert.`);
    }

    // --- Abschluss ---
    destSheet.getRange("A1").activate(); // Activate A1 as per VBA
    navigateOnSuccess();
    Logger.log("--- Finished importToOGQualityCases ---");

  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
}
IMPORT_DATA_OG_Qualif_o_LFN.gs

/**
 * Imports and processes data from 'Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN' to 'O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'Daten_Aus_RohdatenOGQualitätsfälleohneLFN_Importieren' (Modul44).
 * De-duplicates based on a 3-column key: "Grund DE" (C), "Artikel" (D), and "Grund EN" (E).
 */
function importToOGQualityCasesNoLFN() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sourceSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN");
  const destSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importToOGQualityCasesNoLFN ---");

  if (!sourceSheet || !destSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find the source ("Rohdaten...") or destination ("O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN") sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // Check source sheet using Column E (Artikel) as per VBA
  const columnEValues = sourceSheet.getRange("E1:E" + sourceSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let sourceLastRow = 0;
  for (let i = columnEValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (String(columnEValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      sourceLastRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (sourceLastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'The "Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN" sheet has no data to import (checked Col E).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process on the source sheet.');
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found data up to row ${sourceLastRow} on source sheet.`);

  try {
    // --- 1. Clear Old Data Content ---
    const destLastRow = destSheet.getLastRow();
    if (destLastRow >= 6) { // Data starts at row 6
      Logger.log(`Clearing old content from A6:O${destLastRow} in 'O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN'.`);
      destSheet.getRange("A6:O" + destLastRow).clearContent();
    }

    // --- 2. Read, Re-order, and De-duplicate Data in Memory ---
    Logger.log("Reading source data...");
    // Read all relevant columns (A, B, C, E, Q) from the source sheet at once.
    const sourceRange = sourceSheet.getRange("A8:Q" + sourceLastRow);
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();

    const uniqueKeys = new Set(); // Use a Set to track unique combinations
    const processedData = [];

    Logger.log("Processing and de-duplicating data based on 3-column key (Grund DE, Artikel, Grund EN)...");
    for (const row of sourceValues) {
      // Get the values for the 3-column de-duplication key
      const grundDE = row[0]; // Source Col A -> Dest Col C
      const artikel = row[4]; // Source Col E -> Dest Col D
      const grundEN = row[16]; // Source Col Q -> Dest Col E

      const uniqueKey = `${grundDE}|||${artikel}|||${grundEN}`;
      
      if (!uniqueKeys.has(uniqueKey)) {
        processedData.push([
          row[1], // Source B -> Dest A (LFN QUELLE)
          row[2], // Source C -> Dest B (KW)
          grundDE, // Source A -> Dest C (Grund DE)
          artikel, // Source E -> Dest D (Artikel)
          grundEN  // Source Q -> Dest E (Grund EN)
        ]);
        uniqueKeys.add(uniqueKey);
      }
    }
    Logger.log(`Finished processing. Found ${processedData.length} unique rows.`);
    
    if (processedData.length === 0) {
        ui.alert('No Data', 'No unique data rows were found to import.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        return;
    }

    // --- 3. Write Processed Data (A:E) to Destination ---
    Logger.log("Writing processed data to 'O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN' sheet (A:E).");
    destSheet.getRange(6, 1, processedData.length, 5).setValues(processedData); // A6:E<newLastRow>
    
    const newLastRow = 5 + processedData.length; // Row number of the last written data row

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas (F:O) using a Format-Preserving Method ---
    Logger.log(`Applying formulas from F3:O3 to F6:O${newLastRow} using R1C1 notation.`);
    const formulaTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("F3:O3"); // Template row is 3
    const templateFormulas = formulaTemplateRange.getFormulasR1C1()[0]; 

    if (templateFormulas.join('').length > 0) {
        const numRows = newLastRow - 5; // Number of data rows (from 6 to newLastRow)
        const formulasForRange = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < numRows; i++) {
            formulasForRange.push(templateFormulas);
        }
        
        const formulaDestinationRange = destSheet.getRange("F6:O" + newLastRow);
        formulaDestinationRange.setFormulasR1C1(formulasForRange);
    } else {
        Logger.log("Warning: No formulas found in template range F3:O3.");
    }
    
    // --- 5. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(5000);

    Logger.log(`Converting formulas in F6:O${newLastRow} to static values.`);
    const rangeToConvert = destSheet.getRange("F6:O" + newLastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 6. Apply Formatting (Mimicking VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from template row A6:O6 to all data rows.");
    const formatTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:O6");
    if (newLastRow >= 6) {
        const formatDestination = destSheet.getRange("A6:O" + newLastRow);
        formatTemplateRange.copyTo(formatDestination, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
    }

    // --- 7. Sort the Data (as per VBA) ---
    Logger.log("Sorting the data...");
    const fullDataRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:O" + newLastRow); // VBA sorts from row 6
    
    // Pass 1: D, E
    fullDataRange.sort([
        { column: 4, ascending: true }, // Col D (Artikel)
        { column: 5, ascending: true }  // Col E (Grund EN)
    ]);

    // --- 8. Cleanup: Lösche alte Formatierungen unterhalb der neuen Daten ---
    if (destLastRow > newLastRow) {
        // Wir löschen alles von der ersten Zeile nach den neuen Daten 
        // bis zur vorherigen letzten Zeile (Spalten A bis O = 15 Spalten)
        destSheet.getRange(newLastRow + 1, 1, destLastRow - newLastRow, 15).clear();
        Logger.log(`Alte Formatierungen von Zeile ${newLastRow + 1} bis ${destLastRow} gelöscht.`);
    }
    
    destSheet.getRange("A1").activate(); // Activate A1 as per VBA
    ss.toast('Die Daten wurden erfolgreich generiert!', 'Erfolg!', 10);
    Logger.log("--- Finished importToOGQualityCasesNoLFN ---");

  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
}

IMPORT_DATA_OG_SONSTIGES.gs

/**
 * 🔎 Imports raw data for 'O+G Sonstiges'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'ImportRohdatenOGSonstiges' (Modul37).
 */
function importOGOther() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("O+G Sonstiges");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importOGOther ---");

  if (!settingsSheet || !targetSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "O+G Sonstiges" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_O+G_DE_Sonstiges"; // Source file name for this sheet
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; 
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
        return;
      }
      break; 
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }

  // --- 2. Prepare Target Sheet (Clear A7:K<lastRow>) ---
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getRange("A" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
  if (lastRow >= 7) { // Data starts at row 7
    targetSheet.getRange(7, 1, lastRow - 6, 11).clearContent(); // A7:K<lastRow>
    Logger.log(`Cleared old data from A7:K${lastRow}`);
  }

  // --- 3. Get Source Data ---
  try {
    const sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
    const sourceDataSheet = sourceSs.getSheets()[0]; // VBA uses Worksheets(1)
    if (!sourceDataSheet) {
      ui.alert('Sheet Error', 'Could not find the first sheet in the source file.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }
    Logger.log(`Using source sheet: ${sourceDataSheet.getName()}`);

    const sourceLastRow = sourceDataSheet.getLastRow();
    if (sourceLastRow < 3) { // VBA checks lr > 2
      ui.alert('No Data', 'Source file has no data to import (less than 3 rows).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }

    // --- 4. Copy data from source A3:A -> target A7 ---
    const sourceRange = sourceDataSheet.getRange(3, 1, sourceLastRow - 2, 1); // A3:A<sourceLastRow>
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();
    
    const destinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(7, 1, sourceValues.length, 1); // A7:A...

    destinationRange.setValues(sourceValues);
    Logger.log(`Successfully imported ${sourceValues.length} rows of data into Column A.`);
    
    targetSheet.getRange("A1").activate(); // Activate A1 as per VBA
    ss.toast('Die Daten wurden erfolgreich importiert! Klicke jetzt auf "DATEN GENERIEREN".', 'Erfolg!', 10);
  
  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Import Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
  Logger.log("--- Finished importOGOther ---");
}

/**

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row ---

        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);

      }
      break;

  // --- 2. Prepare Target Sheet (Clear A7:K<lastRow>) ---

    Logger.log(`Cleared old data from A7:K${lastRow}`);

      ui.alert('Sheet Error', 'Could not find the first sheet in the source file.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }
    Logger.log(`Using source sheet: ${sourceDataSheet.getName()}`);


    const sourceLastRow = sourceDataSheet.getLastRow();
    if (sourceLastRow < 3) { // VBA checks lr > 2
      ui.alert('No Data', 'Source file has no data to import (less than 3 rows).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }

    // --- 4. Copy data from source B3:B -> target A7 ---
    const sourceRange = sourceDataSheet.getRange(3, 2, sourceLastRow - 2, 1); // A3:A<sourceLastRow>
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();
    
    const destinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(7, 1, sourceValues.length, 1); // A7:A...

    destinationRange.setValues(sourceValues);
    Logger.log(`Successfully imported ${sourceValues.length} rows of data into Column A.`);

  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Import Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
  Logger.log("--- Finished importOGAssortmentWishes ---");
}

/**
 * 🔎 Imports raw data for 'Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsfälle'.
 * FIX: Plain Text method + Paste Values Only (Preserves existing borders/colors).
 * Removes destructive .toFixed(2) logic that was altering numbers.
 */
function importRawOGQualityCases() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsfälle");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importRawOGQualityCases (Strict Plain Text) ---");

  if (!settingsSheet || !targetSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsfälle" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_O+G_DE_Qualitätsfälle"; 
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' };

    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
      (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; 
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        return;
      }
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 2. Prepare Target Sheet (Clear A8:Q<lastRow>) ---
  // const lastRow = targetSheet.getRange("E" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow(); // VBA checks Col E
  // if (lastRow >= 8) { // Data starts at row 8
  //   targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, lastRow - 7, 17).clearContent(); // A8:Q<lastRow>
  //   Logger.log(`Cleared old data from A8:Q${lastRow}`);
  // }

    // 1. Get the actual last row with content in the entire sheet
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getLastRow(); 

  // 2. Check if that last row is at or beyond your starting point (Row 8)
  if (lastRow >= 8) {
    // We calculate the number of rows to clear: (Total - Start + 1)
    // For example: if lastRow is 10, we clear 10 - 8 + 1 = 3 rows (8, 9, 10).
    const rowsToClear = lastRow - 8 + 1;
    
    targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, rowsToClear, 17).clearContent(); 
    Logger.log(`Cleared old data from A8:Q${lastRow}`);
  } else {
    Logger.log("No data found to clear (last row is less than 8).");
  }

  Utilities.sleep(5000);

  // --- 3. Get Source Data ---
  let sourceSs;
  try {
    sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('File Access Error', `Could not open source file.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const sourceDataSheet = sourceSs.getSheets()[0]; 
  if (!sourceDataSheet) {
    ui.alert('Sheet Error', 'Could not find the first sheet in the source file.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const sourceLastRow = sourceDataSheet.getLastRow();
  if (sourceLastRow < 3) { 
    ui.alert('No Data', 'Source file has no data to import (less than 3 rows).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 4. Read data from source (using getDisplayValues to capture exact text) ---
  const sourceRange = sourceDataSheet.getRange(3, 1, sourceLastRow - 2, 6);
  const sourceValues = sourceRange.getDisplayValues();
  
  // --- CLEANING LOOP (No Zero Manipulation) ---
  for (let r = 0; r < sourceValues.length; r++) {
    for (let c = 0; c < sourceValues[r].length; c++) {
      let val = sourceValues[r][c];
      
      // Force string, remove quotes and non-breaking spaces
      if (!val || String(val).trim() === "") {
        sourceValues[r][c] = "";
      } else {
        sourceValues[r][c] = String(val).replace(/"/g, "").replace(/\u00A0/g, " ").trim();
      }
    }
  }

  // --- 5. Write clean data BACK to the source file as Plain Text ---
  sourceRange.setNumberFormat("@"); 
  sourceRange.setValues(sourceValues); 

  // --- 6. Write to Target Sheet (Column B / 2) as Plain Text (Values Only) ---
  const destinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(8, 2, sourceValues.length, sourceValues[0].length); 
  destinationRange.setNumberFormat("@");
  destinationRange.setValues(sourceValues);

  targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate();
  ss.toast('Die Daten wurden erfolgreich importiert! Klicke jetzt auf "DATEN GENERIEREN".', 'Erfolg!', 10);
}

IMPORT_DATA_Rohdaten Allg. Sortimentsw..gs
/**
 * Imports raw data for General Assortment Wishes ('Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche').
 * Replicates VBA macro 'ImportRohdatenAllgemeineSortimentswünscheFood'.
 */
function importRawGeneralAssortment() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Allg. Sortimentsw.");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importRawGeneralAssortment ---");

  if (!settingsSheet || !targetSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Rohdaten Allg. Sortimentsw." sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche"; // Source file name for this sheet
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; // Case-insensitive compare
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F (assuming standard layout)
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileUrl) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file URL for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File URL for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
  
  try {
    const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
    if (match && match[1]) {
      sourceFileId = match[1]; 
      Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
    } else {
      throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
    }
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
    return;
  }

  // --- 2. Prepare Target Sheet ---
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow >= 8) {
    // Clear A8:K as per VBA
    targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, lastRow - 7, 11).clearContent(); 
    Logger.log(`Cleared old data from A8:K${lastRow}`);
  }

  // --- 3. Get Source Data ---
  try {
    const sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
    // VBA uses Worksheets(1), assuming it's the first sheet
    const sourceDataSheet = sourceSs.getSheets()[0]; 
    if (!sourceDataSheet) {
      ui.alert('Sheet Error', 'Could not find the first sheet in the source file.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }

    const sourceLastRow = sourceDataSheet.getLastRow();
    if (sourceLastRow < 3) { // VBA checks lr > 2
      ui.alert('No Data', 'Source file has no data to import (checked below row 2).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }

    // --- 4. Copy data from source A3:A -> target B8 ---
    const sourceRange = sourceDataSheet.getRange(3, 1, sourceLastRow - 2, 1); // A3:A<last>
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();

    // --- START: Perfected Cleaning Loop ---
    // Note: Since this import is only 1 column, only the c === 0 logic will apply.
    Logger.log("Starting data cleaning loop...");
    for (let r = 0; r < sourceValues.length; r++) {
      for (let c = 0; c < sourceValues[r].length; c++) {

        let cellValue = sourceValues[r][c];

        // 1. Specific fix for Col G (WG), which is c === 0 (the first column)
        if (c === 0) {
          // First, clean it up if it's a string to remove spaces, quotes, etc.
          if (typeof cellValue === 'string') {
            cellValue = cellValue.replace(/"/g, "")
              .replace(/\u00A0/g, " ")
              .trim();
          }

          // Now, check if the (potentially cleaned) value is numeric
          let numericValue;
          if (typeof cellValue === 'number') {
            numericValue = cellValue;
          } else if (typeof cellValue === 'string' && cellValue !== "") {
            // Replace comma with dot for robust parsing, then parse
            const parsableString = cellValue.replace(',', '.');
            numericValue = parseFloat(parsableString);
          } else {
            // It's an empty string or some other type, not a number
            numericValue = NaN;
          }

          // If it's a valid finite number, format it to 2 decimal places.
          // isFinite() handles NaN and Infinity
          if (isFinite(numericValue)) {
            sourceValues[r][c] = numericValue.toFixed(2); // e.g., 30.1 -> "30.10"
          } else {
            // It's not a number (e.g., "N/A" or was empty), just assign the cleaned string
            // If it was a number originally (like Infinity), convert to string
            sourceValues[r][c] = (typeof cellValue === 'string') ? cellValue : String(cellValue);
          }
        }
        // 2. Clean all other string values (c > 0)
        else if (typeof cellValue === 'string') {
          sourceValues[r][c] = cellValue.replace(/"/g, "")         // 1. Remove all quotes
            .replace(/\u00A0/g, " ") // 2. Replace non-breaking spaces
            .trim();                 // 3. Remove all leading/trailing spaces
        }
      }
    }
    Logger.log("Data cleaning loop finished.");
    // --- END: Perfected Cleaning Loop ---

    // --- Write clean data BACK to the source file ---
    Logger.log("Writing clean data back to source file...");
    sourceRange.setNumberFormat("@"); // Set source column to Plain Text
    sourceRange.setValues(sourceValues); // Paste clean values back
    Logger.log("Source file successfully cleaned.");
    // --- End of "write-back" code ---

    const destinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(8, 2, sourceValues.length, 1); // B8:B...

    // --- Force target column B to Plain Text ---
    Logger.log("Setting destination column B to Plain Text format.");
    destinationRange.setNumberFormat("@");

    destinationRange.setValues(sourceValues);
    Logger.log(`Successfully imported ${sourceValues.length} rows into Column B.`);

    // VBA doesn't update formulas here, it happens in the next step.

    targetSheet.getRange("C1").activate(); // Activate C1 as per VBA's Range("C1").Select
    ss.toast('Die Daten wurden erfolgreich importiert! Klicke jetzt auf "DATEN GENERIEREN".', 'Erfolg!', 10);

  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred during import: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Import Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
  Logger.log("--- Finished importRawGeneralAssortment ---");
}

/**
 * 🔎 Imports raw data for 'Rohdaten Food Qualitätsfälle'.
 * FIX: Plain Text method + Paste Values Only (Preserves existing borders/colors).
 * Removes destructive .toFixed(3) logic that was altering WG codes.
 */
function importRawFoodQualityCases() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Food Qualitätsfälle");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importRawFoodQualityCases (Strict Plain Text) ---");
  if (!settingsSheet || !targetSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Required sheets missing.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Qualitätsfälle";
  let sourceFileId = null;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' };

    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      sourceFileId = settingsValues[i][4];
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

// --- Prepare Target Sheet (Clear CONTENT only to preserve borders/colors) ---
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getLastRow(); 
  
  if (lastRow >= 8) {
    targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, lastRow - 7, 25).clearContent();
  }

  let sourceSs;
  try {
    sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('File Access Error', `Could not open source file.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }
  
  const sourceDataSheet = sourceSs.getSheetByName("In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F");
  if (!sourceDataSheet) {
    ui.alert('Sheet Error', 'Tab not found.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }
  const sourceLastRow = sourceDataSheet.getLastRow();
  if (sourceLastRow < 3) return;

  // --- Read Data (using getDisplayValues to capture exact text) ---
  const sourceRange = sourceDataSheet.getRange(3, 1, sourceLastRow - 2, 8);
  const sourceValues = sourceRange.getDisplayValues();

  // --- CLEANING LOOP (No Zero Manipulation) ---
  for (let r = 0; r < sourceValues.length; r++) {
    for (let c = 0; c < sourceValues[r].length; c++) {
      let val = sourceValues[r][c];
      
      // Force string, remove quotes and non-breaking spaces
      if (!val || String(val).trim() === "") {
        sourceValues[r][c] = "";
      } else {
        sourceValues[r][c] = String(val).replace(/"/g, "").replace(/\u00A0/g, " ").trim();
      }
    }
  }

  // --- 1. Write clean data BACK to the source file as Plain Text ---
  sourceRange.setNumberFormat("@");
  sourceRange.setValues(sourceValues);

  // --- 2. Write to Target Sheet (Column G / 7) as Plain Text (Values Only) ---
  const destinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(8, 7, sourceValues.length, sourceValues[0].length); 
  destinationRange.setNumberFormat("@");
  destinationRange.setValues(sourceValues); // setValues inherently acts like "Paste Values Only"
  
  targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate();
  ss.toast('Import successful! Data formatted perfectly as Plain Text.', 'Success', 5);
}
