/**
 * 🔎 Imports raw data for Sorting Arrangement Wishes ('Änderungswünsche Sortierung').
 * FIX: Plain Text method + Dynamic Border Formatting.
 * UPDATE: Aggressively clears ALL borders and content from Row 8 to the very bottom of the sheet.
 */
function importChangeWishesSorting() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Änderungswünsche Sort.");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importChangeWishesSorting (Strict Plain Text + MaxRow Clear) ---");

  if (!settingsSheet || !targetSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Required sheets missing.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- Find Source File ID ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Änderungswünsche Sortierung";
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' };

    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
      (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      sourceFileId = settingsValues[i][4]; // File ID in Column E
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- Prepare Target Sheet (THE BORDER FIX) ---
  const maxRows = targetSheet.getMaxRows(); // Gets the absolute bottom of the sheet
  if (maxRows >= 8) {
    // Clear everything (content & borders) from Row 8 down to the absolute bottom, spanning 18 columns
    const clearRange = targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, maxRows - 7, 18);
    clearRange.clearContent();
  }

  // --- Get Source Data ---
  let sourceSs;
  try {
    sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('File Access Error', `Could not open source file.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const sourceDataSheet = sourceSs.getSheetByName("In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F");
  if (!sourceDataSheet) {
    ui.alert('Sheet Error', 'Tab "In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F" not found.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const sourceLastRow = sourceDataSheet.getLastRow();
  if (sourceLastRow < 3) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'Source file has no data.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- Read Data (using getDisplayValues to capture exact text) ---
  const sourceRange = sourceDataSheet.getRange(3, 1, sourceLastRow - 2, 4);
  const sourceValues = sourceRange.getDisplayValues(); 

  // --- CLEANING LOOP (No Zero Manipulation) ---
  for (let r = 0; r < sourceValues.length; r++) {
    for (let c = 0; c < sourceValues[r].length; c++) {
      let val = sourceValues[r][c];
      
      // Force string, remove quotes and non-breaking spaces
      if (!val || String(val).trim() === "") {
        sourceValues[r][c] = "";
      } else {
        sourceValues[r][c] = String(val).replace(/"/g, "").replace(/\u00A0/g, " ").trim();
      }
    }
  }

  // --- 1. Write clean data BACK to the source file as Plain Text ---
  sourceRange.setNumberFormat("@");
  sourceRange.setValues(sourceValues); 

  // --- 2. Write to Target Sheet (Column F / 6) as Plain Text ---
  const destinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(8, 6, sourceValues.length, sourceValues[0].length);
  destinationRange.setNumberFormat("@");
  destinationRange.setValues(sourceValues);

  // --- 3. Apply Formatting (Borders/Fonts/Colors) from Row 6 ---
  const formatTemplate = targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, 1, 18); // A6:R6
  const targetFormatRange = targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, sourceValues.length, 18);
  formatTemplate.copyTo(targetFormatRange, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);

  updateRohdatenChangeWishesFormulas(foundRowNumber);

  targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate();
  ss.toast('Import successful!', 'Success', 5);
}

/**
 * 🔄 Dynamically updates the template formula in 'Rohdaten Änderungswünsche Sort.'
 */
function updateRohdatenChangeWishesFormulas(foundRowNumber) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Änderungswünsche Sort.");
  if (!targetSheet) return;

  const urlCellReference = `Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber}`;
  const sheetName = 'In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F';

  const newFormulaForJ6 = `=LET(` +
    `url;${urlCellReference};` +
    `sheet_name;"${sheetName}";` +
    `data_range;IMPORTRANGE(url;"'"&sheet_name&"'!E3:Q1000");` +
    `criteria1_range;IMPORTRANGE(url;"'"&sheet_name&"'!B3:B1000");` +
    `criteria2_range;IMPORTRANGE(url;"'"&sheet_name&"'!C3:C1000");` +
    `header_range;IMPORTRANGE(url;"'"&sheet_name&"'!E1:Q1");` +
    `filtered_row;IFERROR(FILTER(data_range;TO_TEXT(criteria1_range)=TO_TEXT($G6);criteria2_range=$H6));` +
    `IF(ISBLANK(filtered_row);"";IFERROR(IF(J$5=J$4;INDEX(filtered_row;1;MATCH(J$5;header_range;0));N(INDEX(filtered_row;1;MATCH(J$5;header_range;0)))+N(INDEX(filtered_row;1;MATCH(J$4;header_range;0))))))` +
    `)`;

  const templateFormulaCell = targetSheet.getRange("J6");
  templateFormulaCell.setFormula(newFormulaForJ6);

  const fullTemplateRange = targetSheet.getRange("J6:Q6");
  templateFormulaCell.autoFill(fullTemplateRange, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
}

/**
 * 🔎 Imports raw data for Food Assortment Wishes.
 * FIX: Uses getDisplayValues() and Plain Text format ("@") on both SOURCE and TARGET 
 * to ensure WG and CW columns remain exactly as they are without zero or date manipulation.
 */
function importFoodAssortmentWishes() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche");
  
  Logger.log("--- Starting importFoodAssortmentWishes (Strict Plain Text) ---");

  if (!settingsSheet || !targetSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Required sheets missing.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- Find Source File ID ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Sortimentswünsche";
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' };

    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
      (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      sourceFileId = settingsValues[i][4];
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found in Settings.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- Prepare Target ---
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow >= 8) {
    targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, lastRow - 7, 18).clearContent();
  }

  // --- Get Source Data ---
  let sourceSs;
  try {
    sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('File Access Error', `Could not open source file: ${e.message}`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }
  
  const sourceDataSheet = sourceSs.getSheetByName("In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F");
  if (!sourceDataSheet) {
    ui.alert('Sheet Error', 'Tab "In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F" not found.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const sourceLastRow = sourceDataSheet.getLastRow();
  if (sourceLastRow < 3) return;

  // Read Data using DisplayValues to capture exact text representation (preserves "30.10" and "2026-01")
  const sourceRange = sourceDataSheet.getRange(3, 1, sourceLastRow - 2, 4);
  const sourceValues = sourceRange.getDisplayValues(); 

  // --- CLEANING LOOP (No Zero Manipulation) ---
  for (let r = 0; r < sourceValues.length; r++) {
    for (let c = 0; c < sourceValues[r].length; c++) {
      let val = sourceValues[r][c];
      
      // Force it to be a strict string, remove double quotes, remove non-breaking spaces, and trim
      if (!val || String(val).trim() === "") {
        sourceValues[r][c] = "";
      } else {
        sourceValues[r][c] = String(val).replace(/"/g, "").replace(/\u00A0/g, " ").trim();
      }
    }
  }

  // --- 1. Write back to Source as Plain Text ---
  sourceRange.setNumberFormat("@"); 
  sourceRange.setValues(sourceValues);

  // --- 2. Write to Target as Plain Text ---
  const destinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(8, 6, sourceValues.length, sourceValues[0].length); 
  destinationRange.setNumberFormat("@"); 
  destinationRange.setValues(sourceValues);
  
  updateRohdatenFoodFormulas(foundRowNumber);

  targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate();
  ss.toast('Import successful! WG and CW columns sanitized as Plain Text.', 'Success', 5);
}

function updateRohdatenFoodFormulas(foundRowNumber) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Food Sortimentswünsche");
  if (!targetSheet) return;

  const newFormulaForJ6 = `=ARRAY_CONSTRAIN(ARRAYFORMULA(IFERROR(IF(J$5=J$4;INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$Q$1000");MATCH(1;($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$B$1000"))*($H6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$1000"));0);MATCH(J$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$1:$Q$1");0));IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$Q$1000");MATCH(1;($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$B$1000"))*($H6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$1000"));0);MATCH(J$5;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$1:$Q$1");0)));0)+IFERROR(NUMBERVALUE(INDEX(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$3:$Q$1000");MATCH(1;($G6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$B$3:$B$1000"))*($H6=IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$C$3:$C$1000"));0);MATCH(J$4;IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber};"In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F!$E$1:$Q$1");0)));0));"")); 1; 1)`;

  const templateFormulaCell = targetSheet.getRange("J6");
  templateFormulaCell.setFormula(newFormulaForJ6);
  const fullTemplateRange = targetSheet.getRange("J6:Q6");
  templateFormulaCell.autoFill(fullTemplateRange, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
}
IMPORT_DATA_Rohdaten_OG_Qualif_o_LFN.gs
/**
 * 🔎 Imports raw data for 'Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'ImportRohdatenOGQualitätsfälleohneLFN' (Modul42).
 * V1: Fixes bug where sourceFileId was never assigned.
 */
function importRawOGQualityCasesNoLFN() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importRawOGQualityCasesNoLFN (V1 - ID Fix) ---");

  if (!settingsSheet || !targetSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_O+G_DE_Qualitätsfälle (ohne LFN)"; // Source file name for this sheet
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null; // This variable must be assigned
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; 
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      // --- START OF FIX ---
      // Extract the ID from the URL and assign it to sourceFileId
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
        return;
      }
      // --- END OF FIX ---
      break; // Exit loop once found
    }
  }

  // This check will now pass
  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }

  // // --- 2. Prepare Target Sheet (Clear A8:Q<lastRow>) ---
  // // VBA checks last row of column E ("Artikel")
  // const lastRow = targetSheet.getRange("E" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
  // if (lastRow >= 8) { // Data starts at row 8
  //   targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, lastRow - 7, 17).clearContent(); // A8:Q<lastRow>
  //   Logger.log(`Cleared old data from A8:Q${lastRow}`);
  // }

    // 1. Get the actual last row with content in the entire sheet
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getLastRow(); 

  // 2. Check if that last row is at or beyond your starting point (Row 8)
  if (lastRow >= 8) {
    // We calculate the number of rows to clear: (Total - Start + 1)
    // For example: if lastRow is 10, we clear 10 - 8 + 1 = 3 rows (8, 9, 10).
    const rowsToClear = lastRow - 8 + 1;
    
    targetSheet.getRange(8, 1, rowsToClear, 17).clearContent(); 
    Logger.log(`Cleared old data from A8:Q${lastRow}`);
  } else {
    Logger.log("No data found to clear (last row is less than 8).");
  }

  // --- 3. Get Source Data ---
  try {
    const sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
    // The VBA macro (Modul42) uses worksheet 1
    const sourceDataSheet = sourceSs.getSheets()[0]; // Use the first sheet
    if (!sourceDataSheet) {
      ui.alert('Sheet Error', 'Could not find the first sheet in the source file.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }
    Logger.log(`Using source sheet: ${sourceDataSheet.getName()}`);

    const sourceLastRow = sourceDataSheet.getLastRow();
    if (sourceLastRow < 3) {
      ui.alert('No Data', 'Source file has no data to import (less than 3 rows).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }

    // --- 4. Copy data from source and paste to target ---
    // VBA: wb.Worksheets(1).Range("A3:F" & lr).Copy
    // VBA: ...Worksheets("Rohdaten O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN").Range("B8").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues
    const sourceRange = sourceDataSheet.getRange(3, 1, sourceLastRow - 2, 6); // A3:F<sourceLastRow>
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();
    
    // Paste into B8 (row 8, column 2)
    const destinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(8, 2, sourceValues.length, sourceValues[0].length); // B8:G<lastRow>

    // --- !! ADDED LINE TO OVERWRITE DESTINATION FORMATS !! ---
    // Set destination to Plain Text to ignore any pre-existing formats
    destinationRange.setNumberFormat("@"); 
    // --- !! END OF ADDED LINE !! ---

    destinationRange.setValues(sourceValues);
    Logger.log(`Successfully imported ${sourceValues.length} rows of data into B8:G${7 + sourceValues.length - 1}.`);
    
    targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate(); // Activate E2 as per VBA
    ss.toast('Die Daten wurden erfolgreich importiert! Klicke jetzt auf "DATEN GENERIEREN".', 'Erfolg!', 10);
  
  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Import Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
  Logger.log("--- Finished importRawOGQualityCasesNoLFN ---");
}

/**
 * 🔎 Imports raw data for 'Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'ImportRohdatenSonstigesFoodundAktuelleThemen' (Modul30).
 * This script only copies data; it does not update any template formulas.
 */
function importRawOtherFoodTopics() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importRawOtherFoodTopics ---");

  if (!settingsSheet || !targetSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find "Einstellungen" or "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Source File ID Row ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow()).getValues();
  const searchFileName = "8WS_Food_DE_Sonstiges und aktuelle Themen"; // Source file name for this sheet
  let sourceFileUrl = null;
  let sourceFileId = null;
  let foundRowNumber = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    const cellA = settingsValues[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = settingsValues[i][1].toString().trim();
    const excelFileName = searchFileName + ".xlsx";
    const options = { sensitivity: 'base' }; 
    if ((cellA && cellA.localeCompare(searchFileName, undefined, options) === 0) ||
        (cellB && cellB.localeCompare(excelFileName, undefined, options) === 0)) {
      
      foundRowNumber = i + 1;
      sourceFileUrl = settingsValues[i][5]; // Get the URL from Column F
      Logger.log(`Found source file URL on row: ${foundRowNumber}: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
      
      // --- START OF FIX ---
      // Extract the ID from the URL and assign it to sourceFileId
      try {
        const match = sourceFileUrl.match(/\/d\/(.+?)\//);
        if (match && match[1]) {
          sourceFileId = match[1];
          Logger.log(`Successfully extracted File ID: ${sourceFileId}`);
        } else {
          throw new Error("Could not parse File ID from URL.");
        }
      } catch (e) {
        ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Invalid Google Sheet URL found for "${searchFileName}".`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        Logger.log(`Error: Could not extract File ID from URL: ${sourceFileUrl}`);
        return;
      }
      // --- END OF FIX ---
      break; // Exit loop once found
    }
  }

  if (!sourceFileId) {
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find the file ID for "${searchFileName}". Check the 'Einstellungen' sheet.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`Error: File ID for "${searchFileName}" not found.`);
    return;
  }

  // --- 2. Prepare Target Sheet (Clear A7:R<lastRow>) ---
  // VBA checks last row of column E ("Thema")
  const lastRow = targetSheet.getRange("E" + targetSheet.getMaxRows()).getNextDataCell(SpreadsheetApp.Direction.UP).getRow();
  if (lastRow >= 7) {
    targetSheet.getRange(7, 1, lastRow - 6, 18).clearContent(); // A7:R<lastRow>
    Logger.log(`Cleared old data from A7:R${lastRow}`);
  }

  // --- 3. Get Source Data ---
  try {
    const sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
    // The VBA macro (Modul30) uses worksheet 1, which we assume is 'In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F'
    const sourceDataSheet = sourceSs.getSheetByName("In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F"); 
    if (!sourceDataSheet) {
      ui.alert('Sheet Error', 'Could not find "In_Development_8_weeks_Report_F" in source.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }

    const sourceLastRow = sourceDataSheet.getLastRow();
    if (sourceLastRow < 3) {
      ui.alert('No Data', 'Source file has no data to import (less than 3 rows).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }

    // --- 4. Copy data from source and paste to target ---
    // VBA: wb.Worksheets(1).Range("A3:A" & lr).Copy
    // VBA: Workbooks("...").Worksheets("Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen").Range("E7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues
    const sourceRange = sourceDataSheet.getRange(3, 1, sourceLastRow - 2, 1); // Column A, from row 3
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();
    
    const destinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(7, 5, sourceValues.length, 1); // Column E, from row 7

    destinationRange.setValues(sourceValues);
    Logger.log(`Successfully imported ${sourceValues.length} rows of data into Column E.`);
    
    // No formula update function is called in this VBA macro.

    targetSheet.getRange("E2").activate(); // Activate E2 as per VBA
    ss.toast('Die Daten wurden erfolgreich importiert! Bitte fülle Spalten P & Q manuell aus und klicke dann auf "DATEN GENERIEREN".', 'Erfolg!', 15);
  
  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Import Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
  Logger.log("--- Finished importRawOtherFoodTopics ---");
}
IMPORT_DATA_Änderungswünsche Sortierung_import.gs
/**
 * Imports and processes data from 'Rohdaten Änderungswünsche Sort.' to 'Änderungswünsche Sortierung'.
 * Replicates VBA macro 'Daten_Aus_RohdatenÄnderungswünscheSort_Importieren'.
 * Key difference: De-duplicates based on BOTH Artikelnummer (Col F) AND Artikel (Col G).
 */
function importToChangeWishesSorting() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sourceSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Rohdaten Änderungswünsche Sort.");
  const destSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Änderungswünsche Sortierung");

  Logger.log("--- Starting importToChangeWishesSorting ---");

  if (!sourceSheet || !destSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Could not find the source ("Rohdaten...") or destination ("Änderungswünsche Sortierung") sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Error: A required sheet is missing.');
    return;
  }

// Check source sheet using Column H (Artikel) as per VBA
  const columnHValues = sourceSheet.getRange("H1:H" + sourceSheet.getMaxRows()).getValues();
  let sourceLastRow = 0;
  for (let i = columnHValues.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (String(columnHValues[i][0]).trim() !== "") {
      sourceLastRow = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (sourceLastRow < 8) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'The "Rohdaten Änderungswünsche Sort." sheet has no data to import (checked Col H).', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log('Warning: No data to process on the source sheet.');
    // Optional: Add redirect logic here if needed
    return;
  }
  Logger.log(`Found data up to row ${sourceLastRow} on source sheet.`);

  try {
    // --- 1. Clear Old Data Content ---
    const destLastRow = destSheet.getLastRow();
    if (destLastRow >= 6) {
      Logger.log(`Clearing old content from A6:R${destLastRow} in 'Änderungswünsche Sortierung'.`);
      destSheet.getRange("A6:R" + destLastRow).clearContent();
    }

    // --- 2. Read, Re-order, and De-duplicate Data in Memory ---
    Logger.log("Reading source data...");
    // Read all relevant columns (A to H) from the source sheet at once.
    const sourceRange = sourceSheet.getRange("A8:H" + sourceLastRow);
    const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();

    const uniqueKeys = new Set(); // Use a Set to track unique combinations
    const processedData = [];

    Logger.log("Processing and de-duplicating data based on Artikelnummer AND Artikel...");
    for (const row of sourceValues) {
      const artikelNummer = row[4]; // Column E (becomes Col F in dest)
      const artikel = row[7];       // Column H (becomes Col G in dest)
      const uniqueKey = `${artikelNummer}|||${artikel}`; // Combine both for uniqueness check
      
      // If we haven't seen this combination before, process it.
      if (!uniqueKeys.has(uniqueKey)) {
        processedData.push([
          row[0], // Column A -> A
          row[1], // Column B -> B
          row[2], // Column C -> C
          row[3], // Column D -> D
          row[5], // Column F -> E ('Artikelnummer QUELLE')
          artikelNummer, // Column E -> F ('Artikelnummer') - Part 1 of key
          artikel,       // Column H -> G ('Artikel') - Part 2 of key
        ]);
        uniqueKeys.add(uniqueKey);
      }
    }
    Logger.log(`Finished processing. Found ${processedData.length} unique rows.`);
    
    if (processedData.length === 0) {
        ui.alert('No Data', 'No unique data rows were found to import.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
        return;
    }

    // --- 3. Write Processed Data to Destination ---
    Logger.log("Writing processed data to 'Änderungswünsche Sortierung' sheet (A:G).");
    destSheet.getRange(6, 1, processedData.length, 7).setValues(processedData);
    
    const newLastRow = 5 + processedData.length;

    // --- 4. Apply Formulas using a Format-Preserving Method ---
    Logger.log(`Applying formulas from H3:R3 to H6:R${newLastRow} using R1C1 notation.`);
    const formulaTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("H3:R3");
    const templateFormulas = formulaTemplateRange.getFormulasR1C1()[0]; 

    if (templateFormulas.join('').length > 0) {
        const numRows = newLastRow - 5;
        const formulasForRange = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < numRows; i++) {
            formulasForRange.push(templateFormulas);
        }
        
        const formulaDestinationRange = destSheet.getRange("H6:R" + newLastRow);
        formulaDestinationRange.setFormulasR1C1(formulasForRange);
    } else {
        Logger.log("Warning: No formulas found in template range H3:R3.");
    }
    
    // --- 5. Wait for Calculations and Convert to Values ---
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Logger.log("Waiting for formulas to calculate...");
    Utilities.sleep(5000);

    Logger.log(`Converting formulas in H6:R${newLastRow} to static values.`);
    const rangeToConvert = destSheet.getRange("H6:R" + newLastRow);
    rangeToConvert.copyTo(rangeToConvert, { contentsOnly: true });

    // --- 6. Sort the Data ---
    Logger.log("Sorting the data...");
    const fullDataRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:R" + newLastRow); 
    
    fullDataRange.sort({ column: 7, ascending: true }); // First sort: by Column G
    fullDataRange.sort([ // Second sort: multi-level
        { column: 1, ascending: true },
        { column: 2, ascending: true },
        { column: 3, ascending: true }
    ]);

    // --- 7. Apply Formatting (Mimicking VBA) ---
    // Although setFormulasR1C1 preserves format, the VBA explicitly reapplies it.
    Logger.log("Applying formatting from template row A6:R6 to all new rows.");
    const formatTemplateRange = destSheet.getRange("A6:R6");
    if (newLastRow > 6) {
        const formatDestination = destSheet.getRange("A7:R" + newLastRow);
        formatTemplateRange.copyTo(formatDestination, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
    }
    
    // --- 8. Cleanup: Lösche alles unterhalb der formatierten/sortierten Daten ---
    const maxRows = destSheet.getMaxRows();
    if (maxRows > newLastRow) {
        // Löscht alles ab der ersten leeren Zeile bis ganz unten. 
        // Spalten A bis R = 18 Spalten
        destSheet.getRange(newLastRow + 1, 1, maxRows - newLastRow, 18).clear();
        Logger.log(`Tabelle von Zeile ${newLastRow + 1} bis ${maxRows} komplett gesäubert.`);
    }

    destSheet.getRange("A1").activate(); // Activate A1 as per VBA
    navigateOnSuccess();
    Logger.log("--- Finished importToChangeWishesSorting ---");
    
    // Optional: Add redirect logic here if needed (e.g., activate another sheet)

  } catch (e) {
    const errorMessage = `An error occurred: ${e.message}\n\nStack:\n${e.stack}`;
    ui.alert('Processing Error', errorMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.stack}`);
  }
}

/**
 * 💡 Smarter MIS Import Trigger
 * Populates data from "WE-Menge pro Artikel-Lieferant"
 * Updates formula referencing "Abverkauf bereinigt pro Artikel"
 */
function runMisImportSmarter() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  
  if (!settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Sheet "Einstellungen" could not be found.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const dataRange = settingsSheet.getRange("A1:F" + settingsSheet.getLastRow());
  const values = dataRange.getValues();
  
  // Define our two distinct search targets
  const searchTextData = "WE-Menge pro Artikel-Lieferant";
  const searchTextFormula = "Abverkauf bereinigt pro Artikel";
  
  let misFileId = null;
  let formulaRowIndex = -1;

  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    const cellA = values[i][0].toString().trim();
    const cellB = values[i][1].toString().trim();

    // 1. Find Data Source (WE-Menge) -> Get File ID from Col E [4]
    if (cellA.includes(searchTextData) || cellB.includes(searchTextData)) {
      misFileId = values[i][4]; 
      Logger.log(`Found Data File ID (WE-Menge) at row ${i + 1}: ${misFileId}`);
    }
    
    // 2. Find Formula Source (Abverkauf) -> Get Row Index for URL in Col F
    if (cellA.includes(searchTextFormula) || cellB.includes(searchTextFormula)) {
      formulaRowIndex = i + 1; 
      Logger.log(`Found Formula File (Abverkauf) at row ${formulaRowIndex}`);
    }
  }

  // --- Proceed only if BOTH rows were found ---
  if (misFileId && formulaRowIndex > 0) {
    
    const misFinalSheet = ss.getSheetByName("MIS Final");
    if (!misFinalSheet) {
      ui.alert('Error', 'Sheet "MIS Final" could not be found.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }
    
    // The exact tab name inside the Abverkauf sheet
    const targetTabName = "8 W S DE Food - Abverkauf berei"; 
    
    // ⚠️ CRITICAL FIX: Used commas (,) instead of semicolons (;) for Apps Script compatibility.
    // Apps Script will automatically translate these to semicolons in your German Google Sheet.
    const newFormula = `=XLOOKUP(IFERROR(A4*1; A4); ARRAYFORMULA(IFERROR(IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${formulaRowIndex}; "'${targetTabName}'!A:A")*1; IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${formulaRowIndex}; "'${targetTabName}'!A:A"))); IMPORTRANGE(Einstellungen!$F$${formulaRowIndex}; "'${targetTabName}'!C:C"); 0; 0; 1)`;
    
    
    try {
      // Set the new formula in cell F4
      misFinalSheet.getRange("F4").setFormula(newFormula);
    } catch (e) {
      ui.alert('Formula Error', `Could not update the formula in 'MIS Final'!F4. Error: ${e.message}`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }

    // --- 3. Run the main data import process using the WE-Menge ID ---
    importAndProcessMisData(misFileId); 
    
    // --- 4. Update Deckblatts ---
    updateDeckblattFoodFormulas();
    updateDeckblattNonFoodFormulas();
    updateDeckblatt_O_G_Formulas();

  } else {
    // Show an error if either row wasn't found
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find both configuration rows in the "Einstellungen" sheet.\n\nMake sure both "WE-Menge" and "Abverkauf" are listed.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  }
}


/**
 * 📋 Imports MIS data, pastes it, and correctly processes formula columns.
 * This version includes SpreadsheetApp.flush() to ensure calculations are
 * complete before converting formulas to values.
 *
 * @param {string} sourceFileId The Google Drive ID of the source MIS Google Sheet.
 */
function importAndProcessMisData(sourceFileId) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName("MIS Final");
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  if (!targetSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Target sheet "MIS Final" could not be found.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  let sourceSs;
  try {
    sourceSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(sourceFileId);
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('File Error', `Could not open the source file with ID: ${sourceFileId}. Please check the ID and your permissions.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const sourceSheet = sourceSs.getSheets()[0];
  const sourceLastRow = sourceSheet.getLastRow();

  if (sourceLastRow < 2) {
    ui.alert('No Data', 'The source MIS file contains no data to import.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const sourceRange = sourceSheet.getRange(2, 1, sourceLastRow - 1, 4); // A2:D<lastRow>
  const sourceValues = sourceRange.getValues();
  
  // Paste the initial data into columns A:D
  targetSheet.getRange(6, 1, sourceValues.length, sourceValues[0].length).setValues(sourceValues);

  // Determine the last row of the newly pasted data
  const newLastRow = 5 + sourceValues.length;
  
  // --- Process the formulas for columns E:G ---
  if (newLastRow >= 6) {
    // 1. Get the range for the template formulas (E4:G4)
    const formulaTemplateRange = targetSheet.getRange("E4:G4");
    // 2. Define the destination range for the formulas (e.g., E6:G100)
    const formulaDestinationRange = targetSheet.getRange(6, 5, newLastRow - 5, 3);

    // 3. "Drag and drop" the formulas into the destination range.
    // This correctly increments the cell references (A4 -> A6, A7, etc.)
    formulaTemplateRange.copyTo(formulaDestinationRange);

    // ✅ **THE CRITICAL FIX:** This command forces the sheet to finish all calculations
    // before the script continues. This solves the #VALUE! error.
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();

    // 4. Now that calculations are done, get the final display values (the numbers)
    const calculatedValues = formulaDestinationRange.getDisplayValues();
    
    // 5. Paste the final numbers over the formulas, making them static values
    formulaDestinationRange.setValues(calculatedValues);
    formulaDestinationRange.setFontColor('black');
    formulaDestinationRange.setBackground('white');
  }
  
  targetSheet.getRange("D1").activate();
  //ui.alert('Import Complete', 'The MIS data was successfully imported and processed!', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  navigateOnSuccess();
}

/**
 * Converts German umlauts and ß to their simple ASCII equivalents for robust matching.
 * V2: Adds Unicode Normalization (NFC) and removes non-alphanumeric chars.
 */
function normalizeGermanUmlauts(str) {
  if (typeof str !== 'string') return str;
  return str.normalize('NFC') 
            .toUpperCase()
            .replace(/Ä/g, 'A').replace(/Ö/g, 'O').replace(/Ü/g, 'U').replace(/ß/g, 'S')
            .replace(/[^A-Z0-9]/g, ''); 
}

/**
 * Converts Excel files and updates existing Google Sheets.
 * Includes a mandatory "Un-mangle" step to fix Google's aggressive date auto-formatting.
 */
function convertExcelFilesToSheets() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getActiveSheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  try {
    // --- 1. Get file names from the sheet (Input is in B4:B17) ---
    const fileNamesRange = sheet.getRange("B4:B17");
    const fileNamesValues = fileNamesRange.getValues();
    const namesMap = new Map(); 

    fileNamesValues.flat().forEach(name => {
      const trimmedName = name.toString().trim();
      if (trimmedName.length >= 3) {
        let baseName = trimmedName;
        if (trimmedName.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xlsx')) baseName = trimmedName.slice(0, -5);
        else if (trimmedName.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xls')) baseName = trimmedName.slice(0, -4);

        const robustName = normalizeGermanUmlauts(baseName);
        if (robustName.length >= 3) {
          namesMap.set(robustName, trimmedName);
        }
      }
    });

    if (namesMap.size === 0) {
      ui.alert('No Files Listed', 'No valid file names were found in cells B4:B17.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }

    // --- 2. Get the folder URL and Folder ID ---
    const folderUrl = sheet.getRange("B19").getValue();
    if (!folderUrl || !folderUrl.includes('drive.google.com/')) {
      ui.alert("Folder Link Missing", "Please paste the full Google Drive folder link into cell B19.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      return;
    }
    const folderId = folderUrl.split('/').pop().split('?')[0];

    // --- 3. List all files in the folder (Drive API) ---
    let processedCount = 0;
    const finalFileIds = new Map(); 
    let allFilesInFolder = [];
    
    let pageToken;
    do {
      const listResult = Drive.Files.list({
        q: `'${folderId}' in parents and trashed = false`,
        corpora: "allDrives",
        supportsAllDrives: true,
        includeItemsFromAllDrives: true,
        pageToken: pageToken,
        pageSize: 1000
      });
      if (listResult.items) { allFilesInFolder.push(...listResult.items); }
      pageToken = listResult.nextPageToken;
    } while (pageToken);

    const excelFilesToProcess = allFilesInFolder.filter(file => {
      const isExcel = file.title.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xlsx') || file.title.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xls');
      if (isExcel) {
        const baseNameRaw = file.title.replace(/\.xlsx$/i, '').replace(/\.xls$/i, '');
        return namesMap.has(normalizeGermanUmlauts(baseNameRaw));
      }
      return false;
    });

    // --- Process Loop ---
    for (const file of excelFilesToProcess) {
      const fileName = file.title;
      const baseNameRaw = fileName.replace(/\.xlsx$/i, '').replace(/\.xls$/i, '');
      const robustBaseName = normalizeGermanUmlauts(baseNameRaw);
      let tempFile = null;

      try {
        SpreadsheetApp.getActive().toast(`Converting: ${fileName}`);

        const destinationSheetFile = allFilesInFolder.find(item => 
          item.mimeType === MimeType.GOOGLE_SHEETS &&
          normalizeGermanUmlauts(item.title) === robustBaseName
        );

        // --- NEU: Konvertierung mit Retry-Logik und Blob-Methode ---
        let attempts = 0;
        while (attempts < 7) {
          try {
            attempts++;
            const fileBlob = DriveApp.getFileById(file.id).getBlob();
            const resource = {
              title: `temp_${new Date().getTime()}`,
              mimeType: MimeType.GOOGLE_SHEETS
            };
            
            tempFile = Drive.Files.insert(resource, fileBlob, { 
              supportsAllDrives: true,
              convert: true 
            });
            
            if (tempFile) break; // Erfolg! Schleife verlassen.
            
          } catch (err) {
            Logger.log(`Versuch ${attempts} fehlgeschlagen für ${fileName}: ${err.message}`);
            if (attempts >= 7) throw err; // Nach 7 Versuchen endgültig aufgeben
            Utilities.sleep(5000); // 5 Sekunden warten vor nächstem Versuch
          }
        }

        // --- AB HIER WIEDER DEIN ORIGINALER CODE FÜR DIE DATEN ---
        const tempSpreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(tempFile.id);
        const tempSourceSheet = tempSpreadsheet.getSheets()[0];
        
        // GET RAW VALUES (Retrieves the Date objects Google created)
        const rawValues = tempSourceSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); 

        // --- CRITICAL FIX: UN-MANGLE THE DATA ---
        // Map over the data and reverse Google's date logic
        const sanitizedData = rawValues.map(row => {
          return row.map(cell => {
            // Check if Google turned this cell into a Date object
            if (Object.prototype.toString.call(cell) === '[object Date]') {
              // Rebuild the YYYY-MM string! (e.g., May 1, 2026 -> "2026-05")
              const year = cell.getFullYear();
              const month = String(cell.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
              return `${year}-${month}`; 
            }
            // If it's empty, keep it empty. Otherwise, force to a string so it doesn't get re-evaluated
            return cell === '' ? '' : String(cell);
          });
        });

        if (!destinationSheetFile) {
          // --- CASE: CREATE NEW ---
          // Clear the temp sheet entirely
          tempSourceSheet.clear(); 
          const targetRange = tempSourceSheet.getRange(1, 1, sanitizedData.length, sanitizedData[0].length);
          
          // Lock to plaintext, then paste our sanitized data
          targetRange.setNumberFormat('@');
          targetRange.setValues(sanitizedData);
          
          const tempFileParents = Drive.Files.get(tempFile.id, { supportsAllDrives: true }).parents;
          const parentIdsToRemove = tempFileParents.map(p => p.id).join(',');

          Drive.Files.update({ title: baseNameRaw }, tempFile.id, null, {
            addParents: folderId,
            removeParents: parentIdsToRemove,
            supportsAllDrives: true
          });

          finalFileIds.set(robustBaseName, tempFile.id);
          tempFile = null; // Saved, don't trash
        
        } else {
          // --- CASE: OVERWRITE EXISTING ---
          const destSpreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(destinationSheetFile.id);
          const destSheet = destSpreadsheet.getSheets()[0];
          
          destSheet.clear(); 
          
          if(sanitizedData.length > 0 && sanitizedData[0].length > 0) {
            const targetRange = destSheet.getRange(1, 1, sanitizedData.length, sanitizedData[0].length);
            // Lock to plaintext, then paste our sanitized data
            targetRange.setNumberFormat('@'); 
            targetRange.setValues(sanitizedData);
          }
          finalFileIds.set(robustBaseName, destinationSheetFile.id);
        }
        processedCount++;
      } catch(e) {
        Logger.log(`Failed to process ${fileName}: ${e.message}`);
      } finally {
        if (tempFile) {
          // --- HIER IST DER LÖSCH-FIX VON VORHIN ---
          try { Drive.Files.trash(tempFile.id, { supportsAllDrives: true }); } catch (e) {}
        }
      }
    }

    // --- 4. Write IDs to Column E ---
    const outputIdsArray = fileNamesValues.map(row => {
      const name = row.toString().trim();
      let baseName = name;
      if (name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xlsx')) baseName = name.slice(0, -5);
      else if (name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xls')) baseName = name.slice(0, -4);
      return [ finalFileIds.get(normalizeGermanUmlauts(baseName)) || '' ];
    });
    sheet.getRange("E4:E17").setValues(outputIdsArray);
    
    SpreadsheetApp.getActive().toast(`${processedCount} files processed.`, "Complete", 5);

  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert('Error', `Details: ${e.message}`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  }
}

MIS_FINAL_LOCHEN.gs
/**
 * Clears data from the 'MIS Final' sheet.
 * This function replicates the functionality of the MISDatenLöschen VBA macro.
 */
function clearMisData() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("MIS Final");
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  // Check if the sheet exists
  if (!sheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Sheet "MIS Final" could not be found.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();

  // Check if there is data to clear (VBA checks if last row is < 6)
  if (lastRow < 6) {
    ui.alert('No Data Found', 'There is no data to delete in the "MIS Final" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  } else {
    // Define the range to be cleared (A6:G<lastRow>)
    const rangeToClear = sheet.getRange("A6:G" + lastRow);
    
    // Clear the contents of the range
    rangeToClear.clearContent();
    
    ui.alert('Success!', 'The data has been successfully deleted from the "MIS Final" sheet.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  }
}

PDF_Export_Core.gs

/**
 * --- CORE UTILITIES ---
 * Uses Robust Template Injection.
 */

function getExportFolderId() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const exportSheet = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");
  if (!exportSheet) throw new Error("Sheet 'EXPORT' not found.");

  const folderValue = exportSheet.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  if (!folderValue) throw new Error("Folder ID/URL missing in 'EXPORT!D4'.");

  const folderMatch = folderValue.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
  if (folderMatch && folderMatch[1]) return folderMatch[1];

  const idParamMatch = folderValue.match(/[?&]id=([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
  if (idParamMatch && idParamMatch[1]) return idParamMatch[1];

  const rawIdMatch = folderValue.match(/^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{20,}$/);
  if (rawIdMatch) return folderValue;

  throw new Error("EXPORT!D4 enthält keine gültige Google-Drive-Ordner-ID oder Ordner-URL.");
}

function fetchRawSheetData(sheetNames) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const rawTables = [];
  const uniqueNames = [...new Set(sheetNames)];

  uniqueNames.forEach(name => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (!sheet) return;

    const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
    const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
    if (lastRow < 1 || lastCol < 1) return;

    const dataRange = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol);
    
    // Fetch Column Widths
    const colWidths = [];
    let totalWidth = 0;
    for (let i = 1; i <= lastCol; i++) {
        const w = sheet.getColumnWidth(i);
        colWidths.push(w);
        totalWidth += w;
    }
    const widthPercents = colWidths.map(w => (w / totalWidth * 100) + '%');

    rawTables.push({
      sheetName: name,
      values: dataRange.getDisplayValues(),
      colors: dataRange.getBackgrounds(),
      fontColors: dataRange.getFontColors(),
      fontWeights: dataRange.getFontWeights(),
      colWidths: widthPercents
    });
  });

  return rawTables;
}

/**
 * BATCH CONTEXT FETCHER
 */
function getBatchContext(batchType, extraConfig) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let items = [];
  let sheetNames = [];
  
  // -- NEW: Deckblatt Logic --
  if (batchType === "DECKBLATT_BATCH") {
      // For Deckblatts, the "Items" are the sheet names themselves
      items = ["Deckblatt Gesamt", "Deckblatt Food", "Deckblatt O+G"];
      sheetNames = items;
  }
  // -- Existing Logic --
  else if (batchType === "GL_EK_INT_QUAL") {
      const mapSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Mapping");
      if (mapSheet.getLastRow() > 1) items = [...new Set(mapSheet.getRange(2, 10, mapSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getDisplayValues().flat().filter(String))];
      sheetNames = ["Food Qualitätsfälle"];
  } 
  else if (batchType === "GL_EK_INT_SORT") {
       const mapSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Mapping");
       if (mapSheet.getLastRow() > 1) items = [...new Set(mapSheet.getRange(2, 11, mapSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getDisplayValues().flat().filter(String))];
       sheetNames = ["Food Sortimentswünsche", "Änderungswünsche Sortierung", "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche"];
  }
  else if (batchType === "GL_EK_INT_SONST") {
      const mapSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Mapping");
      if (mapSheet.getLastRow() > 1) items = [...new Set(mapSheet.getRange(2, 10, mapSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getDisplayValues().flat().filter(String))];
      sheetNames = ["Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen"];
  }
  else if (batchType === "EKL_DE") {
      const mapSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Mapping");
      if (mapSheet.getLastRow() > 1) items = [...new Set(mapSheet.getRange(2, 11, mapSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getDisplayValues().flat().filter(String))];
      sheetNames = ["Food Sortimentswünsche", "Änderungswünsche Sortierung", "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen", "Food Qualitätsfälle"];
  }

  const rawData = fetchRawSheetData(sheetNames);
  const sheetConfigs = {};
  sheetNames.forEach(name => {
    sheetConfigs[name] = getWrapperParams(name);
  });

  if (batchType === "DECKBLATT_BATCH") {
    sheetConfigs["Deckblatt Gesamt"] = {
      printArea: "A5:N57",
      headerRows: 0,
      hideRows: extraConfig && extraConfig.hide53 ? [57] : []
    };
    sheetConfigs["Deckblatt Food"] = {
      printArea: "R4:U56",
      headerRows: 0,
      hideRows: extraConfig && extraConfig.hide53 ? [56] : []
    };
    sheetConfigs["Deckblatt O+G"] = {
      printArea: "R4:U56",
      headerRows: 0,
      hideRows: extraConfig && extraConfig.hide53 ? [56] : []
    };
  }

  return {
    items: items,
    rawData: rawData,
    sheetConfigs: sheetConfigs,
    targetFolderId: getExportFolderId(),
    batchType: batchType,
    extraConfig: extraConfig || {} // Pass things like '53 weeks' decision
  };
}

// --- LAUNCHERS ---

function launchSingleReport(config) {
  const sheetNames = config.sheets.map(s => s.name);
  const rawData = fetchRawSheetData(sheetNames);
  
  if (rawData.length === 0) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast("No data found.", "Warning");
    return;
  }

  config.rawTables = rawData;
  config.targetFolderId = getExportFolderId();
  config.centerHeader = config.centerHeader || config.header || "";
  config.centerFooter = config.centerFooter || config.footer || "";

  const template = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('Dialog');
  template.jsonPayload = JSON.stringify(config); 
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(template.evaluate().setWidth(600).setHeight(450), `Generating: ${config.pdfName}`);
}

function launchBatchRenderer(type, title, extraConfig) {
  // Fetch Context Server-Side immediately
  const context = getBatchContext(type, extraConfig);
  
  const template = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('DialogBatchRenderer');
  template.jsonPayload = JSON.stringify(context); 
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(template.evaluate().setWidth(600).setHeight(500), title);
}

function uploadPDFBlobToDrive(pdfBase64, pdfName, folderId) {
  try {
    const targetFolder = DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId);
    const base64 = String(pdfBase64).includes(',')
      ? String(pdfBase64).split(',').pop()
      : String(pdfBase64);
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(Utilities.base64Decode(base64), 'application/pdf', pdfName);
    targetFolder.createFile(blob);
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(`Saved: ${pdfName}`, "Success", 3);
    return "OK";
  } catch (e) {
    throw new Error(e.message);
  }
}

/**
 * UNIVERSAL JANITOR: Scans the entire workbook and deletes any orphaned "Temp_" sheets.
 * This acts as a foolproof safety net against aborted runs or skipped data.
 */
function cleanUpOrphanedTempSheets() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();
  
  for (let i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
    const sheetName = sheets[i].getName();
    // Case-insensitive check for any tab starting with "temp_"
    if (sheetName.toLowerCase().startsWith("temp_")) {
      try {
        if (ss.getSheets().length > 1) ss.deleteSheet(sheets[i]);
        console.log(`Gelöscht: ${sheetName}`);
      } catch (e) {
        console.error(`Konnte ${sheetName} nicht löschen: ${e.message}`);
      }
    }
  }
}

const PDF_WRAPPER_SIG = "Ersteller: Kundenservice Einkauf";

const PDF_WRAPPER_CONFIG = {
  "Food Sortimentswünsche": { header: `&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&11Mehrfach angeforderte Sortimentswünsche Food ${PDF_WRAPPER_YEAR}`, printArea: "A4:R" },
  "Änderungswünsche Sortierung": { header: `&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&11Änderungswünsche Sortierung Food ${PDF_WRAPPER_YEAR}`, printArea: "A4:R" },
  "Sonstiges Food u Akt. Themen": { header: `&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&14Sonstiges Food und aktuelle Themen ${PDF_WRAPPER_YEAR}`, printArea: "A5:O" },
  "Food Qualitätsfälle": { header: `&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&14Qualitätsreklamationen Food ${PDF_WRAPPER_YEAR}`, printArea: "A4:V" },
  "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche": { header: `&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&11Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche Food ${PDF_WRAPPER_YEAR}`, printArea: "A4:K" },
  "O+G Sortimentswünsche": { header: `&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&14Sortimentswünsche O+G ${PDF_WRAPPER_YEAR}`, printArea: "A5:K" },
  "O+G Sonstiges": { header: `&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&14Sonstiges O+G ${PDF_WRAPPER_YEAR}`, printArea: "A5:K" },
  "O+G Qualitätsfälle": { header: `&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&14Qualitätsreklamationen O+G / B+P ${PDF_WRAPPER_YEAR}`, printArea: "A4:O" },
  "O+G Qualitätsf. o. LFN": { header: `&C&B&""Lidl Font Pro""&14Qualitätsreklamationen O+G / B+P ${PDF_WRAPPER_YEAR} ${String.fromCharCode(10)}(nicht ermittelbare Lieferantendaten)`, printArea: "A4:O" }
};

function getWrapperFooter(kw) {
  return `&C&""Lidl Font Pro""&9Statistik KW ${kw} ${String.fromCharCode(10)}- &P &"";`;
}

function getWrapperParams(sheetName) {
    if (!PDF_WRAPPER_CONFIG[sheetName]) return { printArea: "", headerRows: 2 };
    return {
        printArea: PDF_WRAPPER_CONFIG[sheetName].printArea,
        headerRows: 2 
    };
}

Save Archive.gs


/**
 * This script creates a copy of the current Google Sheet in its parent folder
 * and stores the new copy's ID in the 'Einstellungen' sheet, cell E18.
 * This script requires Drive API access.
 */

/**
 * Main function to create a copy of the document, place it in the same folder,
 * and store the new file's ID in a specific cell.
 */
function createDocumentCopy() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheetName = 'Einstellungen'; // The name of the sheet to write the ID to
  var cellAddress = 'E18';         // The cell to write the ID to
  
  var ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  try {
    var fileId = ss.getId();
    var currentFile = DriveApp.getFileById(fileId);
    
    // Get parent folders
    var parents = currentFile.getParents();
    
    if (!parents.hasNext()) {
      // This should rarely happen, but it's good to check.
      ui.alert('Error: This file does not have a parent folder. Cannot determine where to save the copy.');
      return;
    }

    // Get current date, spreadsheet timezone, and format the date
    var now = new Date();
    var timezone = ss.getSpreadsheetTimeZone();
    var formattedDate = Utilities.formatDate(now, timezone, 'dd_MM_yyyy');

    // Get original file name
    var originalName = currentFile.getName();
    
    // Get the first parent folder. This works for both My Drive and Shared Drives.
    var parentFolder = parents.next();
    
    // Create the copy in the same folder
    var copyName = 'Archive_' + originalName + '_' + formattedDate;
    var newCopy = currentFile.makeCopy(copyName, parentFolder);
    var newCopyId = newCopy.getId();

    // Get the target sheet and cell
    var targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (!targetSheet) {
      ui.alert('Error: Sheet "' + sheetName + '" not found. \n\nThe copy was created (ID: ' + newCopyId + ') but the ID could not be stored.');
      return;
    }

    var targetCell = targetSheet.getRange(cellAddress); // Zelle E18 für die ID
    var urlCell = targetSheet.getRange('F18');          // NEU: Zelle F18 für die URL
    
    // --- NEU: URL der Kopie abfragen ---
    var newCopyUrl = newCopy.getUrl();
    
    // Store the new ID in the specified cell (E18)
    targetCell.setValue(newCopyId);
    
    // --- NEU: URL in Zelle F18 schreiben ---
    urlCell.setValue(newCopyUrl);
    
    SpreadsheetApp.getActive().toast('Success! \nCopy created with Name: ' + copyName + '\nID stored in E18, URL stored in F18.');

  } catch (e) {
    // Log the error for debugging and alert the user
    Logger.log(e);
    ui.alert('An error occurred: ' + e.message);
  }
}
/**
    // Get the target sheet and cell
    var targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (!targetSheet) {
      ui.alert('Error: Sheet "' + sheetName + '" not found. \n\nThe copy was created (ID: ' + newCopyId + ') but the ID could not be stored.');
      return;
    }

    var targetCell = targetSheet.getRange(cellAddress);
    
    // Store the new ID in the specified cell
    targetCell.setValue(newCopyId);
    
    SpreadsheetApp.getActive().toast('Success! \nCopy created with Name: ' + copyName + '\nStored in: ' + sheetName + '!' + cellAddress);

  } catch (e) {
    // Log the error for debugging and alert the user
    Logger.log(e);
    ui.alert('An error occurred: ' + e.message);
  }
}

/**
 * SERVER SIDE: ExportSortimentswünscheGLEKINT
 * Generates batch reports per recipient (GL-EK INT).
 * Uses Client-Side pdf-lib rendering to handle headers, footers, and merging.
 */

function openGLEKINTDialog() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");
  
  if (!sheetExport) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // Fetch Dashboard Texts once to save time
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
  } catch (e) {
    folderId = folderUrl; 
  }

  const allgSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche");
  const kwValue = allgSheet ? allgSheet.getRange("J7").getValue() : "XX";

  // Package layout data to send to frontend
  const layouts = {
    food: {
      htl: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche header left"), htc: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche header center"), htr: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche header right"),
      fbl: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche footer left"), fbc: "Statistik KW " + kwValue + "\n- [PAGE] -", fbr: getDashboardText("Food Sortimentswünsche footer right")
    },
    aenderung: {
      htl: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung header left"), htc: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung header center"), htr: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung header right"),
      fbl: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer left"), fbc: "Statistik KW " + kwValue + "\n- [PAGE] -", fbr: getDashboardText("Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer right")
    },
    allgemeine: {
      htl: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header left"), htc: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header center"), htr: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header right"),
      fbl: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer left"), fbc: "Statistik KW " + kwValue + "\n- [PAGE] -", fbr: getDashboardText("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer right")
    }
  };

  const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('ExportSortimentswünscheGLEKINT');
  htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
    layouts: layouts, 
    folderId: folderId,
    kwValue: kwValue
  });
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(
    htmlTemplate.evaluate().setWidth(600).setHeight(500), 
    'Generating GL-EK INT Reports...'
  );
}

/**
 * Gets unique recipients from Mapping Col J (Index 10) as per VBA Modul9
 */
function getGlekIntRecipients() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Mapping");
  if (!sheet) throw new Error("Sheet 'Mapping' not found");
  
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return [];
  
  const data = sheet.getRange(2, 10, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues().flat();
  return [...new Set(data)].filter(String).sort();
}

/**
 * Server-side generation of Base PDFs for a specific recipient
 */
function getPdfDataForRecipient(recipient) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  const configs = [
    { id: "food", name: "Food Sortimentswünsche", filterCol: 4, headerRows: 5, keepCols: 18 },
    { id: "aenderung", name: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung", filterCol: 4, headerRows: 5, keepCols: 18 },
    { id: "allgemeine", name: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche", filterCol: null, headerRows: 7, keepCols: 11 } // No filter
  ];

  const parts = [];

  for (const config of configs) {
    const liveSheet = ss.getSheetByName(config.name);
    if (!liveSheet) continue;

    const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
    const tempSheet = liveSheet.copyTo(ss);
    tempSheet.setName("Temp_" + config.id + "_" + uniqueSuffix);
    const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
    tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

    try {
      const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
      if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

      const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
      if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

      // Filtering Logic
      let hasData = true;
      const lastRow = tempSheet.getLastRow();

      if (config.filterCol && lastRow > config.headerRows) {
        const values = tempSheet.getRange(config.headerRows + 1, config.filterCol, lastRow - config.headerRows, 1).getValues().flat();
        const deleteRequests = [];
        let startDelete = -1;
        let dataCount = 0;

        for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
          if (values[i] !== recipient) {
            if (startDelete === -1) startDelete = i;
          } else {
            if (startDelete !== -1) {
              deleteRequests.push({ deleteDimension: { range: { sheetId: sheetId, dimension: "ROWS", startIndex: config.headerRows + startDelete, endIndex: config.headerRows + i } } });
              startDelete = -1;
            }
            dataCount++;
          }
        }
        if (startDelete !== -1) {
          deleteRequests.push({ deleteDimension: { range: { sheetId: sheetId, dimension: "ROWS", startIndex: config.headerRows + startDelete, endIndex: config.headerRows + values.length } } });
        }
        if (deleteRequests.length > 0) {
          deleteRequests.reverse();
          Sheets.Spreadsheets.batchUpdate({ requests: deleteRequests }, ss.getId());
        }
        
        if (dataCount === 0) hasData = false;
      }

      SpreadsheetApp.flush();

      // Only fetch the URL if there's actually data to print (Allgemeine always prints)
      if (hasData) {
        const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
          `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}&size=A4&portrait=false&fitw=true&gridlines=false` +
          `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
          `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

        const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token }, muteHttpExceptions: true });
        
        if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
          parts.push({
            id: config.id,
            base64: Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes())
          });
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    }
  }

  return { parts: parts, tempSheets: tempSheetIds };
}

function saveMergedPdfToDrive_batch(base64Data, filename, folderId, tempSheets) {
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId);
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  if (base64Data) {
    const decodedBytes = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(decodedBytes, 'application/pdf', filename);
    folder.createFile(blob);
  }

  for (const ts of tempSheets) {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
    if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
  }

  return true;
}

/**
 * 🖨️ EXPORT SORTIMENTSWÜNSCHE GESAMT (Merged PDF)
 * Creates a single, merged landscape PDF from up to 3 sheets.
 * Dynamically skips sheets that contain no data.
 */

function export_sortimentswuensche_gesamt() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const sheetExport = ss.getSheetByName("EXPORT");

  if (!sheetExport) {
    ui.alert("Fehler", "Tabellenblatt 'EXPORT' nicht gefunden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 1. RESOLVE FOLDER ---
  const folderUrl = sheetExport.getRange("D4").getValue().toString().trim();
  let folderId = null;
  try {
    const match = folderUrl.match(/\/folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    folderId = match ? match[1] : folderUrl;
    DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId); 
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert("Ordner Fehler", "Der Zielordner konnte nicht gefunden werden.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // Get KW explicitly from Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche as per VBA logic
  const allgSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche");
  const kwValue = allgSheet ? allgSheet.getRange("J7").getValue() : "XX";

  ss.toast("Prüfe Tabellenblätter... Bitte warten.", "Schritt 1/3", 10);

  // --- 2. FETCH DASHBOARD DATA (B31:D144) ---
  const dashboardData = sheetExport.getRange("B31:D144").getValues();
  function getDashboardText(key) {
    const row = dashboardData.find(r => r[0] === key);
    return row && row[2] ? row[2].toString().trim() : "";
  }

  // --- 3. CONFIGURATIONS ---
  const configs = [
    {
      name: "Food Sortimentswünsche",
      dataRowStart: 6, // Rows below 5 are data
      keepCols: 18,    // Keep A-R
      keys: {
        htl: "Food Sortimentswünsche header left", htc: "Food Sortimentswünsche header center", htr: "Food Sortimentswünsche header right",
        fbl: "Food Sortimentswünsche footer left", fbc: "Food Sortimentswünsche footer center", fbr: "Food Sortimentswünsche footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung",
      dataRowStart: 6, // Rows below 5 are data
      keepCols: 18,    // Keep A-R
      keys: {
        htl: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung header left", htc: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung header center", htr: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung header right",
        fbl: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer left", fbc: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer center", fbr: "Änderungswünsche Sortierung footer right"
      }
    },
    {
      name: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche",
      dataRowStart: 8, // Rows below 7 are data
      keepCols: 11,    // Keep A-K
      keys: {
        htl: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header left", htc: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header center", htr: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche header right",
        fbl: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer left", fbc: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer center", fbr: "Allgemeine Sortimentswünsche footer right"
      }
    }
  ];

  const token = ScriptApp.getOAuthToken();
  const pdfParts = [];
  const tempSheetIds = [];

  // --- 4. PREPARE BASE PDFs (Only for sheets with data) ---
  for (const config of configs) {
    const liveSheet = ss.getSheetByName(config.name);
    if (!liveSheet) continue;

    // Check if sheet actually has data (mimicking VBA's check)
    const lastRow = liveSheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < config.dataRowStart) {
      console.log(`Skipping ${config.name} - No Data`);
      continue; 
    }

    // Clone & Trim
    const uniqueSuffix = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
    const tempSheet = liveSheet.copyTo(ss);
    tempSheet.setName("Temp_Merge_" + uniqueSuffix);
    const sheetId = tempSheet.getSheetId();
    tempSheetIds.push({ id: sheetId, name: tempSheet.getName() });

    try {
      // Clear UI elements
      const drawings = tempSheet.getDrawings();
      if (drawings) drawings.forEach(d => d.remove());

      // Trim extra columns
      const maxCols = tempSheet.getMaxColumns();
      if (maxCols > config.keepCols) tempSheet.deleteColumns(config.keepCols + 1, maxCols - config.keepCols);

      SpreadsheetApp.flush(); 
      Utilities.sleep(1500); 

      // Fetch Base PDF (LANDSCAPE mode via portrait=false)
      const url = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${ss.getId()}/export?` +
        `format=pdf&gid=${sheetId}` +
        `&size=A4&portrait=false&fitw=true&gridlines=false` +
        `&printtitle=false&sheetnames=false&pagenum=UNDEFINED` +
        `&horizontal_alignment=CENTER` + 
        `&top_margin=0.787&bottom_margin=0.709&left_margin=0.4&right_margin=0.4`;

      const responseAPI = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
        headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      });

      if (responseAPI.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        const base64Pdf = Utilities.base64Encode(responseAPI.getBlob().getBytes());
        
        pdfParts.push({
          sheetName: config.name,
          base64: base64Pdf,
          layout: {
            htl: getDashboardText(config.keys.htl),
            htc: getDashboardText(config.keys.htc),
            htr: getDashboardText(config.keys.htr),
            fbl: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbl),
            fbc: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbc),
            fbr: getDashboardText(config.keys.fbr)
          }
        });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    }
  }

  // --- 5. OPEN HTML FRONTEND ---
  if (pdfParts.length > 0) {
    const finalFilename = `02_Statistik_Food_Sortimentswünsche_KW${kwValue}_DE.pdf`;
    
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('multi-page-support-pdf-lib');
    htmlTemplate.payload = JSON.stringify({ 
      parts: pdfParts, 
      folderId: folderId, 
      filename: finalFilename,
      tempSheets: tempSheetIds 
    });
    
    const htmlOutput = htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setWidth(500)
      .setHeight(300)
      .setTitle('Merge & PDF Renderer');
      
    ui.showModalDialog(htmlOutput, 'Generiere zusammengeführtes PDF...');
  } else {
    ui.alert("Hinweis", "Keine der ausgewählten Tabellen enthält Daten.", ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    // Cleanup any empty temp sheets just in case
    for (const ts of tempSheetIds) {
      const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
      if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
    }
  }
}

/**
 * BACKEND CALLBACK: Saves the single merged PDF and cleans up.
 */
function saveMergedPdfToDrive_new(base64Data, filename, folderId, tempSheets) {
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(folderId);
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  // Save single PDF
  const decodedBytes = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
  const blob = Utilities.newBlob(decodedBytes, 'application/pdf', filename);
  folder.createFile(blob);

  // Clean up Temp Sheets
  for (const ts of tempSheets) {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(ts.name);
    if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
  }

  cleanUpOrphanedTempSheets();

  return true;
}


UPDATE_DECKBLATT_FOOD_FORMULAS.gs
/**
 * 🔄 Dynamically Updates Formulas on the 'Deckblatt Food' Sheet.
 * This version correctly creates formulas that REFERENCE the cell containing the URL
 * in the 'Einstellungen' sheet, rather than embedding the URL string itself.
 * This is run from the runMisImportSmarter() function on the IMPORT_MIS_DATEN code page.
 */
function updateDeckblattFoodFormulas() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const settingsSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Einstellungen");
  const deckblattSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Deckblatt Food");
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  // --- 1. Validate that the necessary sheets exist ---
  if (!settingsSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Sheet "Einstellungen" could not be found. The script cannot continue.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }
  if (!deckblattSheet) {
    ui.alert('Error', 'Sheet "Deckblatt Food" could not be found. The script cannot continue.', ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    return;
  }

  // --- 2. Find the correct row number ---
  const settingsValues = settingsSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const searchText = "Deckblatt Food";
  let foundRowNumber = -1; // Use -1 to indicate "not found"

  // Loop through all rows to find thesearchText
  for (let i = 0; i < settingsValues.length; i++) {
    // Check if any cell in the current row contains the search text
    if (settingsValues[i].some(cell => cell.toString().includes(searchText))) {
      foundRowNumber = i + 1; // Get the actual sheet row number (1-based)
      break; // Stop searching once the first match is found
    }
  }

  // --- 3. Proceed only if the row was found ---
  if (foundRowNumber > -1) {
    try {
      // --- 4. Construct the cell reference and new formulas ---
      const sheetName = "X8_weeks_Report_Deckblatt_DE";
      // This creates the dynamic, absolute reference string, e.g., "Einstellungen!$F$7"
      const urlCellReference = `Einstellungen!$F$${foundRowNumber}`;
      
      const newFormulaM4 = `=IF(AND(J4<ISOWEEKNUM(TODAY()-56);YEAR(TODAY()-56)=YEAR(TODAY()));R4;XLOOKUP(L4;IMPORTRANGE(${urlCellReference};"'${sheetName}'!A:A");IMPORTRANGE(${urlCellReference};"'${sheetName}'!B:B");"";0;1))`;
      const newFormulaN4 = `=IF(AND(J4<ISOWEEKNUM(TODAY()-56);YEAR(TODAY()-56)=YEAR(TODAY()));S4;XLOOKUP(L4;IMPORTRANGE(${urlCellReference};"'${sheetName}'!A:A");IMPORTRANGE(${urlCellReference};"'${sheetName}'!C:C");"";0;1))`;
      const newFormulaO4 = `=IF(AND(J4<ISOWEEKNUM(TODAY()-56);YEAR(TODAY()-56)=YEAR(TODAY()));T4;XLOOKUP(L4;IMPORTRANGE(${urlCellReference};"'${sheetName}'!A:A");IMPORTRANGE(${urlCellReference};"'${sheetName}'!D:D");"";0;1))`;

      // --- 5. Apply formulas to the top row AND auto-fill down to row 57 ---
      deckblattSheet.getRange("M4").setFormula(newFormulaM4);
      deckblattSheet.getRange("N4").setFormula(newFormulaN4);
      deckblattSheet.getRange("O4").setFormula(newFormulaO4);

      const sourceRange = deckblattSheet.getRange("M4:O4");
      const destinationRange = deckblattSheet.getRange("M4:O57");
      
      sourceRange.autoFill(destinationRange, SpreadsheetApp.AutoFillSeries.DEFAULT_SERIES);
      
      //ui.alert('Success!', `The formulas in M4:O57 on "Deckblatt Food" have been updated to reference cell ${urlCellReference}.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
      SpreadsheetApp.getActive().toast(`The formulas in M4:O57 on "Deckblatt Food" have been updated to reference cell ${urlCellReference}.`);

    } catch (e) {
      ui.alert('Formula Error', `Could not update the formulas. Error: ${e.message}`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    }
  } else {
    // Show an error if the specific row wasn't found
    ui.alert('Configuration Error', `Could not find a row containing "${searchText}" in the "Einstellungen" sheet. Please check the sheet configuration.`, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
  }
}
